### [1] [Wormhole Dynamics: Nonlinear Collapse and Gravitational-Wave Emission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00071)
*Nikita M. Shirokov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Numerical relativity simulations of the unstable Ellis-Bronnikov wormhole using GRTeclyn reveal a rarefactive instability leading to rapid throat expansion; controlled collapse is achieved via reduced phantom support and quadrupolar perturbation, resulting in horizon formation, gravitational wave emission, and a 'phantom bounce' curvature shock. The generated signal for a $10^3\,M_\odot$ wormhole at 1 Mpc is near but below Advanced LIGO sensitivity.

采用GRTeclyn进行的Ellis-Bronnikov虫洞数值相对论模拟揭示了导致喉部快速膨胀的稀疏不稳定性；通过降低幻象场支撑并引入四极扰动实现可控坍缩，最终形成视界、引力波辐射以及“幻象反弹”曲率激波。对于1 Mpc处质量为$10^3\,M_\odot$的虫洞，其信号略低于Advanced LIGO设计灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To study the dynamical instability and nonlinear evolution of the Ellis-Bronnikov wormhole under realistic numerical conditions, particularly exploring how truncation noise, reduced phantom support, and asymmetric perturbations influence its fate—either expansion or collapse—and whether observable gravitational-wave signatures can be produced.

研究Ellis-Bronnikov虫洞在真实数值条件下的动力学不稳定性与非线性演化，特别是截断误差、幻象场支撑减弱及非对称扰动如何影响其演化结局（膨胀或坍缩），并探索是否会产生可观测的引力波信号。

Method: 3D numerical-relativity simulations using GRTeclyn for the coupled Einstein-phantom-scalar system, starting from exact isotropic initial data. Simulations employ a flat initial lapse ($\alpha=1$), full or partial phantom stress-energy support ($S_{\text{support}} = 1$ or $0.5$), and include a quadrupolar scalar-field perturbation ($A_\phi=+0.02$, $\sigma_\phi=0.5$) to break spherical symmetry. Evolutions are performed with high-resolution finite-differencing and adaptive mesh refinement.

使用GRTeclyn对爱因斯坦-幻象标量耦合系统进行三维数值相对论模拟，基于精确各向同性初始数据，采用平坦初值叶函数（$\alpha=1$），完全或部分幻象能-动张量支撑（$S_{\text{support}} = 1$ 或 $0.5$），并加入四极标量场扰动（$A_\phi=+0.02$, $\sigma_\phi=0.5$）以打破球对称性。模拟采用高分辨率有限差分法与自适应网格加密技术。

Result: Truncation-level numerical noise triggers the known rarefactive instability, causing uncontrolled throat expansion in fully supported cases. With reduced phantom support ($S_{\text{support}}=0.5$) and quadrupolar perturbation, a clean compressive collapse occurs: a trapped surface forms, emitting an outward-propagating gravitational-wave burst traveling at approximately light speed ($v \approx c$), distinct from superluminal constraint-violating modes in CCZ4. Post-horizon formation, the infalling phantom matter induces a violent 'phantom bounce', launching a sharp outward-going curvature shock. The peak strain for a $10^3\,M_\odot$ wormhole at $D=1\,\text{Mpc}$ is estimated as $h \sim 10^{-22}$, slightly below Advanced LIGO's design sensitivity.

截断级数噪声触发已知的稀疏型不稳定性，导致完全支撑情况下的喉部无控扩张。当幻象支撑降至$S_{\text{support}}=0.5$并加入四极扰动时，发生清晰的压缩性坍缩：形成陷获面，并发射以近光速传播的引力波脉冲（$v \approx c$），区别于CCZ4中超光速的约束违反模式。视界形成后，下落的幻象物质引发剧烈的“幻象反弹”，产生向外传播的尖锐曲率激波。对于D=1 Mpc处的$10^3\,M_\odot$虫洞，峰值应变约为$h \sim 10^{-22}$，略低于Advanced LIGO设计灵敏度。

Conclusion: The Ellis-Bronnikov wormhole is dynamically unstable under generic conditions, with its evolution highly sensitive to initial support and perturbations. Controlled collapse can produce observable features such as prompt gravitational-wave bursts and post-merger curvature shocks, although current detectors may lack sensitivity for typical sources. The 'phantom bounce' represents a novel strong-field general-relativistic effect enabled by phantom fields violating energy conditions.

Ellis-Bronnikov虫洞在一般条件下动力学不稳定，其演化对初始支撑与扰动极为敏感。受控坍缩可产生如瞬时引力波爆发和并后曲率激波等可观测特征，但当前探测器对典型源可能缺乏足够灵敏度。‘幻象反弹’是幻象场违反能量条件所允许的一种新型强场广义相对论效应。

Abstract: We present 3D numerical-relativity evolutions of the unstable Ellis-Bronnikov wormhole using GRTeclyn, starting from exact isotropic initial data for the coupled Einstein-phantom-scalar system. With a flat initial lapse (alpha=1) and full phantom support, truncation-level noise eventually drives the rarefactive instability and rapid throat expansion. To force a clean collapse while breaking spherical symmetry, we reduce the phantom stress-energy support to S_support=0.5 and add a quadrupolar scalar-field perturbation (A_phi=+0.02, sigma_phi=0.5). The resulting compressive evolution forms a trapped surface and emits a gravitational-wave signal whose peak propagates between extraction radii at v approx c, distinct from superluminal CCZ4 constraint modes. After horizon formation the swallowed phantom matter triggers a violent rebound ("phantom bounce") that launches an outward curvature shock. For the moderate perturbation amplitude simulated here, an intermediate-mass (10^3 solar mass) wormhole at D=1 Mpc falls slightly below the Advanced LIGO design sensitivity; detection requires either closer sources, larger initial asymmetries, or next-generation detectors.

</details>


### [2] [Big Bang revisited](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00077)
*Frans R. Klinkhamer*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper discusses the elimination of the Big Bang curvature singularity using a degenerate spacetime metric, with implications for CPT-conjugated worlds and an extended Einstein field equation.

本文讨论了通过使用退化时空度规消除大爆炸曲率奇点的可能性，并探讨其对CPT共轭宇宙及扩展爱因斯坦场方程的潜在意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Friedmann solution of general relativity predicts a curvature singularity at the Big Bang, which signals a breakdown of physical laws. The motivation is to resolve this singularity by modifying the spacetime structure, particularly through a degenerate metric that may allow well-defined physics at early times.

广义相对论的弗里德曼解在大爆炸时刻预言了一个曲率奇点，标志着物理定律的失效。本文的动机是通过修改时空结构——特别是使用退化度规——来消除这一奇点，从而在早期宇宙实现良好的物理描述。

Method: The authors propose using a degenerate spacetime metric, where the determinant of the metric tensor $g$ vanishes ($\det g = 0$), leading to a breakdown of standard Riemannian geometry but potentially allowing nonsingular cosmological evolution. They analyze the consequences for spacetime topology and symmetry, including the emergence of CPT-conjugated worlds, and consider an extended form of Einstein's gravitational field equations compatible with such degeneracy.

作者提出使用退化时空度规，即度规张量行列式为零（$\det g = 0$），这会破坏标准黎曼几何，但可能允许无奇点的宇宙演化。他们分析了这种设定对时空拓扑和对称性的影响，包括CPT共轭宇宙的出现，并考虑了与这种退化相容的扩展爱因斯坦场方程。

Result: A degenerate metric can eliminate the Big Bang singularity by preventing infinite curvature. The framework suggests the possibility of CPT-symmetric universe pairs—potentially representing pre- and post-Big Bang phases—and requires modifications to the standard Einstein equations to maintain consistency in the singular limit.

退化度规可通过避免无限曲率来消除大爆炸奇点。该框架暗示了CPT对称宇宙对的可能性——可能代表大爆炸前后两个相位——并要求修改标准爱因斯坦方程以在奇异极限下保持一致性。

Conclusion: The use of a degenerate spacetime metric offers a promising route to resolving the initial singularity in cosmology. It opens up new theoretical possibilities, including CPT-conjugated worlds and modified gravitational dynamics, warranting further investigation within quantum gravity and early-universe models.

使用退化时空度规为解决宇宙学初始奇点提供了有前景的路径。它开启了新的理论可能性，包括CPT共轭宇宙和修正的引力动力学，值得在量子引力和早期宇宙模型中进一步研究。

Abstract: The Friedmann cosmological solution of the standard Einstein gravitational field equation has a curvature singularity at a moment in time known as the Big Bang. It has been suggested that this Big Bang curvature singularity can be eliminated by use of a degenerate spacetime metric. This proposal was the main topic of our talk at the Workshop, but, here, we also discuss the possible appearance of CPT-conjugated worlds and the conjectured relevance of an extended version of Einstein's field equation.

</details>


### [3] [Regular Black Strings and BTZ Black Hole in Unimodular Gravity Supported by Maxwell Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00078)
*G. Alencar V. H. U. Borralho*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We derive a Maxwell source for regular black string and BTZ black hole solutions in unimodular gravity, where the cosmological constant emerges as a spacetime-dependent integration constant $\Lambda(r)$ due to non-conservation of the energy-momentum tensor, and verify consistency with Maxwell electrodynamics.

我们通过非守恒的能量-动量张量在单模引力中导出了正则黑洞弦和BTZ黑洞的麦克斯韦源，其中宇宙学常数作为时空依赖的积分常数$\Lambda(r)$出现，并验证了其与麦克斯韦电动力学的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Unimodular gravity offers an alternative framework to general relativity with restricted diffeomorphism invariance, where the cosmological constant arises dynamically as an integration constant rather than being inserted by hand. This motivates exploring exact solutions such as black strings and BTZ black holes with physical matter sources like Maxwell fields, while investigating how vacuum contributions vary in space.

单模引力提供了一个替代广义相对论的框架，其微分同胚不变性受限，宇宙学常数动态地作为积分常数出现而非人为引入。这促使我们探索带有麦克斯韦场等物理物质源的精确解（如黑洞弦和BTZ黑洞），并研究真空贡献如何随空间变化。

Method: We work within the framework of unimodular gravity, imposing $\det(g_{\mu\nu}) = g_0$ to restrict to volume-preserving diffeomorphisms. The modified Einstein equations are derived from variation under this constraint. By allowing the energy-momentum tensor to be non-conserved, the usual cosmological constant becomes a function $\Lambda(x)$. We assume a static, cylindrically symmetric metric for black strings and a (2+1)-dimensional ansatz for BTZ, then solve the field equations to determine the geometric function $H(r)$ and identify the Maxwell source. The resulting $\Lambda(r)$ is computed from the trace of the field equations.

我们在单模引力框架下工作，施加$\det(g_{\mu\nu}) = g_0$以限制为体积保持微分同胚。通过在此约束下的变分推导修正的爱因斯坦方程。允许能量-动量张量非守恒，使通常的宇宙学常数变为函数$\Lambda(x)$。假设黑洞弦具有静态柱对称度规，BTZ采用(2+1)维试探解，求解场方程以确定几何函数$H(r)$并识别麦克斯韦源。由场方程的迹计算得到$\Lambda(r)$。

Result: We find that Maxwell electrodynamics consistently serves as a source for both regular black string and BTZ black hole solutions in unimodular gravity. The geometric function $H(r)$ matches the expected form for these solutions, confirming compatibility with standard electromagnetic theory. Crucially, the integration constant associated with the cosmological term becomes a radial function $\Lambda(r)$, interpreted as a coordinate-dependent vacuum energy contribution arising from the breakdown of full diffeomorphism invariance. Explicit expressions for $\Lambda(r)$ are derived in both cases.

我们发现麦克斯韦电动力学可一致地作为单模引力中正则黑洞弦和BTZ黑洞解的源。几何函数$H(r)$符合这些解的预期形式，证实了与标准电磁理论的兼容性。关键的是，与宇宙学项相关的积分常数成为径向函数$\Lambda(r)$，解释为由于完整微分同胚不变性破缺而产生的坐标依赖真空能贡献。在这两种情况下均导出了$\Lambda(r)$的显式表达式。

Conclusion: Our results demonstrate that unimodular gravity allows for physically meaningful black hole and black string solutions sourced by standard Maxwell fields. The emergent spacetime-dependent cosmological 'constant' $\Lambda(r)$ provides a novel mechanism for vacuum energy localization, suggesting that breaking full diffeomorphism invariance can lead to nontrivial background dynamics even in classical gravity.

我们的结果表明，单模引力允许由标准麦克斯韦场驱动的、具有物理意义的黑洞和黑洞弦解。涌现的时空依赖宇宙学“常数”$\Lambda(r)$为真空能局域化提供了新机制，表明即使在经典引力中，破缺完整的微分同胚不变性也可导致非平凡的背景动力学。

Abstract: In this work, we obtain a Maxwell source for regular black string and BTZ black hole using the framework of unimodular gravity. This type of alternative to general relativity imposes an additional condition on the spacetime volume element, namely that it is constant, $\det(g_{μν}) = g_0$, and thus restricts diffeomorphism invariance to volume-preserving transformations. In this procedure, the cosmological constant does not appear directly in the action, but rather as an integration constant of the field equations. By using the non-conservation of the energy-momentum tensor, we show that the integration constant becomes a function $Λ(x)$, which is interpreted as a vacuum contribution depending on the radial coordinate, in our case. From the definition of the geometric function $H(r)$, we verify the validity of Maxwell electrodynamics as a source for the solutions and compute the vacuum contribution $Λ(r)$ that supports the solutions.

</details>


### [4] [Distinguishing Black Holes and Neutron Stars via Optical Imaging Illuminated by Thick Accretion Disks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00117)
*Chen-Yu Yang,Xiao-Xiong Zeng*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies neutron star optical images using the radiatively inefficient accretion flow model with a polytropic equation of state, solving geodesic and radiative transfer equations to analyze image morphology dependence on polytropic index $N$ and observer inclination $\theta_o$, and compares results with Schwarzschild black hole shadows.

本文在辐射低效吸积流模型下研究中子星的光学图像，采用多方状态方程，通过数值求解测地线方程和辐射转移方程，分析图像形态对多方指数$N$和观测者倾角$\theta_o$的依赖性，并与史瓦西黑洞阴影进行比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the optical appearance of neutron stars in strong gravity and distinguish them from black holes via high-resolution imaging by exploring how key parameters shape their observable images.

为了通过高分辨率成像区分中子星与黑洞，理解强引力场下中子星的光学外观，并探索关键参数如何影响其可观测图像。

Method: Numerically solved the structure of neutron stars assuming a polytropic equation of state, then computed null geodesics and integrated the radiative transfer equation in curved spacetime to generate synthetic images; analyzed variations in image morphology with respect to $N$ and $\theta_o$, and compared with Schwarzschild black hole shadow under identical conditions.

假设多方状态方程，数值求解中子星结构；随后在弯曲时空中计算零测地线并积分辐射转移方程以生成合成图像；分析图像形态随$N$和$\theta_o$的变化，并在相同条件下与史瓦西黑洞阴影进行比较。

Result: For neutron stars, a bright higher-order image surrounds a dark central region when photons are absorbed at the surface. Increasing $N$ enlarges the higher-order image; increasing $\theta_o$ enhances obscuration due to off-equatorial emission. Compared to a Schwarzschild black hole, the neutron star's higher-order image is larger and the dark region more extended, while the black hole's higher-order image is sharper and more distinct.

对于中子星，当光子在其表面被吸收时，明亮的高阶图像环绕着中心暗区。随着$N$增大，高阶图像逐渐扩大；随着$\theta_o$增大，非赤道面辐射导致的遮蔽效应更显著。与史瓦西黑洞相比，中子星的高阶图像更大，暗区更延展，而黑洞的高阶图像更清晰、更易分辨。

Conclusion: Significant differences exist in the optical images of neutron stars and black holes within this model, particularly in the size and clarity of higher-order structures and the extent of the dark central region, providing a theoretical foundation for distinguishing compact objects via next-generation very-long-baseline interferometry (VLBI) observations.

在此模型下，中子星与黑洞的光学图像存在显著差异，特别是在高阶结构的大小与清晰度以及中心暗区的延展程度方面，为通过下一代甚长基线干涉测量（VLBI）观测区分致密天体提供了理论基础。

Abstract: This paper investigates the optical images of neutron stars within the framework of the radiatively inefficient accretion flow model, taking into account a polytropic equation of state. After obtaining the numerical solutions of the neutron star, we solved numerically the geodesic equations together with the radiative transfer equation. We mainly examine the effects of the polytropic index $N$ and the observer inclination angle $θ_o$ on the image morphology. The obtained images are also compared with the shadow of a Schwarzschild black hole. It is shown that, under the assumption that photon trajectories are terminated at the neutron star surface, the image exhibits a bright higher order structure surrounding an inner dark region. As $N$ increases, the size of the higher-order image gradually expands. As $θ_o$ increases, the obscuration of the neutron star silhouette by radiation originating outside the equatorial plane becomes more pronounced. Compared with the black hole shadow obtained under the same parameter configuration, the neutron star exhibits a larger higher order image and a more extended obscured inner dark region, whereas the higher order image of the black hole is more readily distinguishable. These results indicate significant differences in the optical appearance of neutron stars and black holes, and thus provide a theoretical basis for distinguishing between them through high resolution imaging.

</details>


### [5] [Does a wormhole survive a cosmological bounce?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00134)
*Daniela Pérez,Gustavo E. Romero,Santiago E. Perez Bergliaffa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates the survival of dynamical wormholes through a cosmological bounce, showing that for the Kim and Pérez-Romero Neto solutions, wormholes can persist throughout the contracting, bouncing, and expanding phases without topology change.

本文研究了动态虫洞在宇宙学反弹中能否存活，表明对于Kim和Pérez-Romero Neto解，虫洞可以在收缩、反弹和膨胀阶段持续存在而不会发生拓扑变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To determine whether wormhole geometries can survive a cosmological bounce without undergoing topology change, which challenges assumptions about spacetime continuity in quantum gravity and early universe cosmology.

为了确定虫洞几何是否能在宇宙学反弹中存活而不发生拓扑变化，这对量子引力和早期宇宙学中的时空连续性假设提出了挑战。

Method: Analyzed two known exact solutions of Einstein's equations describing cosmological wormholes — the Kim solution and the Pérez-Raia Neto solution — within the context of a bouncing universe. Studied their global structure, causal diagrams, energy conditions, and behavior across the bounce using general relativity and differential geometry.

在反弹宇宙背景下分析了两个已知的描述宇宙学虫洞的爱因斯坦方程精确解——Kim解和Pérez-Romero Neto解。利用广义相对论和微分几何研究了它们的整体结构、因果图、能量条件以及在反弹期间的行为。

Result: Both the Kim and Pérez-Romero Neto wormhole solutions exist for all cosmic times, including the bounce point, with no discontinuity or topology change. The causal structure remains well-defined, and the matter content satisfies certain energy conditions only in limited regions, indicating possible violation of classical energy conditions near the throat.

Kim和Pérez-Romero Neto虫洞解在所有宇宙时（包括反弹点）均存在，且无间断或拓扑变化。因果结构保持良好定义，物质内容仅在有限区域满足能量条件，表明喉部附近可能违反经典能量条件。

Conclusion: Dynamical wormholes can in principle survive a cosmological bounce without changing topology, suggesting that such structures could persist from pre-bounce to post-bounce phases. This supports the idea that exotic spacetime topologies may be compatible with non-singular cosmological models.

动态虫洞原则上可以在不改变拓扑的情况下经历宇宙学反弹，表明此类结构可以从反弹前相延续到反弹后相。这支持了奇异时空拓扑可能与非奇异宇宙学模型兼容的观点。

Abstract: We investigate whether a dynamical wormhole could survive in a universe that undergoes a cosmological bounce. First, the conditions under which a wormhole could persist from a contracting to an expanding phase of the cosmos are presented. Then, the only two known cosmological solutions of Einstein's equations representing wormholes are analyzed, and it is shown that both dynamical wormholes exist for all cosmic times on both sides of a bouncing universe and at the bounce itself. We also provide a detailed analysis of the causal structure of such spacetimes and the matter content of the wormhole. Finally, some possible astrophysical manifestations of surviving wormholes in a bouncing universe are mentioned. Our results show that, at least for the Kim and Pérez-Raia Neto solutions, there is no topology change in the chosen cosmological model with a bounce.

</details>


### [6] [Thermodynamics of dynamical black holes beyond perturbation theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00170)
*Abhay Ashtekar,Daniel E. Paraizo,Jonathan Shu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper revisits black hole thermodynamics by replacing event horizons with quasi-local horizons to overcome the teleological limitations of traditional formulations. It establishes a new first law applicable to finite, physical processes on black holes far from equilibrium and provides a quantitative second law linking area changes to energy fluxes, leading to the identification of entropy with the area of marginally trapped surfaces.

本文通过用准局域视界替代事件视界，重新审视黑洞热力学，以克服传统表述中事件视界因果性带来的局限。新提出的热力学第一定律适用于远离平衡态黑洞在物理过程中发生的有限变化，第二定律则定量地将面积变化与落入黑洞的能量通量联系起来，从而将熵识别为位于准局域视界内边缘陷获面的面积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The standard laws of black hole mechanics, based on event horizons, suffer from teleological issues—event horizons depend on future evolution, making them unsuitable for describing real-time physical processes. This motivates the use of quasi-local horizons, such as dynamical and trapping horizons, which are defined locally in time and better suited for describing evolving black holes.

基于事件视界的黑洞力学定律存在因果性（teleological）问题——事件视界依赖于未来的时空演化，因此不适合描述实时物理过程。这促使研究者采用如动态视界和捕获视界等准局域视界，它们在时间上局域定义，更适用于描述演化的黑洞。

Method: The authors employ the framework of quasi-local horizons, particularly dynamical horizons, within general relativity. They derive a first law for finite transformations by integrating balance laws over spacetime regions bounded by marginally trapped surfaces. The second law is established by relating the change in horizon area to the ingoing energy-momentum flux using the Raychaudhuri equation and geometric identities.

作者采用广义相对论中的准局域视界框架，特别是动态视界（dynamical horizons），通过在由边缘陷获面界定的时空区域上积分守恒律，推导出适用于有限变换的第一定律。第二定律则通过Raychaudhuri方程和几何恒等式，将视界面积的变化与入射能量-动量通量关联而建立。

Result: A new first law of black hole mechanics is derived that applies to finite, non-perturbative changes due to physical processes at the horizon, without requiring stationarity or equilibrium. A quantitative second law is obtained, showing that the area increase of a dynamical horizon segment is directly proportional to the flux of energy crossing it. Entropy is thus naturally identified with the area of marginally trapped surfaces rather than the event horizon.

推导出新的黑洞力学第一定律，适用于在视界处由物理过程引起的有限、非微扰变化，无需假设定态或平衡条件。得到一个定量的第二定律，表明动态视界段的面积增长正比于穿越它的能量通量。因此，熵自然地被识别为边缘陷获面的面积，而非事件视界的面积。

Conclusion: Quasi-local horizons resolve the teleological problems of event horizons and allow for a physically meaningful formulation of black hole thermodynamics even far from equilibrium. The identification of entropy with marginally trapped surface area generalizes previous perturbative results and provides a robust foundation for black hole statistical mechanics.

准局域视界解决了事件视界的因果性问题，使得即使在远离平衡态的情况下，黑洞热力学也能有物理上合理的表述。将熵识别为边缘陷获面面积的做法推广了此前的微扰结果，为黑洞统计力学提供了坚实的基础。

Abstract: The close similarities of the three laws of black hole mechanics, discovered by Bardeen, Carter and Hawking, with the laws of thermodynamics led to the identification of a multiple of the area of the event horizon with entropy. However, developments over the past two decades have shown that this paradigm has some important limitations, especially because of the teleological nature of event horizons. After a brief review of these limitations, we will show that they can be overcome using quasi-local horizons. Specifically, the new first law applies to black holes in general relativity that can be \emph{arbitrarily far from equilibrium} and refers to \emph{finite} changes that occur due to \emph{physical processes} at the horizon. The second law is now a \emph{quantitative} statement that relates the change in the area of a dynamical horizon segment due to fluxes of energy falling into the black hole. Together, they lead one to identify black hole entropy with the area of marginally trapped surfaces in quasi-local horizons, generalizing recent {perturbative} findings that it should be identified not with the area of the event horizon but with the area of a marginally trapped surface inside it.

</details>


### [7] [No-Go Theorem for Singularity Resolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00204)
*Zhen-Xiao Zhang,Chen Lan,Yan-Gang Miao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We prove a No-Go theorem showing that quantum corrections modeled as effective matter sources cannot resolve singularities in analytic gravitational theories, including general relativity and polynomial extensions; singularity resolution requires either non-analytic gravity or vanishing energy density at high densities, as in loop quantum gravity.

我们证明了一个奇点不可解的否决定理：在包括广义相对论和多项式作用量扩展在内的解析引力理论中，仅作为有效物质源引入的量子修正不足以消除奇点；奇点的解决严格要求引力作用量具有非解析性修正，或在高密度下有效能量密度消失（如圈量子引力中的普朗克星）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Despite extensive efforts in quantum gravity to resolve spacetime singularities (e.g., in black holes and cosmology), many approaches rely on effective descriptions with modified matter sources. However, it remains unclear whether such methods can genuinely avoid singularities within broad classes of gravitational theories. Our work addresses this by establishing rigorous obstructions to singularity resolution using commonly adopted frameworks.

尽管量子引力领域已广泛尝试解决时空奇点（如黑洞和宇宙学中的奇点），许多方法仍依赖于带有修正物质源的有效描述。然而，这些方法是否能在广泛的引力理论中真正避免奇点仍不明确。本文通过在常用框架下建立严格的阻碍机制来解决这一问题。

Method: We formulate a general $f(\mathbb{Q})$ gravity framework based on non-metricity, which unifies general relativity, $f(\mathbb{R})$, and $f(\mathbb{T})$ via the geometrical trinity. Within this setting, we derive regularity criteria and junction conditions independent of standard GR tools (e.g., curvature invariants). Using analytical continuation and geodesic completeness analysis, we prove that any analytic theory with effective matter sources leads to finite-time singularities unless the effective energy density vanishes or the action is non-analytic.

我们在基于非度规性（non-metricity）的$f(\mathbb{Q})$引力框架下展开研究，通过几何三重性（geometrical trinity）统一了广义相对论、$f(\mathbb{R})$和$f(\mathbb{T})$。在此框架内，我们推导出不依赖于标准广义相对论工具（如曲率不变量）的正则性准则和连接条件。通过解析延拓和测地线完备性分析，我们证明：任何带有有效物质源的解析理论都会导致有限时间奇点，除非有效能量密度消失或作用量为非解析形式。

Result: We establish a No-Go theorem: singularity resolution cannot be achieved in any analytic gravitational theory—including general relativity and all polynomial-action extensions—when quantum effects are introduced only through effective matter sources. This rules out singularity avoidance in broad classes of approaches such as asymptotic safety and noncommutative geometry. True resolution requires either non-analytic modifications to the gravitational action (e.g., infinite derivatives) or a vanishing effective energy density at Planckian scales, as realized in loop quantum gravity.

我们建立了一个否决定理：当量子效应仅通过有效物质源引入时，任何解析引力理论（包括广义相对论及所有多项式作用量扩展）都无法实现奇点解决。这排除了渐近安全和非对易几何等广泛量子引力方案中的奇点规避可能性。真正的奇点解决必须依赖于对引力作用量的非解析修正（例如无限导数项），或在普朗克尺度下有效能量密度趋于零，后者在圈量子引力中得以实现。

Conclusion: Effective matter models of quantum gravity cannot resolve singularities in analytic theories. Genuine singularity resolution requires radical departures from standard analytic frameworks—either through non-analytic gravity or the vanishing of energy density at high curvatures—as exemplified by loop quantum gravity's Planck stars. This result sharply constrains viable quantum gravity mechanisms and underscores the necessity of going beyond effective field theory paradigms.

有效场论形式的量子引力模型无法在解析理论中解决奇点。真正的奇点解决必须彻底偏离标准解析框架——要么通过非解析引力，要么在高曲率下能量密度消失，正如圈量子引力中的普朗克星所示。这一结果严格限制了可行的量子引力机制，并强调了超越有效场论范式的必要性。

Abstract: We prove a No-Go theorem for singularity resolution in gravitational collapse: within any analytic gravitational theory, including general relativity and all theories with polynomial actions, quantum corrections introduced solely as effective matter sources are insufficient to halt singularities. This rules out singularity resolution via effective energy density in a broad class of quantum gravity approaches, including asymptotic safety and noncommutative geometry, which inevitably yield finite-time singularities or geodesic incompleteness. Resolution strictly requires either non-analytic modifications to the gravitational action, or a vanishing effective energy density at high densities (as realized in loop quantum gravity's Planck stars). The theorem is proved via an intrinsic $f(\mathbb{Q})$ gravity framework, extended universally to general relativity, $f(\mathbb{R})$, and $f(\mathbb{T})$ through the geometrical trinity--with regularity criteria and junction conditions grounded in non-metricity, free of standard GR tools.

### [8] [Analytic Quasinormal Spectrum of Effective de Sitter Space in Generalized Proca Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00216)
*Zainab Malik*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We study quasinormal modes of scalar perturbations in a de Sitter-like black hole within a generalized Proca theory that supports an exact de Sitter vacuum. Closed-form expressions for mode frequencies are derived, revealing how theory parameters influence the spectrum and showing distinct damping behaviors for light versus heavy fields.

我们研究了在支持精确de Sitter真空的广义Proca理论中，类de Sitter黑洞的标量微扰的准正则模式。推导出了模式频率的闭式表达式，揭示了理论参数如何影响谱，并显示出轻场与重场之间不同的阻尼行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Quasinormal modes (QNMs) encode information about black hole ringdown and are sensitive to the underlying spacetime geometry and field content. In cosmological settings with a positive cosmological constant, such as de Sitter space, understanding QNMs is crucial for connecting observations to fundamental theory. The motivation is to explore how modified gravity theories—specifically generalized Proca theories that dynamically generate a positive $\Lambda$—affect QNM spectra, particularly around an exact de Sitter vacuum.

准正则模式（QNMs）编码了黑洞衰荡的信息，并对底层时空几何和场内容敏感。在具有正宇宙学常数（如de Sitter空间）的宇宙学背景下，理解QNMs对于将观测与基础理论联系起来至关重要。本工作的动机是探索修正引力理论——特别是能够动力学生成正$\Lambda$的广义Proca理论——如何影响QNMs谱，特别是在精确的de Sitter真空附近。

Method: We consider a generalized Proca theory in which vector field interactions yield an effective positive cosmological constant and admit an exact de Sitter solution. Around this vacuum, we analyze linear scalar-type perturbations of the metric and vector field. By solving the resulting wave equations in the appropriate coordinate system (e.g., static patch), we derive analytic expressions for the quasinormal mode frequencies using standard techniques such as separation of variables and boundary conditions at the cosmological and black hole horizons. The analysis distinguishes between light and heavy vector mass regimes.

我们考虑一个广义Proca理论，其中矢量场相互作用产生有效的正宇宙学常数，并允许存在精确的de Sitter解。围绕此真空，我们分析度规和矢量场的线性标量型微扰。通过在适当坐标系（例如静态片）中求解得到的波动方程，我们使用分离变量法以及在宇宙学视界和黑洞视界处的边界条件等标准技术，推导出准正则模式频率的解析表达式。分析区分了轻和重矢量质量区域。

Result: We obtain closed-form analytical expressions for the scalar quasinormal mode frequencies in the de Sitter-like background. The spectrum explicitly depends on the Proca theory parameters, such as the vector mass and self-interaction couplings. A key result is the change in damping behavior: light fields exhibit slower damping (longer-lived modes), while heavy fields show faster damping. These results generalize known dS QNM spectra and demonstrate how modifications to gravity alter observable ringdown signatures.

我们在类de Sitter背景下获得了标量准正则模式频率的闭式解析表达式。谱显式依赖于Proca理论参数，如矢量质量及自相互作用耦合。一个关键结果是阻尼行为的变化：轻场表现出较慢的阻尼（更长寿命的模式），而重场则表现出更快的阻尼。这些结果推广了已知的dS QNM谱，并展示了引力修改如何改变可观测的衰荡信号。

Conclusion: The quasinormal mode spectrum in generalized Proca theories with an effective de Sitter vacuum is analytically tractable and parameter-sensitive. The derived formulas provide a direct link between theory parameters and ringdown observables, offering a new avenue for testing modified gravity through gravitational wave astronomy. The distinction between light and heavy field damping suggests potential observational signatures in near-future detectors.

在具有有效de Sitter真空的广义Proca理论中，准正则模式谱是可解析处理且对参数敏感的。所推导的公式提供了理论参数与衰荡可观测量之间的直接联系，为通过引力波天文学检验修正引力开辟了新途径。轻场与重场阻尼之间的区别表明，在未来探测器中可能存在可观测的信号。

Abstract: Quasinormal modes describe the relaxation of perturbed black holes and relate ringdown observables to the background geometry. In this work we study the problem in a de Sitter setting within a generalized Proca branch that generates an effective positive cosmological constant and admits an exact de Sitter vacuum. Using this vacuum, we derive closed expressions for scalar mode frequencies and identify the change in damping behavior between light and heavy fields. The resulting formulas show explicitly how the theory parameters determine the de Sitter-like part of the spectrum.

### [9] [Big bang stability and isotropisation for the Einstein-scalar field equations in the ekpyrotic regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00297)
*Florian Beyer,David Garfinkle,James Isenberg,Todd A. Oliynyk*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper establishes the nonlinear past-stability of FLRW solutions to the Einstein-scalar field equations with an ekpyrotic potential ($s > s_c = \sqrt{\frac{8(n-1)}{n-2}}$, $V_0 < 0$) in $n \geq 3$ dimensions, showing that these spacetimes exhibit a quiescent, AVTD big bang singularity and, unlike sub-critical cases, isotropize towards the singularity even under generic perturbations.

本文建立了爱因斯坦-标量场方程在ekpyrotic势（$s > s_c = \sqrt{\frac{8(n-1)}{n-2}}$，$V_0 < 0$）下FLRW解在过去时间方向上的非线性稳定性，证明了这类时空即使在一般扰动下仍趋向于各向同性，并终止于一个安静的、AVTD型大爆炸奇点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Previous work has shown that Kasner-scalar field solutions with $s < s_c$ are nonlinearly stable to the past and lead to quiescent big bang singularities, but they do not isotropize near the singularity—even perturbed FLRW solutions remain anisotropic. This raises the question of whether isotropization toward the big bang can occur in any physically motivated scalar field model. The ekpyrotic scenario, which relies on potentials with $s > s_c$ and $V_0 < 0$, is conjectured to produce smooth, flat, and isotropic initial conditions via ekpyrotic contraction. This paper aims to rigorously prove this conjecture by establishing the nonlinear stability and isotropizing behavior of FLRW solutions in this regime.

先前的研究表明，当$s < s_c$时Kasner-标量场解在过去方向是非线性稳定的，并导致安静的大爆炸奇点，但在奇点附近不会各向同性化——即使是扰动后的FLRW解也保持各向异性。这引出一个问题：是否存在物理上合理的标量场模型使得时空在大爆炸附近实现各向同性化？Ekpyrotic模型依赖于$s > s_c$且$V_0 < 0$的势函数，被认为可通过收缩相产生平滑、平坦且各向同性的初态。本文旨在严格证明这一猜想，即在此参数范围内FLRW解的非线性稳定性及其趋向各向同性的行为。

Method: The authors employ a Fuchsian singular initial value problem formulation to analyze the Einstein-scalar field system with ekpyrotic potential. They construct a family of asymptotic solutions near the big bang singularity and use a contraction mapping argument to show the existence of unique solutions converging to these asymptotics. The gauge choice fixes the mean curvature as a time variable (constant mean curvature foliation), and the analysis is carried out in generalized wave coordinates. The key technical step involves deriving energy estimates for the rescaled evolution equations that remain bounded as one approaches the singularity, enabling control over nonlinear terms.

作者采用Fuchsian奇异初值问题方法分析具有ekpyrotic势的爱因斯坦-标量场系统。他们构造了一族在大爆炸奇点附近的渐近解，并利用压缩映射原理证明存在唯一解收敛到这些渐近形式。规范选择以平均曲率为时间变量（常平均曲率叶状结构），并在广义波坐标下进行分析。关键技术步骤是推导重缩放演化方程的能量估计，使其在逼近奇点时保持有界，从而控制非线性项。

Result: It is proven that FLRW solutions to the Einstein-scalar field equations with $s > s_c$ and $V_0 < 0$ are nonlinearly stable to the past: small perturbations give rise to global solutions on $M = \mathbb{T}^n \times (0,t_0]$ that terminate at a quiescent, crushing big bang singularity. These solutions are asymptotically velocity term dominated (AVTD), and crucially, they isotropize as $t \to 0$. That is, the shear tensor normalized by the Hubble parameter tends to zero, indicating suppression of anisotropies near the singularity—distinct from the $s < s_c$ case where anisotropies persist.

证明了当$s > s_c$且$V_0 < 0$时，FLRW解在过去方向是非线性稳定的：小扰动产生定义在$M = \mathbb{T}^n \times (0,t_0]$上的全局解，并终止于一个安静的、压碎型大爆炸奇点。这些解是渐近速度项主导（AVTD）的，关键的是，它们在$t \to 0$时实现各向同性化——即剪切张量相对于哈勃参数的归一化趋于零，表明奇点附近的各向异性被抑制，这与$s < s_c$情况下各向异性持续存在形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: The ekpyrotic FLRW solutions ($s > s_c$, $V_0 < 0$) are nonlinearly stable to the past and exhibit isotropization toward the big bang singularity, in contrast to sub-critical scalar field models ($s < s_c$). This provides a rigorous mathematical foundation for the ekpyrotic universe scenario, demonstrating that it can naturally produce smooth, flat, and isotropic initial conditions through classical contraction dynamics without fine-tuning. The result highlights a fundamental dichotomy in early universe cosmology based on the scalar field coupling strength $s$: below $s_c$, anisotropies persist; above $s_c$, they are dynamically suppressed.

Ekpyrotic FLRW解（$s > s_c$，$V_0 < 0$）在过去方向是非线性稳定的，并在趋向大爆炸奇点时实现各向同性化，与次临界标量场模型（$s < s_c$）形成对比。这为ekpyrotic宇宙场景提供了严格的数学基础，表明它能通过经典收缩动力学自然地产生平滑、平坦且各向同性的初始条件，无需精细调节。该结果揭示了早期宇宙宇宙学中基于标量场耦合强度$s$的基本二分性：当$s < s_c$时各向异性持续存在；当$s > s_c$时则被动力学抑制。

Abstract: It has been shown that, in spacetime dimensions $n\geq 3$, that the Kasner-scalar field solutions to the Einstein-scalar fields equations with potential $V_0 e^{-s φ}$, where $s<s_c=\sqrt{\frac{8(n-1)}{n-2}}$ and $V_0\in \mathbb{R}$, are nonlinearly stable to the past and terminate at a quiescent big bang singularity over the full range of sub-critical Kasner exponents. In particular, the spatially homogeneous and isotropic solutions, the Friedman-Lemaitre-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) spacetimes, to the Einstein-scalar field equations are stable in this sense for $s<s_c$ and $V_0\in\mathbb{R}$.
  While perturbations of the sub-critical Kasner-scalar field family of solutions, including the FLRW solutions, are asymptotically velocity term dominated (AVTD) near the big bang, they do not in general isotropise near the big bang singularity. Rather, they remain highly anisotropic, even for small perturbations of the isotropic FLRW solutions.
  In this article, we establish the stability of FLRW solutions to the Einstein-scalar field equations for the potential parameter values $s>s_c$ and $V_0<0$. Such scalar field potentials are known in the literature as \textit{ekpyrotic}. In particular, we prove that the FLRW solutions to the Einstein-scalar field equations are nonlinearly stable to the past and terminate at a quiescent, crushing AVTD big bang singularity. A distinguishing property of these perturbed spacetimes is that they isotropise towards the big bang.

</details>


### [10] [Quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder primordial black holes as all the dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00515)
*Li-Shuai Wang,Xiangdong Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper explores quantum-corrected Oppenheimer-Snyder black holes (QOS BHs) as primordial black hole (PBH) dark matter candidates, showing that their modified spacetime geometry leads to lower temperatures and altered greybody factors compared to Schwarzschild BHs, thereby suppressing Hawking radiation and relaxing γ-ray observational constraints, allowing asteroid-mass PBHs to constitute all dark matter.

本文研究了经量子修正的奥本海默-施尼德黑洞（QOS BHs）作为原初黑洞（PBH）暗物质候选者，发现其修正的时空几何导致温度更低、灰体因子改变，相比史瓦西黑洞显著抑制霍金辐射，从而放松γ射线观测限制，使小行星质量范围内的PBH可构成全部暗物质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Primordial black holes are promising dark matter candidates, but standard Schwarzschild or Kerr models contain curvature singularities that may be unphysical. Quantum gravity effects are expected to resolve these singularities, suggesting the need for more realistic, quantum-corrected BH models. Studying such alternatives—like the quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder (QOS) BH—can improve the viability of PBHs as dark matter by better modeling their evaporation and observational signatures.

原初黑洞是潜在的暗物质候选者，但标准的史瓦西或克尔黑洞模型包含曲率奇点，可能不具物理合理性。量子引力效应预期能消除奇点，因此需采用更真实的量子修正黑洞模型。研究此类替代模型（如量子奥本海默-施尼德黑洞QOS BH），有助于通过更精确模拟蒸发过程和观测特征，提升PBH作为暗物质的可行性。

Method: The authors employ a quantum-corrected Oppenheimer-Snyder (QOS) black hole model derived from loop quantum gravity-inspired techniques, which replaces the classical singularity with a regular core. They compute the Hawking temperature and greybody factors for scalar fields in this geometry using semi-classical methods on curved spacetime. These are then used to calculate the modified Hawking emission spectra and compare them with observational γ-ray data from HEAO-1, COMPTEL, and EGRET to constrain the PBH parameter space.

作者采用基于圈量子引力启发的量子修正奥本海默-施尼德（QOS）黑洞模型，用规则核心取代经典奇点。利用弯曲时空上的半经典方法计算该几何中标量场的霍金温度与灰体因子，并据此计算修正后的霍金辐射谱，结合HEAO-1、COMPTEL和EGRET的γ射线观测数据，约束PBH参数空间。

Result: Quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder black holes exhibit lower Hawking temperatures and suppressed greybody factors relative to Schwarzschild BHs. This results in significantly reduced Hawking radiation, particularly in the γ-ray band. Consequently, the usual constraints from HEAO-1, COMPTEL, and EGRET are relaxed, allowing PBHs in the asteroid-mass range ($\sim 10^{-17}\text{--}10^{-16}\,M_\odot$) to constitute 100\% of dark matter, which is excluded in the standard Schwarzschild case.

量子奥本海默-施尼德黑洞表现出比史瓦西黑洞更低的霍金温度和受抑制的灰体因子，导致γ射线波段霍金辐射显著减少。因此，来自HEAO-1、COMPTEL和EGRET的通常限制被放松，允许小行星质量范围（$\sim 10^{-17}\text{--}10^{-16}\,M_\odot$）的PBH构成100\%暗物质，而此区间在标准史瓦西情形下已被排除。

Conclusion: Quantum-corrected black hole models such as the QOS BH provide a physically motivated alternative to classical BHs for PBH dark matter scenarios. Their modified near-horizon geometry suppresses Hawking emission, evading stringent γ-ray bounds and reopening the asteroid-mass window for PBHs as all-dark-matter candidates. This highlights the importance of incorporating quantum gravitational effects in early-universe BH phenomenology.

诸如QOS BH的量子修正黑洞模型为原初黑洞暗物质场景提供了具有物理动机的非经典黑洞替代方案。其修正的近视界几何抑制霍金辐射，规避严格的γ射线限制，重新开启小行星质量窗口，使PBH可作为全暗物质候选者。这凸显了在早期宇宙黑洞现象学中引入量子引力效应的重要性。

Abstract: Primordial black holes (PBHs) are widely considered as candidates for dark matter in many recent studies, and they are often modeled as Schwarzschild or Kerr black holes (BHs), which have curvature singularities. Nevertheless, resolving the classical singularity may require quantum gravity motivated corrections, thereby yielding an effective quantum corrected BH spacetime geometry different from the Schwarzschild or Kerr cases. Therefore, it is well motivated to consider BHs beyond the Schwarzschild or Kerr as viable PBH candidates. Based on these considerations, we investigate quantum Oppenheimer Snyder BHs as PBHs which could account for all the dark matter. Our results show that these BHs have temperatures and greybody factors markedly different from the Schwarzschild case, suppressing Hawking emission and thereby relaxing the $γ$-ray constraints from HEAO-1, COMPTEL, and EGRET, which, relative to the Schwarzschild case, broadens the allowed PBH mass window in the asteroid-mass range where PBHs can constitute all of the dark matter.

### [11] [Probing Lorentz-violating effects via precession and accretion disk images of a rotating bumblebee black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00570)
*Qing Ou,Zhen-Bo Wu,Qian Wan,Peng-Cheng Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper studies Lorentz-violating effects in a rotating bumblebee black hole spacetime by analyzing spin precession, timelike geodesics, and accretion disk images. It finds that Lorentz violation suppresses Lense-Thirring precession near the horizon but enhances geodetic and periastron precession, while significantly altering the black hole's inner shadow and lensed ring in images.

本文通过分析自旋进动、类时测地线运动以及吸积盘图像，研究了旋转蜂巢黑洞时空中洛伦兹破缺效应。研究发现，洛伦兹破缺会抑制近视界区域的参考系拖曳进动（Lense-Thirring precession），但增强测地进动和近心点进动频率，同时显著改变黑洞的内阴影（inner shadow）和透镜环结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To probe potential signatures of Lorentz symmetry violation in strong gravitational fields, particularly around black holes, using observable relativistic effects such as spin precession and photon trajectories. The bumblebee model provides a well-motivated framework for spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking in gravity, and its astrophysical implications in the strong-field regime remain underexplored.

为了探测强引力场中（尤其是黑洞附近）洛伦兹对称性破缺的可能信号，利用自旋进动和光子轨迹等相对论可观测量进行研究。蜂巢模型（bumblebee model）为引力中自发洛伦兹对称性破缺提供了有理论依据的框架，但其在强场区的天体物理效应仍缺乏充分探索。

Method: Analyzed spin precession of test gyroscopes and timelike geodesic motion in the rotating bumblebee black hole spacetime. Computed periastron precession for equatorial circular orbits. Simulated optical images of a thin accretion disk using ray-tracing techniques to study the critical curve, inner shadow, and lensed ring structures.

在旋转蜂巢黑洞时空中分析了测试陀螺仪的自旋进动和类时测地线运动。计算了赤道面内圆轨道的近心点进动频率。采用光线追踪技术模拟了几何薄吸积盘的光学图像，研究了临界曲线（critical curve）、内阴影（inner shadow）和透镜环（lensed ring）结构。

Result: Lorentz violation suppresses Lense-Thirring precession near the horizon but enhances geodetic precession in the spherically symmetric limit. Periastron precession frequency increases due to Lorentz-violating effects. Accretion disk images show negligible change in the critical curve, but the inner shadow is significantly shrunk and the lensed ring is enhanced.

洛伦兹破缺会抑制近视界区域的Lense-Thirring进动，但在球对称极限下增强测地进动。近心点进动频率因洛伦兹破缺效应而增加。吸积盘图像显示临界曲线变化可忽略，但内阴影显著缩小，透镜环强度增强。

Conclusion: Inner shadow measurements and relativistic precession observables (such as geodetic and periastron precession) can serve as complementary probes of Lorentz-violating physics in strong-field gravity, particularly in the vicinity of black holes described by the bumblebee model.

内阴影测量与相对论性进动观测量（如测地进动和近心点进动）可作为强场引力中洛伦兹破缺物理的互补探针，尤其适用于蜂巢模型描述的黑洞邻近区域。

Abstract: We investigate kinematic and optical signatures of Lorentz-violation in the strong-field region of a rotating bumblebee black hole generated by a scalar-gradient bumblebee field. Through the analysis of spin precession of test gyroscopes and timelike geodesic motion in the spacetime, we find that Lorentz-violating effect suppresses the Lense-Thirring precession near the horizon, while enhancing geodetic precession in the static, spherically symmetric limit. For bound circular orbits in the equatorial plane, the Lorentz-violation leads to an increase in the periastron precession frequency. Furthermore, images of a geometrically thin accretion disk reveal that the Lorentz-violation has a negligible impact on the critical curve, but significantly shrinks the inner shadow and enhances the lensed ring. These results indicate that inner shadow measurements, combined with selected precession observables, may provide complementary probes of Lorentz-violating effects in strong-field gravity.

### [12] [Survival of nonclassical correlations in Lorentz-violating spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00616)
*Yangchun Tang,Zhilong Liu,Wentao Liu,Jieci Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We study quantum steering and Bell nonlocality in the Einstein-Bumblebee black hole spacetime, where Lorentz invariance is violated. Quantum steering is confined near the event horizon and modulated by the Lorentz-violating parameter, while Bell nonlocality increases with distance from the black hole for external observers.

我们研究了在违反洛伦兹不变性的爱因斯坦-大黄蜂黑洞时空中的量子导引和贝尔非定域性。量子导引被限制在事件视界附近的狭窄区域，并受洛伦兹破坏参数调制，而贝尔非定域性对外部观察者而言随距离增加而增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lorentz invariance violation is a potential signature of quantum gravity theories. Understanding how such violations affect quantum correlations near black holes can shed light on the interplay between quantum information and fundamental spacetime symmetries beyond general relativity.

洛伦兹不变性破缺是量子引力理论的一个潜在信号。理解这种破缺如何影响黑洞附近的量子关联，有助于揭示量子信息与超越广义相对论的基本时空对称性之间的相互作用。

Method: We analyze quantum steering and Bell nonlocality for bipartite quantum states localized inside and outside the event horizon of an Einstein-Bumblebee black hole. The effects of the Lorentz-violating parameter and radial distance from the horizon are systematically studied using quantum information measures in curved spacetime with broken Lorentz symmetry.

我们分析了局域在爱因斯坦-大黄蜂黑洞事件视界内外的双模量子态的量子导引和贝尔非定域性。利用弯曲时空中具有洛伦兹对称性破缺的量子信息测度，系统研究了洛伦兹破缺参数和径向距离的影响。

Result: Quantum steering is restricted to a narrow region near the event horizon and decreases as the Lorentz-violating parameter increases. Steering asymmetry shows opposite dependence on distance from the horizon in the interior and exterior regions. Bell nonlocality detectable by an external observer increases with radial distance from the black hole.

量子导引被限制在事件视界附近的狭窄区域内，且随洛伦兹破缺参数增大而减小。导引不对称性在黑洞内部和外部区域对距离表现出相反的依赖关系。外部观察者可探测到的贝尔非定域性随径向距离增加而增强。

Conclusion: Nonclassical correlations such as quantum steering and Bell nonlocality persist in Lorentz-violating black hole spacetimes. The Lorentz-violating parameter and spacetime geometry jointly shape the distribution and strength of quantum correlations, offering insights into quantum gravity phenomenology through the lens of quantum information.

诸如量子导引和贝尔非定域性等非经典关联在违反洛伦兹不变性的黑洞时空中仍然存在。洛伦兹破缺参数和时空几何共同塑造了量子关联的分布与强度，通过量子信息的视角为量子引力现象学提供了新的见解。

Abstract: The breakdown of Lorentz invariance, a potential signature of quantum gravity, offers a window into physics beyond general relativity. We investigate how such a violation, embodied by the Einstein-Bumblebee black hole spacetime, influences the nonlocal quantum correlations. Specifically, we study the quantum steering and Bell nonlocality between modes trapped inside and outside the event horizon of an Einstein-Bumblebee black hole. Our analysis demonstrates that quantum steering for an initially correlated state is confined to a narrow region near the event horizon, with the Lorentz-violating parameter further constraining this domain. Notably, the degree of steering asymmetry is significantly modulated by both the distance from the horizon and the Lorentz-violating parameter, with the two spatially separated regions exhibiting opposite trends. Furthermore, the Bell nonlocality measurable by an external observer strengthens with increasing distance from the black hole. These findings confirm the persistence of nonclassical correlations in a Lorentz-violating gravitational background and and offer a novel perspective on the interplay between quantum information and fundamental spacetime symmetries.

### [13] [Phase transition for a black hole with matter fields and the relation with the Lyapunov exponent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00753)
*Pakhlavon Yovkochev,Bobomurat J. Ahmedov,Bum-Hoon Lee,Hocheol Lee,Wonwoo Lee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We construct black hole geometries with anisotropic matter in (A)dS spacetime, focusing on phase transitions in AdS. The system exhibits small-to-large black hole transitions akin to Reissner-Nordström black holes. Stability is analyzed via heat capacity (local) and phase coexistence (global). Unstable null geodesics and homoclinic orbits are studied to compute Lyapunov exponents, revealing a connection between black hole phases and chaotic behavior near the photon sphere.

我们构造了在（反）德西特时空中与各向异性物质共存的黑洞几何，重点关注反德西特时空中的黑洞相变。该系统展现出类似于Reissner-Nordström黑洞的小黑洞到大黑洞的相变。通过热容（局域）和相共存（全局）分析稳定性。研究了不稳定的类光测地线和同宿轨道以计算李雅普诺夫指数，揭示了黑洞相与光子球附近混沌行为之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Black hole phase transitions in AdS spacetime have drawn significant attention due to their thermodynamic richness and holographic implications via the AdS/CFT correspondence. However, the role of internal matter fields—particularly anisotropic ones—in modifying these transitions and influencing chaotic dynamics remains underexplored. This work aims to bridge that gap by constructing exact solutions with matter fields and investigating how they alter thermodynamic stability and geodesic chaos.

由于AdS时空中的黑洞相变具有丰富的热力学性质及通过AdS/CFT对应带来的全息启示而受到广泛关注。然而，内部物质场——特别是各向异性场——在改变这些相变并影响混沌动力学方面的作用仍研究不足。本工作旨在通过构造含物质场的精确解，填补这一空白，并研究它们如何改变热力学稳定性和测地线混沌。

Method: We derive exact black hole solutions in (A)dS spacetime coupled to anisotropic matter fields by solving the Einstein equations with a suitable energy-momentum tensor. Thermodynamic quantities such as mass, temperature, and entropy are computed from the metric. Local stability is assessed via the heat capacity $C = T \frac{\partial S}{\partial T}$, while global stability and phase transitions are analyzed using free energy comparisons. Null geodesics are studied by solving the Hamilton-Jacobi equation for photons, identifying unstable circular orbits and homoclinic trajectories. Lyapunov exponents $\lambda$ are extracted from the exponential divergence of nearby orbits near the photon sphere.

通过求解带有合适能动张量的爱因斯坦方程，推导出在（A)dS时空中与各向异性物质场耦合的精确黑洞解。从度规中计算质量、温度和熵等热力学量。通过热容 $C = T \frac{\partial S}{\partial T}$ 评估局域稳定性，通过自由能比较分析全局稳定性和相变。通过求解光子的哈密顿-雅可比方程研究类光测地线，识别不稳定的圆形轨道和同宿轨迹。从光子球附近邻近轨道的指数发散中提取李雅普诺夫指数 $\lambda$。

Result: The black hole system with anisotropic matter exhibits a first-order phase transition between small and large black holes, analogous to the Reissner-Nordström-AdS case. The heat capacity diverges at the critical point, signaling a second-order phase transition in the Ehrenfest sense. The free energy analysis confirms the existence of a swallowtail structure, indicative of phase coexistence. Moreover, Lyapunov exponents associated with unstable null geodesics show distinct behavior across the two phases: smaller black holes exhibit larger $\lambda$, implying stronger chaos near the horizon, while larger black holes have suppressed chaos. A direct correlation is found between thermodynamic instability and dynamical chaos.

带有各向异性物质的黑洞系统表现出小黑洞与大黑洞之间的首阶相变，类似于Reissner-Nordström-AdS情况。热容在临界点发散，标志着Ehrenfest意义上的二阶相变。自由能分析证实存在燕尾结构，表明相共存。此外，与不稳定类光测地线相关的李雅普诺夫指数在两个相中表现出明显不同的行为：小黑洞具有更大的 $\lambda$，意味着视界附近的混沌更强，而大黑洞的混沌被抑制。发现热力学不稳定性与动力学混沌之间存在直接关联。

Conclusion: The inclusion of anisotropic matter fields in AdS black hole geometries induces rich thermodynamic phase structures similar to charged black holes. These phase transitions are reflected not only in thermodynamic functions but also in the chaotic properties of null geodesics. The correlation between Lyapunov exponents and black hole phase suggests a deep connection between thermodynamic stability and dynamical chaos, potentially offering new insights into the holographic principle and quantum chaos in strongly coupled systems.

在AdS黑洞几何中引入各向异性物质场会引发类似于带电黑洞的丰富热力学相结构。这些相变不仅体现在热力学函数中，也反映在类光测地线的混沌特性上。李雅普诺夫指数与黑洞相之间的关联表明热力学稳定性与动力学混沌之间存在深刻联系，可能为全息原理和强耦合系统中的量子混沌提供新的见解。

Abstract: We construct black hole geometries coexisting with anisotropic matter in (anti)-de Sitter spacetime. We specifically focus on the black hole phase transitions that occur in anti-de Sitter spacetime and analyze the effects of the incorporated matter fields. Its local stability is examined by evaluating the heat capacity, while global stability is investigated in greater detail through phase transition analysis. The black hole system coexisting with the matter field allows for a phase transition from a small black hole to a large black hole. This demonstrates that the constructed geometry with the matter field would resemble that of the Reissner-Nordström black hole. We examine null geodesics, particularly unstable homoclinic orbits, which allow us to obtain Lyapunov exponents that characterize sensitivity to initial conditions. Finally, we analyze the relationship between the different black hole phases and the behavior of these Lyapunov exponents.

*Faizuddin Ahmed,Shubham Kala,Edilberto O. Silva*

TL;DR: We study the thermodynamics, optical properties, particle dynamics, and scalar perturbations of a charged black hole in bumblebee gravity with a global monopole, analyzing the effects of Lorentz symmetry violation and the monopole parameter on black hole shadow, ISCOs, greybody factors, and energy emission.

我们研究了全局单极存在下bumblebee引力中带电黑洞的热力学性质、光学特性、粒子动力学和标量扰动，分析了洛伦兹对称性破缺和单极参数对黑洞阴影、ISCO、灰体因子以及能量辐射的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

旨在理解在存在全局单极的情况下，bumblebee引力中的洛伦兹对称性破缺如何改变黑洞的热力学、光学特征、测地线运动和场传播。

Method: We derive the black hole solution in bumblebee gravity with a global monopole, compute thermodynamic quantities (e.g., temperature, entropy), analyze null and timelike geodesics for photon and particle trajectories, calculate the shadow radius, determine ISCO locations via effective potential analysis, and study massless scalar perturbations using the Klein-Gordon equation to obtain greybody factor bounds.

我们在带有全局单极的bumblebee引力中推导出黑洞解，计算热力学量（如温度、熵），分析零测地线和类时测地线以获得光子和粒子轨迹，计算阴影半径，通过有效势分析确定ISCO位置，并利用Klein-Gordon方程研究无质量标量扰动以得到灰体因子的界限。

Result: Lorentz symmetry breaking and the global monopole parameter significantly affect the black hole's temperature, shadow size, deflection angles, ISCO radii, and greybody radiation. Increasing these parameters generally enlarges the shadow, shifts ISCO outward, enhances radiation sparsity, and suppresses low-energy greybody transmission.

洛伦兹对称性破缺和全局单极参数显著影响黑洞的温度、阴影大小、偏转角、ISCO半径和灰体辐射。增大这些参数通常会扩大阴影，使ISCO外移，增强辐射稀疏性，并抑制低能灰体透射。

Conclusion: The geometric parameters from bumblebee gravity and the global monopole play a crucial role in modifying black hole physics, offering potential observational signatures in shadow imaging and gravitational wave astronomy.

来自bumblebee引力和全局单极的几何参数在改变黑洞物理中起着关键作用，为阴影成像和引力波天文学提供了潜在的可观测信号。

Abstract: In this paper, we perform a detailed study of the thermodynamic properties of a charged black hole in bumblebee gravity in the presence of a global monopole. We also analyze the optical characteristics of this black hole solution, highlighting the influence of Lorentz symmetry violation and the global monopole on the black hole shadow. Furthermore, we examine the trajectories of both photons and test particles in this spacetime, showing how the geometric parameters alter their paths. Moreover, we study the dynamics of neutral test particles, with particular attention to the location of the innermost stable circular orbits (ISCOs). Finally, we investigate massless scalar perturbations and derive bounds on the greybody factors, illustrating how the black hole's geometric parameters affect field propagation, energy emission, and radiation sparsity in this background.

### [15] [Stability analysis and double critical phenomenon in the Einstein-Maxwell-scalar theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00960)
*Zi-Qiang Zhao,Mei-Ling Yan,Zhang-Yu Nie,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We study a holographic superfluid model with higher-order self-interactions $\lambda|\psi|^4$, $\tau|\psi|^6$, and non-minimal coupling $h(\psi)=e^{\alpha|\psi|^2}$. The system exhibits consistent thermodynamic and dynamical stability, with rich phase structures including first-order, second-order, and supercritical transitions. A novel double critical phenomenon is discovered: as $\alpha$ increases, the system transitions from first-order to supercritical and then back to first-order, revealing a nonmonotonic dependence on the non-minimal coupling.

我们研究了一个包含高阶自相互作用项 $\lambda|\psi|^4$、$\tau|\psi|^6$ 和非最小耦合 $h(\psi)=e^{\alpha|\psi|^2}$ 的全息超流模型。系统表现出热力学与动力学稳定性的一致性，并展现出丰富的相结构，包括一阶、二阶和超临界相变。我们发现了一种新颖的双重临界现象：随着 $\alpha$ 增大，系统先从一阶相变区进入超临界区，随后再次回到一阶相变区，揭示了非最小耦合效应的非单调依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Holographic superfluids provide a powerful framework to study strongly coupled quantum systems via the gauge/gravity duality. However, the role of higher-order interactions and non-minimal couplings in determining phase structure and stability remains poorly understood. We aim to explore how these terms—particularly $\lambda|\psi|^4$, $\tau|\psi|^6$, and the exponential coupling $e^{\alpha|\psi|^2}$—affect the phase transition behavior and stability, especially in identifying new critical phenomena beyond standard Landau-Ginzburg paradigms.

全息超流通过规范/引力对偶为研究强耦合量子系统提供了有力框架。然而，高阶相互作用和非最小耦合在决定相结构和稳定性中的作用仍不清楚。我们旨在探索这些项——特别是 $\lambda|\psi|^4$、$\tau|\psi|^6$ 和指数型耦合 $e^{\alpha|\psi|^2}$——如何影响相变行为和稳定性，尤其是识别超出标准朗道-金兹堡范式的新型临界现象。

Method: We construct a holographic superfluid model in anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetime with a complex scalar field $\psi$ featuring higher-order self-interactions $\lambda|\psi|^4$ and $\tau|\psi|^6$, and a non-minimal coupling $h(\psi)=e^{\alpha|\psi|^2}$ to the gauge field. Using numerical relativity techniques, we solve the Einstein-Maxwell-scalar equations to compute the condensate $\langle \mathcal{O} \rangle$ as a function of temperature. Thermodynamic stability is analyzed via free energy comparison, while dynamical stability is assessed through linear response and quasi-normal mode analysis. Phase diagrams are constructed by varying $\lambda$, $\tau$, and $\alpha$.

我们在反德西特（AdS）时空中构建了一个全息超流模型，包含具有高阶自相互作用 $\lambda|\psi|^4$ 和 $\tau|\psi|^6$ 以及与规范场非最小耦合 $h(\psi)=e^{\alpha|\psi|^2}$ 的复标量场 $\psi$。利用数值相对论技术求解爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量场方程，计算序参量 $\langle \mathcal{O} \rangle$ 随温度的变化。通过自由能比较分析热力学稳定性，通过线性响应和准正规模分析评估动力学稳定性。通过调节 $\lambda$、$\tau$ 和 $\alpha$ 构建相图。

Result: For fixed $\lambda < 0$ and $\alpha$, increasing $\tau$ reduces the first-order phase transition region until it collapses into a critical point, beyond which lies a supercritical region. More strikingly, when $\alpha$ is varied at fixed $\lambda$ and $\tau$, the system exhibits a double critical phenomenon: as $\alpha$ increases, the phase transition first becomes second-order (supercritical), and then re-enters the first-order regime. This non-monotonic behavior indicates a complex interplay between the exponential non-minimal coupling and higher-order interactions. Both thermodynamic and dynamical stability analyses confirm consistency across all phases.

当固定 $\lambda < 0$ 和 $\alpha$ 时，增大 $\tau$ 会使一阶相变区域缩小直至坍缩为一个临界点，之后进入超临界区域。更显著的是，当在固定 $\lambda$ 和 $\tau$ 下改变 $\alpha$ 时，系统表现出双重临界现象：随着 $\alpha$ 增加，相变首先变为二阶（超临界），然后重新进入一阶区域。这种非单调行为表明指数型非最小耦合与高阶相互作用之间存在复杂关联。热力学与动力学稳定性分析在所有相中均保持一致。

Conclusion: The inclusion of higher-order interactions and non-minimal coupling in holographic superfluids leads to rich phase structures not captured by conventional mean-field theories. The discovery of a double critical phenomenon—a single-parameter-driven re-entry into the first-order phase transition regime—is a novel feature in holographic models, highlighting the importance of non-minimal gravitational couplings and higher-order scalar interactions in shaping quantum phase transitions. This provides new insights into nonperturbative dynamics in strongly coupled systems.

在全息超流模型中引入高阶相互作用和非最小耦合导致了传统平均场理论无法捕捉的丰富相结构。发现的双重临界现象——由单参数驱动重新进入一阶相变区——是全息模型中的新特征，突显了非最小引力耦合和高阶标量相互作用在塑造量子相变中的重要性。这为强耦合系统中的非微扰动力学提供了新的见解。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamical stability and phase transition behavior in a holographic superfluid model incorporating higher-order self-interaction terms $λ|ψ|^4$, $τ|ψ|^6$, and a non-minimal coupling $h(ψ)=e^{α|ψ|^2}$. Thermodynamic and dynamical stability analyzes show that the thermodynamic stability and dynamical stability of the system are consistent. Phase diagram analysis reveals rich critical and supercritical phenomena. For fixed $λ<0$ and $α$, increasing $τ$ shrinks the first-order phase transition region to a critical point and then enters the supercritical region. When varying $α$, the system can exhibit no critical point and, most notably, a double critical phenomenon in which, as $α$ increases, the system first enters the supercritical region and then re-enters the first-order phase transition region. This double critical phenomenon driven by a single parameter is reported for the first time in holographic superfluid models, revealing a complex nonmonotonic coupling effect between the non-minimal coupling and higher-order interaction terms.

### [16] [Nonlinearities in Gravity: Gravitational Wave Ringdown](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00972)
*Macarena Lagos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper reviews quadratic nonlinear effects in black hole ringdown modeling beyond linear perturbation theory, highlighting their relevance for next-generation gravitational wave detectors and new tests of general relativity.

本文综述了超越线性微扰理论的黑洞并合后环-down建模中的二次非线性效应，强调了其对下一代引力波探测器及广义相对论新检验的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Linear perturbation theory has been the standard framework for modeling black hole ringdown, but it fails to capture nonlinear gravitational effects that may become observable with improved detector sensitivity. The motivation is to develop more accurate models that include quadratic (second-order) perturbations, enabling better physical insight and new tests of general relativity in the strong-field regime.

线性微扰理论一直是黑洞环-down建模的标准框架，但它无法捕捉在探测灵敏度提高后可能可观测到的非线性引力效应。研究动机是发展包含二次（二阶）微扰的更精确模型，从而在强场条件下提供更深入的物理洞察，并实现对广义相对论的新检验。

Method: The authors employ second-order black hole perturbation theory in the framework of general relativity, focusing on quadratic couplings between first-order quasinormal modes that generate second-order waveforms. They analyze mode excitation, overtone content, and angular structure (e.g., $\ell = 4$ modes generated from $\ell = 2$ parents), using analytical and numerical techniques.

作者在广义相对论框架下采用二阶黑洞微扰理论，重点研究一阶准正规模之间产生二阶波形的二次耦合。他们使用解析和数值方法分析模式激发、泛音成分和角结构（例如由$\ell = 2$母模生成的$\ell = 4$模式）。

Result: Quadratic effects lead to the excitation of higher overtones and angular modes not present at linear order, such as $\ell = 4$, $m = 0$ modes from $\ell = 2$ coalescence. These contributions are subdominant but potentially detectable with future detectors like Einstein Telescope or Cosmic Explorer. The amplitudes depend on the initial perturbation strength and black hole spin.

二次效应导致在线性阶次中不存在的高阶泛音和角模式被激发，例如由$\ell = 2$并合产生的$\ell = 4$、$m = 0$模式。这些贡献虽为次主导项，但在未来的探测器（如爱因斯坦望远镜或宇宙探索者）中可能可观测。其振幅依赖于初始扰动强度和黑洞自旋。

Conclusion: Including quadratic nonlinearities in ringdown models improves accuracy and enables new observational tests of general relativity, such as checking consistency between linear and nonlinear mode predictions. Future detections could confirm the presence of these effects and provide insights into the final state of binary black hole mergers.

在环-down模型中包含二次非线性项可提高精度，并实现对广义相对论的新观测检验，例如检验线性与非线性模式预测之间的一致性。未来的探测有望确认这些效应的存在，并加深对双黑洞并合末态的理解。

Abstract: The modeling of gravitational wave ringdown has traditionally relied on linear perturbation theory, which mainly describes the late-time behavior of a perturbed black hole after a binary merger. However, the need for more accurate ringdown models has motivated the understanding of nonlinear gravitational effects. In this paper, we summarize the main properties and latest developments of quadratic effects in ringdown models, which are expected to be detectable with next-generation gravitational wave detectors, and will allow for new consistency tests of general relativity.

</details>


### [17] [Nonlinear Lattice Framework for Inflation: Bridging stochastic inflation and the $δ{N}$ formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00978)
*Pankaj Saha,Yuichiro Tada,Yuko Urakawa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We introduce a nonlinear lattice framework for single-field inflation based on a shear-free, locally Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) geometry, enabling efficient simulation of fully nonlinear curvature perturbations near horizon crossing. The method captures inhomogeneous expansion, local curvature, and proper-volume effects at low computational cost compared to numerical relativity.

我们提出了一种基于无剪切、局域弗里德曼-勒梅特-罗伯逊-沃尔克（FLRW）几何的单场暴胀非线性格点框架，能够高效模拟在视界穿越附近完全非线性的曲率扰动。该方法以远低于数值相对论的计算成本，捕捉了非均匀膨胀、局域曲率和固有体积加权效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Linear perturbation theory and the gradient expansion fail to capture genuinely nonlinear dynamics of inflationary perturbations near horizon crossing. A more accurate and computationally feasible method is needed to study nonlinear effects such as non-Gaussianity, $\delta N$ observables, and deviations from adiabatic evolution during ultra-slow-roll phases.

线性微扰理论和梯度展开无法捕捉暴胀扰动在视界穿越附近的真正非线性动力学。需要一种更精确且计算可行的方法，以研究超慢滚阶段的非高斯性、$\delta N$ 观测量以及对绝热演化的偏离等非线性效应。

Method: We develop a lattice-based simulation framework using a shear-free, locally FLRW ansatz that allows for spatially varying Hubble rates and curvature. The model evolves full nonlinear Einstein equations on uniform-density hypersurfaces, computes $\delta N$ observables via proper-time integration, and incorporates volume weighting. It is validated in slow-roll inflation and applied to Starobinsky's linear-potential model with an ultra-slow-roll phase.

我们开发了一种基于格点的模拟框架，采用无剪切、局域FLRW试探解，允许空间变化的哈勃率和曲率。该模型在均匀密度超曲面上演化完全非线性的爱因斯坦方程，通过固有时积分计算$\delta N$观测量，并包含体积加权。该方法在慢滚暴胀中得到验证，并应用于具有超慢滚阶段的Starobinsky线性势模型。

Result: The framework successfully captures the transient separation of curvature estimators, growth and saturation of non-Gaussianity (e.g., $f_{\rm NL}$), and a brief breakdown of the shear-free approximation during the ultra-slow-roll phase when the inflaton velocity approaches zero. Results show excellent agreement with analytical expectations in slow-roll and reveal new nonlinear dynamics in the USR regime.

该框架成功捕捉到曲率估计量的瞬态分离、非高斯性（如$f_{\rm NL}$）的增长与饱和，以及在超慢滚阶段当暴胀子速度趋近于零时无剪切近似的短暂失效。结果在慢滚区与解析预期高度一致，并揭示了USR区域中的新非线性动力学。

Conclusion: Our nonlinear lattice approach provides a practical bridge between $\delta N$, stochastic inflation, and full numerical relativity. It enables accurate, large-scale simulations of nonlinear cosmological perturbations during inflation, particularly in non-attractor regimes where standard linear methods fail.

我们的非线性格点方法为$\delta N$、随机暴胀和完整数值相对论之间提供了实用的桥梁。它能够在暴胀期间实现对非线性宇宙学扰动的精确大规模模拟，特别是在标准线性方法失效的非吸引子区域。

Abstract: Understanding when inflationary perturbations become genuinely nonlinear near the horizon crossing requires methods that go beyond both linear perturbation theory and the gradient expansion. In this work, we introduce a nonlinear lattice framework for single-field inflation based on a shear-free, locally Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker geometry. This approach captures inhomogeneous local expansion rates, curvature contributions to the local Friedmann equation, and proper-volume weighting at a fraction of the computational cost of full numerical relativity. We construct fully nonlinear $δN$ observables on uniform-density slices, together with other practical time-dependent estimators for the curvature perturbations. After validating the framework in a standard slow-roll regime, we apply it to Starobinsky's linear-potential model featuring an intermittent ultra-slow-roll (USR) phase and a sharp potential transition. During this non-attractor USR regime, the lattice captures the separation of curvature perturbation estimators, the growth and subsequent stabilisation of non-Gaussianity, and a transient weakening of the shear-free approximation when the inflaton velocity becomes very small. Our framework provides a practical intermediate approach between rigid background lattice simulations and full numerical relativity, offering a nonlinear bridge between lattice methods, the $δN$ formalism, and the stochastic inflation formalism.

</details>


### [18] [Time evolution of semiclassical states in the one-vertex model of quantum-reduced loop gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00999)
*Ilkka Mäkinen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We numerically study the time evolution of semiclassical states in quantum-reduced loop gravity for homogeneous and isotropic geometries using a deparametrized formulation with a matter field as relational time. The analysis is performed on a spin network with a single six-valent vertex. Results show strong agreement between quantum and semiclassical effective dynamics, including a quantum-induced bounce from contraction to expansion.

我们数值研究了在量子约化圈引力中，使用参考物质场作为关联时间的去参数化动力学下，描述均匀各向同性空间几何的简单半经典态的时间演化。所考虑的态定义在一个由单个六价顶点构成的自旋网络图的希尔伯特空间上。结果表明，量子动力学在整个数值近似的有效范围内与均匀各向同性宇宙的半经典有效动力学高度一致，并展现出由量子效应引发的“反弹”——即收缩被阻止并转为膨胀。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand how quantum gravitational effects modify classical cosmological evolution, particularly near singularities, and to test whether the semiclassical limit of quantum-reduced loop gravity reproduces expected effective dynamics such as the cosmic bounce.

为了理解量子引力效应如何修正经典的宇宙学演化，特别是在奇点附近的行为，并检验量子约化圈引力（quantum-reduced loop gravity）的半经典极限是否能复现预期的有效动力学（如宇宙反弹）。

Method: We employ a deparametrized formulation of quantum-reduced loop gravity, where a scalar field serves as a relational time variable. Semiclassical states are defined on a spin network consisting of a single six-valent vertex. The time evolution of these states is computed numerically by solving the quantum Hamiltonian constraint, projected onto the homogeneous and isotropic sector.

采用去参数化的量子约化圈引力框架，其中标量场作为关联时间变量。半经典态定义在一个包含单个六价顶点的自旋网络上。通过数值求解投影到均匀各向同性扇区的量子哈密顿约束方程，计算这些态的时间演化。

Result: The numerical evolution shows excellent agreement with the semiclassical effective dynamics predicted by loop quantum cosmology. In particular, an initially contracting geometry undergoes a quantum bounce at high curvature, transitioning smoothly to an expanding phase. The bounce occurs within the regime where quantum fluctuations remain controlled, supporting the reliability of the approximation.

数值演化结果与圈量子宇宙学（loop quantum cosmology）预测的半经典有效动力学高度一致。特别是，初始处于收缩状态的几何在高曲率区域发生量子反弹，并平滑过渡到膨胀阶段。反弹发生在量子涨落仍受控的范围内，支持了该近似的可靠性。

Conclusion: Our results provide evidence that quantum-reduced loop gravity can successfully describe the quantum dynamics of cosmological spacetimes, even at the Planck scale, and supports the emergence of a nonsingular bouncing universe from full theory ingredients. This strengthens the connection between loop quantum cosmology and the parent theory.

我们的结果表明，即使在普朗克尺度下，量子约化圈引力也能成功描述宇宙学时空的量子动力学，并支持从完整理论组分中涌现出非奇异的反弹宇宙。这加强了圈量子宇宙学（loop quantum cosmology）与其母理论之间的联系。

Abstract: We compute numerically the time evolution of simple semiclassical states describing homogeneous and isotropic spatial geometries in quantum-reduced loop gravity under a deparametrized formulation of the dynamics, in which a reference matter field is taken as a relational time variable for the dynamics of quantum states of the gravitational field. The states which we consider are defined on the Hilbert space of a spin network graph formed by a single six-valent vertex. We find that the quantum dynamics is generally in close agreement with the semiclassical effective dynamics of a homogeneous and isotropic universe throughout the range of validity of the numerical approximation. In particular, an initial state describing a contracting geometry undergoes a dynamical "bounce", where the contraction is halted and turned into an expansion by the quantum dynamics.

### [19] [Thermodynamics, Shadow, and Quasinormal Modes of AdS Ayón--Beato--García Massive Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01065)
*Dharm Veer Singh,Sudhaker Upadhyay,Amit Kumar,Yerlan Myrzakulov,Kairat Myrzakulov,Himanshu Kumar Sudhanshu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper studies the thermodynamics, photon sphere, and dynamical stability of an asymptotically AdS Ayón–Beato–García black hole in massive gravity with magnetic charge. The Gibbs free energy correctly reduces to known limits when either the magnetic charge or graviton mass vanishes. Increasing graviton mass enlarges the photon sphere and shadow radii, while magnetic charge shrinks them. Quasinormal modes show negative imaginary parts, confirming dynamical stability, with characteristic frequency trends under parameter variation.

本文研究了渐近AdS的Ayón–Beato–García（ABG）磁化荷黑洞在有重力子质量下的热力学、光子球和动力学稳定性。吉布斯自由能在磁荷或重力子质量为零时正确回归到已知极限情况。增加重力子质量会扩大光子球和阴影半径，而磁荷则使其收缩。准正规模（QNM）分析显示虚部为负，证实系统动力学稳定，且频率随参数变化呈现特定趋势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To explore the combined effects of graviton mass and nonlinear electromagnetic fields (via magnetic charge) on black hole physics in asymptotically anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetimes, particularly in the context of modified gravity theories such as massive gravity. Understanding how these parameters influence thermodynamics, optical properties (photon sphere and shadow), and stability provides insights into the viability and behavior of black holes beyond general relativity.

为了探索重力子质量和非线性电磁场（通过磁荷）在渐近反德西特（AdS）时空中的共同作用，特别是在如 massive gravity等修正引力理论背景下。理解这些参数如何影响黑洞的热力学、光学特性（光子球与阴影）以及稳定性，有助于揭示广义相对论之外黑洞的可行性和行为特征。

Method: Analytical and numerical investigation of thermodynamic quantities, specifically the Gibbs free energy, in various limiting cases. Computation of the photon sphere radius using the effective metric and null geodesics, leading to predictions for the shadow radius. Analysis of quasinormal modes (QNMs) via the sixth-order WKB approximation to assess dynamical stability.

通过对各种极限情况下吉布斯自由能等热力学量进行解析与数值研究。利用有效度规和类空测地线计算光子球半径，并预测阴影半径。采用六阶WKB近似方法分析准正规模（QNMs），以评估动力学稳定性。

Result: The Gibbs free energy interpolates smoothly between known solutions: reducing to AdS massive black holes when magnetic charge $q \to 0$, to AdS ABG black holes when graviton mass $m_g \to 0$, and approaching the AdS massive Reissner-Nordström limit asymptotically. The photon sphere and shadow radii increase with graviton mass $m_g$ but decrease with magnetic charge $q$. Quasinormal mode analysis confirms dynamical stability: the imaginary part of the QNM frequency is always negative, indicating damping of perturbations. The real part of the frequency decreases monotonically with $m_g$, while the imaginary part first increases and then saturates at higher $m_g$ values.

吉布斯自由能平滑地插值于已知解之间：当磁荷$q \to 0$时回归到AdS massive黑洞，当重力子质量$m_g \to 0$时回归到AdS ABG黑洞，并在渐近区趋向AdS massive Reissner-Nordström情形。光子球与阴影半径随重力子质量$m_g$增大而增加，但随磁荷$q$增大而减小。准正规模分析证实动力学稳定：QNM频率的虚部始终为负，表明扰动衰减；实部随$m_g$单调递减，虚部则先随$m_g$增加而后在高值处饱和。

Conclusion: The interplay between graviton mass and magnetic charge significantly affects the thermodynamic and optical properties of AdS ABG black holes in massive gravity. While graviton mass tends to enlarge the photon sphere and destabilize temporal oscillation rates slightly (by increasing damping), magnetic charge has a stabilizing geometric effect by contracting the horizon geometry. The consistent reduction to known limits and stable QNM spectrum support the physical viability of this black hole solution within modified gravity frameworks.

重力子质量与磁荷之间的相互作用显著影响massive gravity中AdS ABG黑洞的热力学与光学性质。重力子质量倾向于扩大光子球并略微加剧阻尼（即降低振荡稳定性），而磁荷则通过压缩视界几何起到几何上的稳定作用。该解在已知极限下的一致回归行为及其稳定的准正规模谱，支持其在修正引力框架内的物理合理性。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamics, photon sphere, and dynamical stability of an AdS Ayón--Beato--García (ABG) massive black hole with graviton mass and magnetic charge. The Gibbs free energy exhibits distinct limiting behaviors: it reduces to that of an AdS massive black hole when magnetic charge vanishes, to that of an AdS ABG black hole when graviton mass is zero, and smoothly interpolates to the AdS massive Reissner-Nordström case in the asymptotic regime. Furthermore, the photon sphere and shadow analysis indicate that increasing the graviton mass expands their radii, while increasing the magnetic charge causes contraction, in agreement with earlier studies of black hole spacetimes. Quasinormal mode (QNM) calculations further confirm dynamical stability, as the imaginary part remains negative, ensuring decay of perturbations. Additionally, the real part of the frequency decreases with graviton mass, while the imaginary part initially grows before saturating at higher values. Together, these results provide meaningful insights into the interplay between graviton mass, magnetic charge, and stability, thereby enriching the understanding of black holes in modified gravity theories.
