### [20] [Cosmology from asymptotically safe Proca theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01090)
*Carlos Pastor-Marcos,Lavinia Heisenberg,Álvaro Pastor-Gutiérrez,Jan M. Pawlowski,Manuel Reichert*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We initiate a programme to study the ultraviolet completion of vector-tensor quantum field theories within asymptotic safety, focusing on generalized Proca theories with a vector condensate. Using the functional renormalization group, we find fixed points including a notable one with four relevant directions—two from gravity and two from matter—supporting non-perturbative renormalizability and constraining late-time cosmology.

我们启动了一项研究矢量-张量量子场论在渐近安全框架下紫外完备性的计划，重点关注具有矢量凝聚的广义Proca理论。利用泛函重整化群方法，我们发现了多个不动点，包括一个具有四个相关方向（两个来自引力，两个来自物质）的显著不动点，支持非微扰可重整性，并对晚期宇宙学施加约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To determine whether vector-tensor theories, particularly generalized Proca theories with a vector condensate, admit a consistent UV completion via asymptotic safety, and to understand how such a fundamental theory constrains infrared physics and cosmological evolution.

旨在确定矢量-张量理论（特别是带有矢量凝聚的广义Proca理论）是否可以通过渐近安全实现一致的紫外完备性，并理解这种基础理论如何约束红外物理和宇宙演化。

Method: We employ the non-perturbative functional renormalisation group (FRG) applied to a truncated action space encompassing gravity and vector degrees of freedom, searching for scaling solutions (fixed points) and computing the associated critical exponents to assess the dimensionality of the UV critical surface.

我们采用非微扰泛函重整化群（FRG）方法，作用于包含引力和矢量自由度的截断作用量空间，寻找标度解（不动点），并计算相关的临界指数以评估紫外临界曲面的维度。

Result: Several fixed points are identified, including Proca-type candidates. A particularly significant fixed point is found with exactly four relevant directions: two associated with gravitational couplings and two with matter (vector) couplings. This indicates a finite-dimensional UV critical surface and provides evidence for non-perturbative renormalisability of the system.

识别出多个不动点，包括Proca型候选者。发现一个特别重要的不动点，具有恰好四个相关方向：两个与引力耦合有关，两个与物质（矢量）耦合有关。这表明紫外临界曲面是有限维的，为系统的非微扰可重整性提供了证据。

Conclusion: Generalized Proca theories coupled to gravity may be asymptotically safe, offering a UV-complete and predictive quantum field theory framework. The existence of a UV fixed point with four relevant directions restricts the allowed infrared trajectories, thereby constraining viable cosmological scenarios at late times.

广义Proca理论与引力的耦合可能是渐近安全的，从而提供一个紫外完备且具有预测能力的量子场论框架。紫外不动点的存在（具有四个相关方向）限制了允许的红外轨迹，从而约束了晚期宇宙中的可行宇宙学场景。

Abstract: Effective field theories for cosmology offer a powerful framework to investigate the dynamics of space--time and address longstanding open puzzles. In this work, we initiate a programme to analyse the ultraviolet completion of vector--tensor quantum field theories within the asymptotic safety paradigm, focusing on generalised Proca theories with a vector condensate. This enables us to assess whether a consistent fundamental UV completion exists and to constrain the set of viable infrared scenarios. Using the non--perturbative functional renormalisation group, we identify several fixed points, including Proca--type candidates, and, among them, a particularly remarkable one with four relevant directions: two associated with gravity and two induced by matter. This provides evidence for the non--perturbative renormalisability of vector--tensor theories. We further outline how the resulting UV critical surface constrains late--time cosmology.

### [21] [Minimal Length Effects on Keplerian Scattering and Gravitational Lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01177)
*Mykola Samar,Mariia Seniak*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates how a minimal length scale, predicted by quantum gravity and generalized uncertainty principles, affects scattering trajectories in the Kepler problem, particularly through modifications to the Hamilton vector precession. It finds that such effects reduce the scattering angle and weaken gravitational lensing, especially for photons, with observational constraints derived from Einstein ring data.

本文研究了由量子引力和广义不确定性原理预测的最小长度尺度如何通过哈密顿矢量进动的修正影响开普勒问题中的散射轨迹。研究发现，这种效应会减小散射角并削弱引力透镜效应，特别是对光子而言，并利用爱因斯坦环观测数据给出了参数约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To explore potential observational consequences of quantum gravity-induced minimal length on classical unbounded orbits, particularly in astrophysical scattering processes like gravitational lensing, where high-precision measurements can probe Planck-scale effects.

探索量子引力诱导的最小长度对经典无界轨道（如引力透镜等天体物理散射过程）可能产生的可观测后果，特别是在高精度测量可探测普朗克尺度效应的情况下。

Method: Using the deformed Heisenberg algebra incorporating a minimal length, the authors analyze perturbations to the Kepler problem via the precession of the Hamilton vector $\mathbf{H}$, which characterizes orbital dynamics. They derive corrections to the scattering trajectory and compute the resulting change in the scattering angle, applying it to massless particles (photons) and comparing predictions with Einstein ring observations.

采用包含最小长度的变形海森堡代数（deformed Heisenberg algebra），作者通过哈密顿矢量$\mathbf{H}$的进动分析开普勒问题的扰动，该矢量表征轨道动力学。他们推导出散射轨迹的修正项，计算散射角的变化，并将其应用于无质量粒子（光子），与爱因斯坦环观测结果进行比较。

Result: Quantum-gravitational corrections due to minimal length lead to a reduction in the scattering angle $\Delta \theta$. For photons, this implies a weakening of gravitational lensing. By fitting theoretical predictions to Einstein ring data, the authors estimate upper bounds on the deformation parameter $\beta$ and the corresponding minimal length $\ell_{\text{min}} \sim \sqrt{\beta} \ell_{\text{Pl}}$ for the electron and Mercury.

由于最小长度引起的量子引力修正导致散射角$\Delta \theta$减小。对于光子，这意味着引力透镜效应减弱。通过将理论预测拟合到爱因斯坦环数据，作者估算了电子和水星对应的变形参数$\beta$及最小长度$\\ell_{\text{min}} \sim \sqrt{\beta} \ell_{\text{Pl}}$的上限。

Conclusion: Minimal length effects, though tiny, may leave observable imprints in high-precision astrophysical phenomena such as gravitational lensing. The Hamilton vector provides a powerful tool for analyzing such deformations in unbounded orbits, offering a novel pathway to test quantum gravity scenarios using current observational data.

尽管最小长度效应极其微弱，但可能在高精度天体物理现象（如引力透镜）中留下可观测印记。哈密顿矢量为分析无界轨道中的此类变形提供了有力工具，为利用现有观测数据检验量子引力场景开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We study the impact of a minimal length, implied by generalized uncertainty principles and quantum gravity models, on unbounded (scattering) trajectories in the Kepler problem. The analysis is based on the precession of the Hamilton vector, which serves as a sensitive probe of orbital perturbations. Within the framework of the deformed Heisenberg algebra, we derive the correction to the trajectory arising from minimal length effects. It is shown that these quantum-gravitational corrections lead to a reduction in the scattering angle. In particular, for massless particles such as photons, the quantization of space results in a weakening of the gravitational lensing effect. Using available experimental data from the observation of the Einstein ring, we estimate the deformation parameter and the corresponding minimal length for the electron and Mercury. These findings highlight potential observational signatures of minimal length scenarios in high-energy astrophysics and gravitational optics.

</details>

### [22] [An All-Loop Amplituhedron in Two Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00083)
*Jonah Stalknecht*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We introduce a positive geometry $\Delta^{(L)}$ in 2D Minkowski space as a generalization of loop amplituhedra, compute its canonical form corresponding to massless banana integrals, integrate it exactly at all loops, observe IR exponentiation, resum into a Fox--Wright function, and uncover a path integral in the $L\to\infty$ limit.

我们引入了一个定义在二维闵可夫斯基空间中的正几何 $\Delta^{(L)}$，作为圈图amplituhedron的推广；计算其对应于无质量香蕉图的典范形式，在所有圈阶上精确积分，观察到红外指数化现象，将其重求和为Fox-Wright函数，并在 $L\to\infty$ 极限下发现一个路径积分结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The amplituhedron formalism has revolutionized the understanding of scattering amplitudes in planar $\mathcal{N}=4$ super Yang--Mills, but its extension beyond four dimensions and standard kinematic configurations remains challenging. By reducing to two-dimensional Minkowski space $\mathbb{R}^{1,1}$, we aim to simplify the geometry while preserving essential features of loop-level positivity and integrability, enabling exact all-loop calculations and new insights into the geometric origin of IR divergences and strong-coupling limits.

amplituhedron形式主义革新了人们对平面 $\mathcal{N}=4$ 超杨-米尔斯理论中散射振幅的理解，但其向四维以上及非常规运动学构型的推广仍具挑战性。通过降至二维闵可夫斯基空间 $\mathbb{R}^{1,1}$，我们旨在简化几何结构的同时保留圈层级正性与可积性的关键特征，从而实现精确的全圈阶计算，并深入理解红外发散与强耦合极限的几何起源。

Method: We define the geometry $\Delta^{(L)}$ using lightcone variables in dual momentum space, showing it arises as a boundary of the standard $L$-loop amplituhedron. The canonical differential form is constructed via positivity conditions on $2L$ parameters, yielding a logarithmic form whose residue structure encodes massless banana diagrams. Integration is performed in dimensional regularization using Mellin--Barnes representations and gamma function identities, allowing closed-form evaluation at any loop order. Resummation is achieved via properties of the Fox--Wright generalized hypergeometric function. The large-$L$ limit is analyzed by interpreting the integrated result as a worldline path integral.

我们在对偶动量空间的光锥变量下定义几何 $\Delta^{(L)}$，并表明其可作为标准 $L$-圈amplituhedron的某一边界出现。典范微分形式由$2L$个参数上的正性条件构造，产生一个对数形式，其留数结构编码了无质量香蕉图。积分在维数正规化下使用Mellin-Barnes表示与伽马函数恒等式完成，实现了任意圈阶的闭式计算。重求和利用Fox-Wright广义超几何函数的性质完成。大-$L$极限通过对积分结果解释为世界线路径积分进行分析。

Result: The canonical form of $\Delta^{(L)}$ is shown to generate precisely the integrand of $L$-loop massless banana diagrams. Upon integration in $d=2-2\epsilon$ dimensions, the result is expressed as a ratio of gamma functions: $\mathcal{I}^{(L)} \propto \Gamma(1 + L\epsilon)/\Gamma(1 + \epsilon)^L$, demonstrating exact IR exponentiation as $\mathcal{I}^{(L)} \sim (\mathcal{I}^{(1)})^L$. The all-loop resummation yields a non-perturbative expression in terms of the Fox--Wright function $_1\Psi_1$. In the $L\to\infty$ limit with fixed $\lambda = L\cdot\text{coupling}$, the amplitude is governed by a path integral over closed worldlines in $\mathbb{R}^{1,1}$, suggesting a dual description akin to a worldsheet or collective field theory.

$\Delta^{(L)}$ 的典范形式被证明恰好生成 $L$-圈无质量香蕉图的被积函数。在 $d=2-2\epsilon$ 维积分后，结果表示为伽马函数之比：$\mathcal{I}^{(L)} \propto \Gamma(1 + L\epsilon)/\Gamma(1 + \epsilon)^L$，展现出精确的红外指数化 $\mathcal{I}^{(L)} \sim (\mathcal{I}^{(1)})^L$。全圈重求和得到以Fox-Wright函数 $_1\Psi_1$ 表示的非微扰表达式。在固定 $\lambda = L\cdot\text{coupling}$ 的 $L\to\infty$ 极限下，振幅由 $\mathbb{R}^{1,1}$ 上闭合世界线的路径积分主导，暗示一种类似世界面或集体场论的对偶描述。

Conclusion: The geometry $\Delta^{(L)}$ provides a solvable model for loop amplituhedra in a reduced dimension, revealing deep connections between positive geometry, infrared physics, and emergent spacetime structures. The exact all-loop integrability, IR exponentiation, and emergence of a worldline path integral in the strong-coupling limit highlight the power of geometric approaches to quantum field theory. This framework offers a promising toy model for exploring non-perturbative phenomena and the holographic emergence of space-time.

几何 $\Delta^{(L)}$ 在降维下为圈图amplituhedron提供了一个可解模型，揭示了正几何、红外物理与涌现时空结构之间的深刻联系。精确的全圈可积性、红外指数化以及强耦合下世界线路径积分的出现，凸显了几何方法在量子场论中的强大潜力。该框架为研究非微扰现象与时空的全息涌现提供了有前景的玩具模型。

Abstract: We define and study a positive geometry $Δ^{(L)}$ which serves as a natural generalization of loop amplituhedra to two-dimensional Minkowski space $\mathbb{R}^{1,1}$. The geometry is formulated in the framework of lightcone geometries in dual momentum space, and can equivalently be obtained as a specific boundary of the $L$-loop amplituhedron for $\mathcal{N}=4$ super Yang--Mills. The simplicity of the two-dimensional setting allows us to calculate the canonical form of $Δ^{(L)}$ at any loop order, which is shown to correspond to massless banana graphs. We integrate the canonical form at all loop orders in dimensional regularization, and find that the full IR divergence structure at $L$-loops is captured by the $L$th power of the one-loop result, a phenomenon analogous to IR exponentiation. Furthermore, these integrated functions can be resummed into a closed-form non-perturbative result given by a Fox--Wright function. In the limit where $L\to\infty$, the geometry gives rise to a path integral over worldlines, suggesting the emergence of a dual description at strong coupling. This construction provides a simple and tractable setting in which to explore the geometry of loop amplitudes, and offers a controlled toy model for investigating loop amplituhedra beyond their standard scope.

</details>


### [23] [Instanton condensation and a new phase of BPS black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00095)
*Jack Holden*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper studies the 1/16-BPS superconformal index for BPS black holes in $AdS_5 \times S^5$ with equal charges, revealing an instability in the microcanonical ensemble due to instanton condensation in the matrix model. This signals a new dominant phase near the small black hole threshold, which is proposed to correspond to the partially deconfined phase in the dual gauge theory.

本文研究了在$AdS_5 \times S^5$中具有等电荷的BPS黑洞的1/16-BPS超共形指数，通过矩阵模型中的瞬子凝聚揭示了微正则系综中的不稳定性。这表明在小黑洞鞍点附近存在一个新的主导相，该相被提议对应于对偶规范理论中的部分退禁闭相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent studies have been unclear about the location and nature of the partially deconfined phase in the BPS black hole phase diagram in $AdS_5/CFT_4$. The authors aim to resolve this confusion by analyzing non-perturbative effects (instantons) in the matrix model description of the superconformal index, seeking to identify where partial deconfinement occurs and how it relates to black hole physics.

近期研究对于在$AdS_5/CFT_4$中BPS黑洞相图里部分退禁闭相的位置和本质尚不清楚。作者旨在通过分析超共形指数的矩阵模型描述中的非微扰效应（瞬子），来澄清这一困惑，并确定部分退禁闭发生的区域及其与黑洞物理的关系。

Method: The analysis is based on the matrix model representation of the 1/16-BPS superconformal index at large $N$, where saddle-point approximations are used. Instanton contributions are computed and their condensation is analyzed as a signature of phase instability. The eigenvalue distribution of the matrix model is studied to identify transitions between confined, partially deconfined, and fully deconfined phases.

该分析基于大$N$下1/16-BPS超共形指数的矩阵模型表示，使用鞍点近似方法。计算了瞬子贡献并通过其凝聚现象作为相不稳定性的标志。通过研究矩阵模型的本征值分布，识别禁闭、部分退禁闭和完全退禁闭相之间的转变。

Result: Instanton condensation is found in the matrix model for black hole states just below the small black hole threshold, signaling a new instability and a previously unidentified dominant phase. This phase is argued to be the holographic dual of the partially deconfined phase in the gauge theory, occurring when only a subset of $SU(N)$ degrees of freedom deconfine. The results clarify the position of partial deconfinement in the BPS phase diagram.

发现在略低于小黑洞阈值的黑洞态对应的矩阵模型中存在瞬子凝聚，标志着一种新的不稳定性和此前未识别出的主导相。该相被认为是规范理论中部分退禁闭相的全息对偶，发生在仅有一部分$SU(N)$自由度退禁闭时。结果澄清了部分退禁闭在BPS相图中的位置。

Conclusion: The study establishes a concrete link between instanton-induced instabilities in the superconformal index and the partially deconfined phase in $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM via holography. It highlights the role of non-perturbative effects in identifying new phases of BPS black holes and provides a refined understanding of how colour degrees of freedom emerge in the gravitational description.

本研究通过全息原理建立了超共形指数中瞬子诱导的不稳定性与$\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM中部分退禁闭相之间的具体联系。强调了非微扰效应在识别BPS黑洞新相中的作用，并深化了对引力描述中色自由度如何出现的理解。

Abstract: We analyse the 1/16-BPS superconformal index for BPS black holes at equal charge in $AdS_5 \times S_5$, uncovering evidence for a new instability in the microcanonical ensemble along the small black hole saddle. This is indicated by instanton condensation in the matrix model description of the index. This instability occurs for black holes of radius close to, but below, the scale at which black holes become `small', and implies a new dominant phase in this region. We propose a connection to the partially deconfined phase in the field theory dual description. This would resolve recent confusion about the location of the partially deconfined phase in the BPS phase diagram and promises new avenues for understanding confinement, partial deconfinement, and the encoding of colour degrees of freedom under the holographic map. We also motivate the importance of instantons in partial deconfinement from a matrix model perspective.

### [24] [de Sitter extremal surfaces, time contours, complexifications and pseudo-entropies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00108)
*K. Narayan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates no-boundary de Sitter (dS) extremal surfaces and their pseudo-entropy for generic boundary subregions, analyzing both real and complex extremal surfaces in different regimes (large vs. small subregions). It emphasizes the role of complex time contours in defining area integrals and identifies multiple extremal surfaces with equivalent areas related by deformations in the complex time plane. These findings suggest a connection between entropy structures in de Sitter and those in anti-de Sitter (AdS) via analytic continuation, illustrated explicitly in $dS_3$. Implications for multi-subregion entropy inequalities and boundary mappings in the static patch are also discussed.

本文研究了无边界德西特（de Sitter, dS）时空中的极值面及其对应未来边界上一般子区域的伪熵。分析涵盖大、小区域情形下的实和复极值面，强调通过复时间平面上的时间轮廓定义面积积分的作用，并发现多条可通过无阻碍形变相互转换的等面积极值面。这些结果暗示德西特熵结构可通过解析延拓与反德西特（AdS）相对应，以$dS_3$为例进行了详细说明，并讨论了多区域熵不等式及静态区中不同切片子区域间的光映射关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding quantum gravity and holography in de Sitter space remains a major challenge, especially compared to the well-developed AdS/CFT correspondence. The no-boundary proposal offers a framework for defining wave functions of the universe, but its implications for entanglement and entropy in dS need clarification. This work aims to extend recent studies on extremal surfaces in dS by systematically analyzing pseudo-entropy and the geometric structure of extremal surfaces for generic boundary regions, particularly through the lens of complex saddles and analytic continuation from AdS.

理解德西特空间中的量子引力与全息原理仍是重大挑战，尤其相较于成熟的AdS/CFT对应而言。无边界提案为宇宙波函数提供了框架，但其在dS中对纠缠与熵的影响尚不明确。本研究旨在通过系统分析一般边界区域下伪熵及极值面的几何结构（特别是借助复鞍点与从AdS的解析延拓），扩展近年来关于dS中极值面的研究。


Method: The authors analyze extremal surfaces in no-boundary $dS$ spacetime by solving the geodesic or minimal surface equations in Lorentzian and Euclidean signatures, extended into the complex time plane. They define the area of pseudo-entropy using path integrals over complex time contours, identifying when different contours yield equivalent results under continuous deformation. The analysis is carried out in general dimensions and illustrated concretely in $dS_3$, where explicit solutions and geometric interpretations are obtained. They also employ analytic continuation from known $AdS$ results and examine how subregions on different slices (future boundary vs. static patch) can be related via null rays.

作者通过求解洛伦兹和欧几里得符号下的测地线或极小曲面方程（并延拓至复时间平面）来分析无边界$dS$时空中的极值面。利用沿复时间轮廓的路径积分定义伪熵对应的面积，识别不同轮廓在连续形变下何时给出等价结果。该分析在一般维度中进行，并以$dS_3$为具体实例展开，获得显式解与几何解释。同时采用从已知AdS结果的解析延拓，并考察未来边界与静态区中不同切片上的子区域如何通过类光线关联。


Result: For large subregions, both timelike+Euclidean and complex extremal surfaces exist with clear geometric interpretations; for small subregions, only complex extremal surfaces are found, analogous to Poincar\'e $dS$. The area integrals are defined via integration over complex time contours, and multiple extremal surfaces are found to have indistinguishable pseudo-entropies if their contours can be continuously deformed into one another in the complex time plane. This implies equivalence among complex replica geometries in $dS$. In $dS_3$, explicit solutions confirm this picture. Furthermore, entropy inequalities for multiple subregions in $dS$ appear to mirror those in $AdS$ via analytic continuation, suggesting a deeper structural correspondence.

对于大子区域，存在具有清晰几何解释的类时+欧几里得及复极值面；对于小子区域，则仅存在复极值面，类似于庞加莱$dS$情形。面积积分通过复时间轮廓定义，若不同轮廓可在复时间平面内连续形变互转，则对应极值面的伪熵不可区分。这表明$dS$中复副本几何之间存在等价性。在$dS_3$中，显式解验证了这一图像。此外，多子区域的熵不等式在$dS$中似乎可通过解析延拓对应于$AdS$中的结果，暗示更深层的结构对应关系。


Conclusion: The study reveals that pseudo-entropy in de Sitter space, computed via no-boundary extremal surfaces, is governed by complex saddle geometries connected through analytic continuation in the complex time plane. Equivalent pseudo-entropy values arise from time contours that are homotopic in this plane, indicating a form of contour equivalence in gravitational path integrals. This supports a holographic interpretation where $dS$ entropy structures are encoded versions of $AdS$ ones. The results provide new insights into entanglement in cosmological spacetimes and suggest a unified framework for understanding extremal surfaces and entropy in $dS$ via complexification and analytic continuation.

研究表明，通过无边界极值面计算的德西特空间伪熵由复鞍点几何控制，这些几何通过复时间平面内的解析延拓相互连接。若时间轮廓在此平面内同伦，则产生等价的伪熵，揭示引力路径积分中的一种轮廓等价性。这支持了一种全息诠释：$dS$熵结构是$AdS$结构的编码版本。结果为宇宙学时空中纠缠的理解提供了新视角，并暗示通过复化与解析延拓可建立统一框架来理解$dS$中的极值面与熵。

Abstract: We study no-boundary de Sitter extremal surfaces and their pseudo-entropy areas for generic subregions at the future boundary, building on previous work. For large subregions, timelike+Euclidean extremal surfaces exist with transparent geometric interpretations, as do complex ones. The situation for small subregions is analogous to Poincare $dS$ and only complex extremal surfaces exist. In general, the extremal surface area integrals are defined via time contours in the complex time plane. We find multiple extremal surfaces with indistinguishable areas whose time contours can be deformed into each other in the complex time plane without obstruction, which are equivalent for these purposes. This also suggests equivalences between complex $dS$ replica geometries. We discuss $dS_3$ as a simple example at length. This suggests a picture for multiple subregions and entropy inequalities in de Sitter, as encoding $AdS$ ones via analytic continuation. We also discuss mapping future boundary subregions and those on constant time slices in the static patch via lightrays.

</details>


### [25] [How to (Non-)Perturb a BPS Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00116)
*Alberto Castellano,Matteo Zatti*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper connects non-perturbative corrections in BPS black hole physics to the dynamics of probe branes in $\text{AdS}_2\times \mathbf{S}^2$ with electromagnetic fluxes, showing how D0-brane effects in M-theory on a Calabi-Yau threefold reproduce Gopakumar--Vafa invariants in the black hole attractor background.

本文通过研究在具有电磁通量的$\text{AdS}_2\times \mathbf{S}^2$中探针膜的动力学，建立了BPS黑洞物理中非微扰修正与M理论中卡拉比-丘三重态上D0膜效应之间的联系，并表明这些效应如何在黑洞吸引子背景下重现Gopakumar--Vafa不变量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the origin of non-perturbative corrections to BPS black hole observables in 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ supergravity, particularly how such corrections are encoded in the near-horizon geometry and related to topological string theory and D-brane physics.

研究动机是理解4维$\mathcal{N}=2$超引力中BPS黑洞可观测量的非微扰修正的起源，特别是这些修正如何被编码在近 horizon 几何中，并与拓扑弦理论和D膜物理相关联。

Method: The authors consider Type II topological string theory contributions from an infinite tower of F-terms, approximated via the constant map contribution at large volume. They study probe D-branes in $\text{AdS}_2\times \mathbf{S}^2$ with electric-magnetic fluxes, analyzing classical trajectories and the 1-loop effective action. A semiclassical analysis is combined with exact path integral evaluation to relate results to the Gopakumar--Vafa integral.

作者考虑来自无限塔F项的II型拓扑弦论贡献，在大体积下通过常数映射近似处理。他们研究在带有电磁通量的$\text{AdS}_2\times \mathbf{S}^2$中的探针D膜，分析经典轨迹和1圈有效作用量。结合半经典分析与精确路径积分计算，将结果与Gopakumar--Vafa积分关联起来。

Result: The 1-loop effective action of probe branes produces force conditions and trajectory constraints that qualitatively explain the structure of non-perturbative corrections. The exact path integral reproduces the Gopakumar--Vafa integral evaluated in the black hole attractor geometry, demonstrating that D0-brane states in M-theory control the higher-derivative corrections and backreacted black hole physics.

探针膜的1圈有效作用量产生力条件和轨迹约束，定性解释了非微扰修正的结构。精确路径积分重现了在黑洞吸引子几何中计算的Gopakumar--Vafa积分，表明M理论中的D0膜态控制着高导数修正和完全反作用的黑洞物理。

Conclusion: The physics of fully backreacted BPS black holes is governed by light D-brane states in the near-horizon region, whose contributions to higher-derivative operators (via topological strings) determine non-perturbative corrections. This establishes a direct link between flat-space Gopakumar--Vafa invariants and black hole microstructure in $\text{AdS}_2$.

完全反作用的BPS黑洞物理由近horizon区域的轻D膜态支配，这些态通过拓扑弦对高导数算符的贡献决定了非微扰修正。这建立了平直空间Gopakumar--Vafa不变量与$\text{AdS}_2$中黑洞微观结构之间的直接联系。

Abstract: We relate the structure of non-perturbative corrections to BPS black hole observables in flat-spacetime theories with certain properties of probe charged particles in the near-horizon geometry. Concretely, we consider 4d $\mathcal{N} = 2$ supergravity with an infinite tower of F-terms and probe branes in $\text{AdS}_2\times \mathbf{S}^2$ backgrounds threaded by constant electric-magnetic fields. The higher dimensional operators we pick are computed by Type II topological string theory, and we approximate them via the constant map contribution, which is valid at large volume and can be interpreted as arising from D0-branes integrated out in M-theory on a Calabi-Yau threefold times a circle. We analyze the resulting force conditions on massive particles carrying $(q_A, p^A)$ charges, their classical trajectories, and the 1-loop effective action they produce. A simple semiclassical analysis allows us to understand qualitatively the structure of the non-perturbative corrections. The exact path integral assessment then reproduces the Gopakumar--Vafa integral of the flat-spacetime theory, now evaluated in the black hole attractor geometry. Thus, we make explicit how the physics of the fully backreacted black hole solution is controlled by the behaviour of the light D-brane states which generate the relevant set of higher derivative corrections.

### [26] [The Observer Paradigm in Semiclassical Gravity: A Postmodern Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00139)
*Sean McBride*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper proposes a postmodern critique of observer-dependent constructions in semiclassical gravity, arguing that the tension between observer-supplied and observer-free descriptions of closed universes reflects a fundamental ambiguity in quantum gravity. It introduces a 'post-postmodern' perspective that embraces this incompatibility as intrinsic to quantum gravity's degrees of freedom.

本文对半经典引力中依赖观察者的构造提出了后现代批判，认为封闭宇宙中依赖观察者与不依赖观察者的描述之间的张力反映了量子引力中的基本模糊性。作者提出一种“后后现代”观点，将这种不相容性视为量子引力自由度的内在特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent developments in semiclassical gravity rely on observers to define meaningful Hilbert spaces in closed universes, raising foundational questions about the role of observation in quantum gravity. The author seeks to interrogate the philosophical underpinnings of such 'observer rules', framing them not as technical problems to be resolved but as symptoms of deeper conceptual instability—what is termed a breakdown of metanarratives in theoretical physics.

近期半经典引力的发展依赖于观察者来在封闭宇宙中定义有意义的希尔伯特空间，这引发了关于观测在量子引力中作用的基础性问题。作者旨在审视这些“观察者规则”的哲学基础，将其视为理论物理学中元叙事崩溃的征兆，而非需要解决的技术问题。

Method: The analysis employs a postmodern philosophical framework to interpret recent results in gravitational path integrals and subregion algebras in quantum gravity. Rather than proposing new mathematical formalism, it reinterprets existing tensions—such as the observer's dual role in enabling and destabilizing the perturbative Hilbert space—as indicative of irreducible epistemic limits, aligning with post-postmodern thought that accepts contradiction without resolution.

该分析采用后现代哲学框架来解读量子引力中引力路径积分和子区域代数的最新结果。它并不提出新的数学形式体系，而是将现有矛盾——例如观察者在建立和破坏微扰希尔伯特空间中的双重角色——重新解释为不可约化的认知局限的体现，与接受矛盾而不寻求解决的后后现代思想一致。

Result: The paper concludes that attempts to formulate consistent 'observer rules' in closed universe quantum gravity are inherently self-undermining, reflecting a metanarrative crisis in physics. It posits that the resulting ambiguity should not be eliminated but embraced as a feature of quantum gravity, marking the first known integration of post-postmodern philosophy into physical theory.

本文得出结论：在封闭宇宙量子引力中制定一致的“观察者规则”的尝试本质上是自我瓦解的，反映了物理学中的元叙事危机。作者认为由此产生的模糊性不应被消除，而应被接受为量子引力的一个特征，这是已知首次将后后现代哲学融入物理理论。

Conclusion: Quantum gravity in closed universes exhibits an irreducible tension between observer-dependent and observer-free descriptions. Instead of seeking a unified resolution, the paper advocates for a post-postmodern stance that treats this ambiguity as fundamental, thereby redefining the nature of physical explanation in quantum cosmology.

封闭宇宙中的量子引力在依赖观察者与不依赖观察者的描述之间表现出不可化约的张力。本文主张采取一种后后现代立场，将这种模糊性视为基本特征，从而重新定义量子宇宙学中物理解释的本质。

Abstract: Recent advances in semiclassical gravity, both in our understanding of the gravitational path integral and the algebraic structure of a gravitating subregion, rely on the presence of an observer to obtain a nontrivial Hilbert space for closed universe backgrounds. Here I examine this proposal from a postmodern lens, identifying attempts to define ``observer rules'' as manifestations of metanarrative breakdown: the observer both supplies and undermines the perturbative gravitational Hilbert space. Rather than resolving this tension, I advocate for a post-postmodern acceptance of the incompatibility between observer-dependent and observer-free descriptions of closed universes, treating the ambiguity as a feature of quantum gravity's fundamental degrees of freedom. To my knowledge, this is the first reference to post-postmodernism in concert with physics.

</details>


### [27] [Manifest Moebius invariance of massive tree-level three-point amplitudes in pure spinor superspace](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00141)
*Chen Huang,Carlos R. Mafra,Yi-Xiao Tao*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: A new compact nested-bracket representation for massive tree-level three-point open-string amplitudes is derived using BRST cohomology in pure spinor superspace, with manifest Moebius invariance.

使用纯旋量超空间中的BRST上同调性质和非自由场OPE括号的恒等式，推导出一种新的紧凑嵌套括号表示，用于有质量树级三点开弦振幅，其莫比乌斯不变性是显然的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To construct a manifestly Moebius-invariant and supersymmetric formulation of massive string amplitudes in the pure spinor formalism, overcoming limitations of previous representations that obscure symmetry properties.

为了在纯旋量形式中构建一个显然具有莫比乌斯不变性和超对称性的有质量弦振幅表述，克服以往表示中对称性不明显的局限性。

Method: Utilized BRST cohomology in pure spinor superspace and operator product expansion (OPE) identities for non-free fields to derive a nested-bracket structure; performed explicit superspace computations for level-one massive states and established BRST recurrence relations for generalization to arbitrary mass levels.

利用纯旋量超空间中的BRST上同调和非自由场的OPE恒等式推导嵌套括号结构；对一级有质量态进行显式的超空间计算，并建立BRST递推关系以推广到任意质量层级。

Result: A new compact expression for massive three-point open-string amplitudes with manifest Moebius invariance is obtained; BRST recurrence relations are derived that relate numerators across different mass levels, confirming the structure at level one and supporting its general validity.

得到了一种新的、具有显然莫比乌斯不变性的有质量三点开弦振幅紧凑表达式；推导出关联不同质量层级振幅分子的BRST递推关系，在一级得到验证并支持其普适性。

Conclusion: The nested-bracket representation provides a powerful framework for computing massive string amplitudes in a way that preserves key symmetries such as Moebius invariance and BRST symmetry, enabling systematic extensions to higher mass levels within the pure spinor formalism.

嵌套括号表示为计算有质量弦振幅提供了一个强大框架，保持了莫比乌斯不变性和BRST对称性等关键对称性，可在纯旋量形式下系统推广至更高质量层级。

Abstract: Using BRST cohomology properties in pure spinor superspace and identities for OPE brackets of non-free fields, we obtain a new compact nested-bracket representation of massive tree-level three-point open-string amplitudes in which Moebius invariance is manifest. Explicit superspace calculations for amplitudes with level-one massive states confirm this finding, and we derive new BRST recurrence relations among three-point numerators to extend the result to arbitrary mass levels. This provides a manifestly Moebius-invariant expression for massive three-point amplitudes in the pure spinor formalism.

### [28] [Sine-Gordon solitons in AdS, dS and other hyperbolic spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00160)
*E. T. Akhmedov,D. V. Diakonov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We discover infinitely many soliton-like solutions in a deformed sine-Gordon theory in $(d+1)$-dimensional $AdS_{d+1}$ for $d \geq 2$, single solitons in $dS_{d+1}$, $\mathrm{H}_{d+1}$, and $AdS_2$, and a deformed kink in scalar field theory. The deformation resembles the bosonic sector of flat-space supersymmetric sine-Gordon theory. While some multisoliton solutions reduce to boosted flat-space solitons in the infinite radius limit, others have no flat-space counterpart.

我们发现了一种在$d \geq 2$的$(d+1)$维$AdS_{d+1}$时空中变形正弦-戈登理论中的无限多类孤立子解，以及在$d \geq 1$的$dS_{d+1}$、$\mathrm{H}_{d+1}$空间和$AdS_2$中的单个孤立子解，并发现了$AdS_2$中具有多项式势的标量场论中kink解的一种变形。该变形显著类似于平直空间超对称正弦-戈登理论的玻色部分。在无限半径极限下，单个孤立子解退化为平直空间中的孤立子；而某些参数下的$AdS_{d+1}$（$d \geq 2$）多孤立子解则退化为沿法向运动的加速孤立子，但也存在一些在平直空间极限下无对应物的多孤立子解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The study aims to extend soliton physics beyond flat spacetime by exploring non-perturbative solutions in curved geometries such as $AdS_{d+1}$, $dS_{d+1}$, and $\mathrm{H}_{d+1}$. Understanding how solitons behave in these backgrounds is crucial for applications in holography, early universe cosmology, and quantum gravity. The resemblance to supersymmetric sine-Gordon theory motivates investigating whether such deformations encode hidden symmetries or integrable structures in curved spacetime.

本研究旨在通过探索反德西特（$AdS_{d+1}$）、德西特（$dS_{d+1}$）和洛巴切夫斯基（$\mathrm{H}_{d+1}$）等弯曲时空中的非微扰解，将孤立子物理推广到平直时空之外。理解孤立子在这些背景下的行为对于全息原理、早期宇宙学和量子引力的研究至关重要。该模型与超对称正弦-戈登理论的相似性促使人们探究此类变形是否在弯曲时空中编码了隐藏对称性或可积结构。

Method: The authors consider a deformation of the sine-Gordon model in curved spacetime with constant curvature, specifically in $AdS_{d+1}$, $dS_{d+1}$, and $\mathrm{H}_{d+1}$. They analyze classical field equations derived from a scalar field action with a modified potential that preserves certain solvability properties. By solving the resulting nonlinear partial differential equations under appropriate boundary conditions and symmetry assumptions (e.g., spherical or planar symmetry), they identify exact soliton-like solutions. The infinite radius (flat space) limit is carefully taken to compare with known flat-space solitons.

作者在具有恒定曲率的弯曲时空中考虑了正弦-戈登模型的一种变形，具体是在$AdS_{d+1}$、$dS_{d+1}$和$\mathrm{H}_{d+1}$中。他们从一个带有修正势的标量场作用量出发，推导并分析经典场方程，该势保留了某些可解性质。通过在适当的边界条件和对称性假设（如球对称或平面对称）下求解所得的非线性偏微分方程，识别出精确的类孤立子解。并通过仔细取无限半径（平直空间）极限，与已知的平直空间孤立子进行比较。

Result: Infinitely many soliton-like solutions are found in $AdS_{d+1}$ for $d \geq 2$, while only single solitonic solutions exist in $dS_{d+1}$ and $\mathrm{H}_{d+1}$ for $d \geq 1$ and in $AdS_2$. A deformed kink solution is obtained in scalar field theory with polynomial potential in $AdS_2$. The deformation closely mirrors the bosonic sector of flat-space supersymmetric sine-Gordon theory. In the infinite radius limit, single solitons reduce to standard flat-space solitons, and certain multisoliton configurations in $AdS_{d+1}$ reduce to a single boosted soliton. However, some multisoliton solutions in $AdS_{d+1}$ do not admit a flat-space limit, indicating genuinely non-perturbative effects in curved spacetime.

在$d \geq 2$的$AdS_{d+1}$中发现了无限多个类孤立子解，而在$d \geq 1$的$dS_{d+1}$、$\mathrm{H}_{d+1}$及$AdS_2$中仅存在单个孤立子解。在$AdS_2$中得到了一个具有多项式势的标量场论的变形kink解。该变形与平直空间中超对称正弦-戈登理论的玻色部分高度相似。在无限半径极限下，单个孤立子退化为标准的平直空间孤立子，某些$AdS_{d+1}$中的多孤立子构型退化为单一加速孤立子。然而，部分$AdS_{d+1}$中的多孤立子解无法取平直空间极限，表明弯曲时空中的确存在真正的非微扰效应。

Conclusion: The existence of infinitely many soliton-like solutions in $AdS_{d+1}$ ($d \geq 2$) reveals a rich non-perturbative structure in curved spacetime field theories. The absence of similar multiplicity in $dS_{d+1}$ and $\mathrm{H}_{d+1}$ suggests a strong dependence on the global geometry and causal structure. The resemblance to supersymmetric models hints at hidden integrability or symmetry in the deformed theory. The presence of multisoliton solutions without flat-space limits underscores the necessity of developing new analytical tools tailored for strongly curved backgrounds.

在$AdS_{d+1}$（$d \geq 2$）中存在无限多个类孤立子解，揭示了弯曲时空场论中丰富的非微扰结构。而在$dS_{d+1}$和$\mathrm{H}_{d+1}$中缺乏类似多重性，表明解的结构强烈依赖于全局几何和因果结构。该模型与超对称模型的相似性暗示变形理论中可能存在隐藏的可积性或对称性。那些没有平直空间极限的多孤立子解的存在，强调了发展适用于强弯曲背景的新解析工具的必要性。

Abstract: We find infinitely many soliton-like solutions in a deformation of the sine-Gordon theory in $(d+1)$-dimensional $AdS_{d+1}$ (anti-de Sitter) spacetime for $d \geq 2$, as well as single solitonic solutions in $dS_{d+1}$ (de Sitter) and $\mathrm{H}{d+1}$ (Lobachevsky) spaces for $d \geq 1$ and in $AdS_2$. We also find a deformation of the kink solution in scalar field theory with a polynomial potential in $AdS_2$. The deformation of the sine-Gordon theory strikingly resembles the bosonic part of the flat-space supersymmetric sine-Gordon theory. In the infinite radius limit, single soliton solutions reduce to solitons in flat space. Meanwhile, the multisoliton solution of $AdS{d+1}$, $d\geq 2$ for certain values of the parameters reduces in the same limit to a single soliton solution boosted in the normal direction. However, there are also multisoliton solutions in $AdS_{d+1}$, $d \geq 2$ that do not have a flat space limit.

</details>


### [29] [Limits to Computational Acceleration Imposed by Quantum Field Theory and Quantum Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00182)
*Leron Borsten,Hyungrok Kim*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper explores the limits of computation in curved spacetimes and shows that relativistic acceleration of computation is fundamentally bounded by quantum gravity and quantum field theory effects. Specifically, the rate of computational acceleration due to time dilation is limited by $\mathcal{O}(1)E$ e-folds per unit time: $(\ln\alpha)/\tau \lesssim E$. Similarly, the memory capacity is constrained analogously to the Bekenstein bound: $(\ln N)/D \lesssim E$, where $N$ is the number of memory states, $D$ is the length scale, and $E$ is the energy scale.

本文探讨了在弯曲时空中计算的极限，表明由于量子引力和弯曲时空中的量子场论效应，相对论性计算加速从根本上受到限制。具体而言，由于时间膨胀导致的计算加速速率被限制在每单位时间 $\mathcal{O}(1)E$ 个e-fold内：$(\ln\alpha)/\tau \lesssim E$。类似地，存储容量也受到类似于贝肯斯坦熵界的约束：$(\ln N)/D \lesssim E$，其中 $N$ 是存储状态数，$D$ 是长度尺度，$E$ 是能量尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: It has been suggested that curved spacetimes and exotic fields could enable otherwise impossible computations by exploiting relativistic effects like time dilation, potentially making undecidable problems (e.g., the halting problem) tractable. This challenges fundamental notions of computability and raises questions about the interplay between general relativity, quantum mechanics, and computation. The authors aim to investigate whether such schemes are physically viable or if they are prevented by deeper physical principles such as those from quantum gravity (e.g., swampland conjectures) and quantum field theory in curved spacetime.

有人提出，弯曲时空和奇异场可以通过利用时间膨胀等相对论效应，实现原本不可能的计算，甚至可能使不可判定问题（例如停机问题）变得可解。这挑战了可计算性的基本概念，并引发了关于广义相对论、量子力学与计算之间相互作用的疑问。作者旨在探究这些方案是否在物理上可行，或者是否会因更深层的物理原理（如来自量子引力的swampland猜想或弯曲时空中的量子场论）而被阻止。

Method: The authors analyze relativistic computation schemes using tools from quantum field theory in curved spacetime and constraints from quantum gravity, particularly the swampland conjectures. They model an observer and a computer system operating at energy scales up to $E$, subject to relativistic effects such as time dilation. By examining the maximum rate at which proper time can be dilated relative to coordinate time (i.e., $\alpha = \Delta\tau_\text{comp}/\Delta t$), they derive an upper bound on computational speedup. They also apply entropy bounds, specifically the Bekenstein bound, to constrain memory capacity in terms of spatial extent $D$ and energy $E$, drawing an analogy between time-resource and space-resource limits in computation.

作者使用弯曲时空中量子场论的工具以及来自量子引力（特别是swampland猜想）的约束来分析相对论性计算方案。他们建立了一个观测者和计算机系统模型，该系统在高达 $E$ 的能量尺度下运行，并受到时间膨胀等相对论效应的影响。通过研究固有时相对于坐标时的最大膨胀率（即 $\alpha = \Delta\tau_\text{comp}/\Delta t$），他们推导出计算加速的上限。此外，他们应用熵界——特别是贝肯斯坦界——将存储容量限制在空间尺度 $D$ 和能量 $E$ 的范围内，从而在计算的时间资源与空间资源限制之间建立类比。

Result: The key result is a universal bound on the rate of computational acceleration via relativistic effects: $(\ln\alpha)/\tau \lesssim E$, where $\alpha$ is the time dilation factor, $\tau$ is the proper time of the computer, and $E$ is the maximum energy scale accessible. This implies that no physical system can achieve super-exponential speedup in computation through spacetime geometry alone. Additionally, the memory capacity of a computer of size $D$ is bounded by $(\ln N)/D \lesssim E$, analogous to the Bekenstein entropy bound. These bounds arise naturally from QFT in curved space and quantum gravity considerations, including the swampland distance conjecture.

主要结果是通过相对论效应进行计算加速的普适性限制：$(\ln\alpha)/\tau \lesssim E$，其中 $\alpha$ 是时间膨胀因子，$\tau$ 是计算机的固有时，$E$ 是可访问的最大能量尺度。这意味着没有任何物理系统能仅通过时空几何实现超指数级的计算加速。此外，大小为 $D$ 的计算机的存储容量受限于 $(\ln N)/D \lesssim E$，类似于贝肯斯坦熵界。这些界限自然地来自于弯曲空间中量子场论和量子引力的考虑，包括swampland距离猜想。

Conclusion: Physical laws, particularly those from quantum field theory in curved spacetime and quantum gravity (e.g., swampland conjectures), prevent the realization of hypercomputation through relativistic time dilation or exotic spacetime geometries. The derived bounds $(\ln\alpha)/\tau \lesssim E$ and $(\ln N)/D \lesssim E$ establish fundamental limits on both time and space resources for computation in any physically realizable system, reinforcing the idea that information processing is deeply tied to spacetime structure and energy scales.

弯曲时空中量子场论和量子引力（例如swampland猜想）的物理定律阻止了通过相对论时间膨胀或奇异时空几何实现超计算的可能性。所推导出的界限 $(\ln\alpha)/\tau \lesssim E$ 和 $(\ln N)/D \lesssim E$ 确立了任何物理可实现系统中计算时间和空间资源的根本限制，强化了信息处理与时空结构和能量尺度密切相关这一观点。

Abstract: A computer, in order to perform a given computation, requires a certain amount of space (memory) and a certain amount of time (runtime). This leaves certain computations beyond reach due to technological limits on processing speed and memory density. Some computations, such as the halting problem, are not possible even in principle. However, curved spacetimes and exotic fields appear to provide avenues to accelerate computation, for instance by exploiting time dilation. Impossible computations seemingly become tractable, butting up against intuition. However, we show that such schemes are consistently thwarted by physical effects from quantum gravity (including swampland conjectures) and quantum field theory in curved space. More precisely, we show that an observer and a computer able to withstand energy scales up to order $E$ can, by using relativistic effects, accelerate computation at a rate of at most $\mathcal O(1)E$ e-folds per unit time in natural units: $(\lnα)/τ\lesssim E$. The Bekenstein bound for entropy can then be understood as the space (memory) analogue to (run)time: if a computer of length scale $D$, operating at energies up to order $E$, has access to $N$ different memory states, then $(\ln N)/D\lesssim E$.

</details>


### [30] [On Entropic Gravity from BFSS Matrix Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00193)
*Korin Aldam-Tajima,Vatche Sahakian*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper presents a numerical study of Matrix theory at strong coupling, reproducing the general relativistic force law between two static objects as an entropic force. By analyzing this force via an operator algebra for an external observer, the authors identify black hole horizons and propose a modified interior geometry, suggesting that the black hole interior is described by AdS space rather than Schwarzschild, supporting Verlinde's entropic gravity and the fuzzball paradigm.

本文通过数值方法研究强耦合下的Matrix理论，将两个静态物体之间的广义相对论性力定律再现为Matrix理论中的熵力。利用描述外部观测者测量两物体相对位置和动量的算符代数，作者识别出黑洞视界的位置，并提出视界内部的Schwarzschild时空需被修正。研究发现黑洞内部更可能由AdS空间描述，为Verlinde的熵引力假说和fuzzball范式提供了数值验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To test Verlinde's proposal of gravity as an entropic force and to explore the microscopic structure of black holes within Matrix theory, particularly the nature of spacetime inside the event horizon, which remains poorly understood in classical general relativity.

检验Verlinde关于引力作为熵力的假说，并在Matrix理论框架下探索黑洞的微观结构，特别是事件视界内部时空的本质，这在经典广义相对论中仍未得到充分理解。

Method: Numerical simulations of Matrix theory at strong coupling are performed for two static objects at a fixed separation. An operator algebra is constructed to model measurements by an external observer, allowing computation of entropic forces. The force law is analyzed to extract horizon locations and infer the internal geometry of the objects, comparing it with classical Schwarzschild and alternative geometries such as AdS.

在固定距离下对强耦合Matrix理论中的两个静态物体进行数值模拟。构建了算符代数以模拟外部观测者的测量，从而计算熵力。通过分析力定律提取物体的视界位置，并推断其内部几何结构，与经典的Schwarzschild时空及其他几何（如AdS）进行比较。

Result: The numerically computed entropic force matches the exact general relativistic force law. Horizon positions are identified from the force profile, and the data suggest that the spacetime inside the horizon deviates from Schwarzschild and is better described by an Anti-de Sitter (AdS) geometry. This provides evidence that black hole interiors are not singular but have a well-defined holographic structure.

数值计算得到的熵力与精确的广义相对论性力定律一致。从力的分布中识别出视界位置，数据表明视界内部的时空偏离Schwarzschild解，更符合反德西特（AdS）几何。这表明黑洞内部并非奇点，而是具有明确的全息结构。

Conclusion: The results provide numerical support for Verlinde's entropic gravity and the fuzzball paradigm, indicating that gravity can emerge from quantum information and entanglement in Matrix theory. Furthermore, the black hole interior is shown to be non-singular and described by AdS space, implying a resolution of the black hole singularity problem within this framework.

研究结果为Verlinde的熵引力和fuzzball范式提供了数值支持，表明引力可在Matrix理论中从量子信息与纠缠中涌现。此外，黑洞内部被证明是非奇异的，并由AdS空间描述，意味着在此框架下黑洞奇点问题得以解决。

Abstract: We study Matrix theory at strong coupling in a setting describing two static objects a fixed distance apart, using numerical techniques. We reproduce the exact general relativistic force law between the two objects as an entropic force in Matrix theory. This involves employing an operator algebra that represents an external observer measuring the relative positions and momenta of the two objects. We identify the location of the horizons of the objects from this entropic force and are led to a modification of the Schwarzschild spacetime inside the horizon. We find evidence that the inside of a black hole is instead to be described by AdS space. The conclusions constitute numerical validation of Verlinde's entropic gravity proposition and the fuzzball paradigm.

</details>


### [31] [Dark energy from string theory: an introductory review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25797)
*David Andriot*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This review discusses the challenges and attempts in deriving dark energy models, particularly de Sitter solutions and quintessence, from string theory, highlighting theoretical constraints, construction difficulties, and observational connections.

本文综述了从弦理论推导暗能量模型（特别是德西特解和第五元素）所面临的挑战与尝试，强调了理论约束、构造困难以及与观测数据的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand whether string theory can provide a theoretical foundation for dark energy—either as a cosmological constant (de Sitter space) or as a dynamical field (quintessence)—given its central role in cosmic acceleration and the lack of a first-principles derivation within quantum gravity.

动机是理解弦理论是否能为暗能量（作为宇宙学常数（德西特空间）或动力学场（第五元素））提供理论基础，鉴于其在宇宙加速中的核心作用以及在量子引力中缺乏第一性原理推导。



Method: The paper reviews theoretical constraints in string theory on obtaining de Sitter vacua and quintessence, including swampland conjectures and asymptotic bounds. It systematically analyzes various proposed de Sitter constructions (e.g., via fluxes, orientifolds, non-perturbative effects), identifying technical and conceptual obstacles. It also examines single-field exponential quintessence models derived from compactifications, discussing their consistency with observational data and matter coupling.

本文回顾了弦理论中获得德西特真空和第五元素的理论约束，包括沼泽地猜想和渐近边界。系统分析了各种提出的德西特构造方案（例如通过通量、定向折叠、非微扰效应），识别技术和概念上的障碍。还研究了从紧化导出的单场指数第五元素模型，讨论其与观测数据的一致性及与物质的耦合。



Result: No fully stable, controlled classical de Sitter solution has been conclusively established in string theory; most proposals face issues with moduli stabilization, tachyonic instabilities, or violation of energy conditions. Swampland conjectures suggest that exact de Sitter vacua may not exist, favoring quintessence with exponential potentials ($V(\phi) \sim e^{-\lambda \phi}$). Single-field models with $\lambda > 1$ in reduced Planck units are favored by both theory and observations, though embedding them consistently in string theory remains challenging.

目前尚未在弦理论中确立完全稳定且可控的经典德西特解；大多数提案面临模空间稳定化、快子不稳定性或违反能量条件等问题。沼泽地猜想表明精确的德西特真空可能不存在，更倾向于具有指数势（$V(\phi) \sim e^{-\lambda \phi}$）的第五元素。在约化普朗克单位下，$\lambda > 1$ 的单场模型受到理论和观测的共同支持，但将其一致嵌入弦理论仍具挑战性。



Conclusion: Deriving dark energy from string theory remains an open problem. While de Sitter constructions face severe theoretical obstacles, quintessence models with exponential potentials offer a more promising avenue, aligned with both swampland conjectures and current data. Further progress requires better understanding of quantum corrections, non-perturbative effects, and consistent matter couplings in string compactifications.

从弦理论推导暗能量仍是一个开放问题。尽管德西特构造面临严重理论障碍，但具有指数势的第五元素模型提供了更有希望的方向，符合沼泽地猜想和当前观测数据。进一步进展需要更好地理解弦紧化中的量子修正、非微扰效应和一致的物质耦合。

Abstract: Dark energy, the main constituent in our expanding universe, responsible for its acceleration, is currently observed at unprecedented precision by different experiments. While several cosmological models can fit this latest data, deriving some of them from string theory would provide a valuable theoretical prior, with information on the nature of dark energy. This article reviews the efforts towards such a derivation, namely the options from string theory to get a cosmological constant (a de Sitter solution) or a dynamical dark energy (via a quintessence model).
  After a brief historical perspective, we first review proven or conjectured constraints in getting dark energy from string theory, in classical or asymptotic regimes. Circumventing such obstructions, by changing regime or ansatz, one can try to construct a de Sitter solution: we present a long list of such attempts, and the difficulties encountered. Among them, we discuss in detail efforts towards classical de Sitter solutions. Then, we review quintessence from string theory, focusing on single-field exponential models. Related topics are discussed, including the coupling to matter, the comparison to observational data, and the absence of a cosmological event horizon.

Abstract: The IKKT matrix model arises at the extremal $p= -1$ limit of holographic dualities based on D$p$-brane geometries. ### [33] [Topological defect induced phase separation in a holographic system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00690)
*Zi-Qiang Zhao,Zhang-Yu Nie,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We study the coupling between symmetry breaking and phase separation in a holographic superfluid model with $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry, based on Einstein-Maxwell-scalar theory. By introducing higher-order scalar potential terms $\lambda\Psi^4$ and $\tau\Psi^6$, we engineer a rich phase structure. Through controlled initial spatial partitions, we identify kinks as triggering sites for phase separation, revealing a novel mechanism linking topological defects to nonequilibrium dynamics.

我们基于Einstein-Maxwell-标量理论，在具有$\mathbb{Z}_2$对称性的全息超流模型中研究对称性破缺与相分离的耦合动力学。通过引入高阶标量势项$\lambda\Psi^4$和$\tau\Psi^6$，构造了丰富的相结构。利用空间分域的初态设置，我们发现扭结（kinks）可作为相分离的触发位点，揭示了一种拓扑缺陷与非平衡动力学耦合的新机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In first-order phase transitions, understanding how symmetry breaking and phase separation dynamically couple remains a challenge, especially in strongly coupled systems where traditional perturbative methods fail. Holographic models offer a powerful framework to explore such nonequilibrium phenomena via the gauge/gravity duality. We aim to elucidate the role of topological defects—such as kinks—in initiating phase separation, which is poorly understood in the context of coupled order parameters.

在一级相变中，对称性破缺与相分离如何动态耦合仍是一个难题，尤其在强耦合系统中传统微扰方法失效。全息模型通过规范/引力对偶为研究此类非平衡现象提供了有力框架。我们旨在阐明拓扑缺陷（如扭结）在相分离启动中的作用，这在耦合序参量背景下尚不清晰。

Method: We construct a holographic superfluid model using the Einstein-Maxwell-scalar theory with $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry. The scalar potential includes higher-order nonlinear terms $\lambda\Psi^4$ and $\tau\Psi^6$, enabling a tunable first-order phase transition and rich phase structure. Numerical simulations of the coupled gravity-matter system are performed under quenches across the critical temperature. Initial states are prepared with spatially partitioned configurations to probe localized triggering effects. The dynamics of kink formation and phase separation are analyzed through real-time evolution of the scalar and gauge fields.

我们基于Einstein-Maxwell-标量理论构建具有$\mathbb{Z}_2$对称性的全息超流模型，标量势包含高阶非线性项$\lambda\Psi^4$和$\tau\Psi^6$，以实现可调的一级相变和丰富相结构。通过对临界温度的淬火，数值模拟引力-物质耦合系统的实时演化。初态采用空间分域构型以探测局域触发效应，并通过标量场与规范场的实时演化分析扭结形成与相分离的动力学。

Result: The inclusion of $\lambda\Psi^4$ and $\tau\Psi^6$ terms generates a first-order phase transition with coexisting phases. These kinks act as nucleation sites for domain growth, indicating a direct coupling between topological defect formation and phase separation dynamics. The process exhibits a clear spatiotemporal correlation between kink positions and the onset of phase separation.

引入$\lambda\Psi^4$和$\tau\Psi^6$项后，系统出现具共存相的一级相变。在淬火过程中，我们观察到相分离并非均匀发生，而是始于对称性破缺时形成的扭结类拓扑缺陷。这些扭结充当区域生长的成核位点，表明拓扑缺陷形成与相分离动力学之间存在直接耦合。该过程展现出扭结位置与相分离起始之间的显著时空关联。

Conclusion: We uncover a novel mechanism in which kinks serve as triggers for phase separation during a first-order quench, demonstrating a strong coupling between symmetry breaking and phase separation in a strongly coupled holographic system. This finding highlights the importance of topological defects in nonequilibrium structure formation and provides new insights into dynamical pattern generation in quantum many-body systems via holography.

我们发现了一种新机制：在一级淬火过程中，扭结可作为相分离的触发器，揭示了强耦合全息系统中对称性破缺与相分离之间的强耦合。该结果强调了拓扑缺陷在非平衡结构形成中的重要性，并通过全息方法为量子多体系统中动力学图样生成提供了新见解。

Abstract: We investigate the coupled dynamics of symmetry breaking and phase separation during quenches across the critical point in a first-order phase transition. Based on the Einstein-Maxwell-scalar theory, we construct a holographic superfluid model with $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry. By introducing higher-order nonlinear terms $λΨ^4$ and $τΨ^6$ into the scalar field potential, we realize a rich phase structure, which enables us to study the coupling effects between symmetry breaking and phase separation. Furthermore, by preparing initial conditions with well-defined spatial partitions, we discover a new triggering mechanism for the invasion phenomenon, namely that kinks serve as triggering sites for the phase separation process. This study reveals a novel coupling mechanism between topological defects and phase separation, enriches our understanding of nonequilibrium structure formation in strongly coupled systems.

### [34] [Tensionless hybrid strings in $\rm AdS_3\times S^3\times S^3\times S^1$: Free field realisation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00769)
*Vit Sriprachyakul*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We construct a Wakimoto-like free field realization of the Lie superalgebra ${\frak d}(2,1;\alpha)_1$ with exact current algebra (no gauging), compute its partition function, and show that, combined with ghost contributions, it reproduces the single-particle partition function of the symmetric orbifold theory ${\rm Sym}^N({\cal S'}_0^2)$ — consisting of 8 free fermions, one compact and one non-compact free boson. We also analyze DDF operators and BRST cohomology.

我们构建了李超代数 ${\frak d}(2,1;\alpha)_1$ 的Wakimoto型自由场实现，其 $\mathfrak{sl}(2,\mathbb{R})$ 子代数的水平为 $k=1$，且无需引入规范固定即精确实现流代数。计算该理论的配分函数，并结合鬼场贡献后，完整的在壳投影弦配分函数精确重现了对称轨道理论 ${\rm Sym}^N({\cal S'}_0^2)$ 的单粒子配分函数，即包含8个自由费米子、一个紧致和一个非紧致自由玻色子的系统。此外还讨论了DDF算符及BRST与物理态条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to find an exact free field realization of the superconformal algebra associated with ${\frak d}(2,1;\alpha)_1$, which plays a key role in AdS$_3$/CFT$_2$ dualities, particularly for strings on AdS$_3 \times {\cal S'}_0^2$. Existing constructions often require gauge fixing or do not realize the full current algebra exactly; this work aims to overcome that limitation.

动机是寻找与 ${\frak d}(2,1;\alpha)_1$ 相关的超共形代数的精确自由场实现，该代数在 AdS$_3$/CFT$_2$ 对偶（特别是 AdS$_3 \times {\cal S'}_0^2$ 上的弦理论）中起关键作用。现有构造常需规范固定或不能精确实现完整流代数，本文旨在克服这一限制。

Method: We develop a Wakimoto-like free field representation of ${\frak d}(2,1;\alpha)_1$ at level $k=1$, avoiding the need for gauging by appropriately choosing free fields (bosons and fermions) that realize the current algebra exactly. The partition function is computed using character formulas of the affine superalgebra. Ghost systems from string quantization are included, and the total on-shell projected partition function is compared to the single-particle spectrum of ${\rm Sym}^N({\cal S'}_0^2)$. DDF operators are constructed to map physical states, and BRST cohomology is analyzed to define the physical state conditions.

我们为水平 $k=1$ 的 ${\frak d}(2,1;\alpha)_1$ 构造Wakimoto型自由场表示，通过适当选取自由玻色子和费米子场，无需规范固定即可精确实现流代数。利用仿射超代数的特征公式计算配分函数，引入弦量子化中的鬼场系统，并将总在壳投影配分函数与 ${\rm Sym}^N({\cal S'}_0^2)$ 的单粒子谱进行比较。构造了DDF算符以映射物理态，并分析BRST上同调以确定物理态条件。

Result: An exact free field realization of ${\frak d}(2,1;\alpha)_1$ is achieved without gauging. Conclusion: This construction provides a fully explicit and exact free field realization of the ${\frak d}(2,1;\alpha)_1$ algebra at $k=1$, which successfully captures the physical content of the dual symmetric orbifold CFT. It offers a powerful framework for studying string theory on AdS$_3 \times {\cal S'}_0^2$ backgrounds via free field methods, with potential applications to higher-point functions and quantum corrections.

该构造提供了 $k=1$ 时 ${\frak d}(2,1;\alpha)_1$ 代数的一个完全显式且精确的自由场实现，成功捕获了对偶对称轨道CFT的物理内容。它为通过自由场方法研究 AdS$_3 \times {\cal S'}_0^2$ 背景上的弦理论提供了有力框架，有望应用于高点函数和量子修正的研究。

Abstract: We discuss a Wakimoto-like free field realisation of ${\frak d}(2,1;α)_1$, whose $\frak{sl}(2,\mathbb{R})$ subalgebra has level $k=1$, that requires no gauging, i.e., realises the current algebra exactly. We then compute the partition function of the theory and show that, by combining this with the ghost contribution, the full, on-shell projected string partition function reproduces precisely the single-particle partition function of the ${\rm Sym}^N({\cal S'}_0^2)$ theory, i.e. the symmetric orbifold theory of 8 free fermions, 1 compact free boson, and 1 non-compact free boson.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Expressed the superconformal index in terms of elliptic Macdonald polynomials labeled by generalized partitions, introduced structure constants $B_λ(p,q,t)$ and normalization constants $\mathcal{N}_λ(p,q,t)$, and solved the elliptic Ruijsenaars-Schneider model perturbatively in $p$ to obtain a power series expansion of the index.

Result: Derived a compact formula for the superconformal index involving sums over generalized partitions weighted by $B_λ$ and $\mathcal{N}_λ$, obtained a systematic expansion in powers of $p$, and verified consistency with known results in the deformed 1/2 BPS limit and large $N$ limit.

Conclusion: The elliptic Ruijsenaars-Schneider system provides a powerful framework for analyzing the superconformal index of $\mathcal{N}=4$ $U(N)$ SYM, revealing deep connections between supersymmetric gauge theories, integrable systems, and special functions like elliptic Macdonald polynomials.

### [36] [Excited solutions in a Skyrme--Chern-Simons model in $2+1$ dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01005)
*Francisco Navarro-Lérida,D. H. Tchrakian*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates excited solutions in a 2+1-dimensional Skyrme--Chern-Simons theory using a Lagrange multiplier method, which is necessary due to discontinuities in standard parametrizations; these excited states are labeled by an integer $p \neq 0$, and while their global charges exhibit non-standard behavior, the energy hierarchy remains unchanged, with $p=0$ (ground state) always being the lowest-energy configuration.

本文研究了在2+1维Skyrme--Chern-Simons理论中使用拉格朗日乘子法求解激发态的必要性，因为标准约束参数化会导致不连续性；这些激发态由整数$p \neq 0$标记。尽管全局荷表现出非标准行为，能量层级未发生显著改变，$p=0$（基态）始终具有最低能量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Excited solitonic solutions in field theories are often difficult to obtain due to numerical instabilities or singularities arising from constraint-preserving parametrizations. In this model, a discontinuity appears when attempting to construct such solutions without additional control, motivating the use of a Lagrange multiplier to properly enforce constraints and stabilize the variational procedure for $p \neq 0$ configurations.

在场论中，由于约束保持参数化引起的数值不稳定或奇异性，孤子激发态通常难以获得。在此模型中，尝试构造此类解时会出现不连续性，因此需要引入拉格朗日乘子来正确施加约束，并稳定$p \neq 0$构型的变分过程。

Method: The authors employ a Lagrange multiplier method to handle the nonlinear constraint inherent in the Skyrme--Chern-Simons model, allowing for smooth variation across field configurations. They solve the resulting Euler--Lagrange equations numerically, identifying solutions indexed by an excitation integer $p$. Global conserved charges such as energy and topological charge are computed as functions of model parameters, analyzing their dependence and stability.

作者采用拉格朗日乘子法处理Skyrme--Chern-Simons模型中的非线性约束，从而实现对场构型的平滑变分。他们数值求解得到的欧拉-拉格朗日方程，识别出由激发整数$p$索引的解，并将能量和拓扑荷等全局守恒量作为模型参数的函数进行计算，分析其依赖性和稳定性。

Result: Excited solutions ($p \neq 0$) are successfully obtained only when the Lagrange multiplier method is used, confirming its necessity. The global charges show non-trivial parameter dependence, deviating from conventional patterns. However, the Skyrme--Chern-Simons term does not significantly alter the energy level structure: the $p=0$ solution consistently has the lowest energy, indicating energetic stability of the ground state.

只有使用拉格朗日乘子法才能成功获得激发态解（$p \neq 0$），验证了该方法的必要性。全局荷表现出非平凡的参数依赖关系，偏离常规模式。然而，Skyrme--Chern-Simons项并未显著改变能级结构：$p=0$解始终具有最低能量，表明基态的能量稳定性。

Conclusion: The Lagrange multiplier method is essential for obtaining regular excited solitons in this system. While new features in global charges emerge for $p \neq 0$, the fundamental solution ($p=0$) remains energetically favored, preserving the stability of the vacuum sector. This highlights the robustness of the ground state despite the presence of higher excitations.

拉格朗日乘子法对于在此系统中获得规则的激发孤子至关重要。尽管$p \neq 0$时全局荷出现新特征，但基态解（$p=0$）在能量上仍占优，保持真空扇区的稳定性。这表明即使存在更高激发态，基态仍具有鲁棒性。

Abstract: We study excited solutions in a Skyrme--Chern-Simons theory in $2+1$ dimensions. In particular, we emphasize the necessity of using a Lagrange multiplier method to obtain excited solutions, due to the appearance of a discontinuity when using a constraint compliant parametrization. These solutions are characterized by an integer number $p$, excited solutions corresponding to $p\neq 0$. The dependence of the global charges on the parameters is analyzed, showing non-standard behaviors. We also find that the presence of the Skyrme--Chern-Simons term does not alter significantly the pattern of energy levels, so $p=0$ solutions (fundamental solutions) have always the minimal energy.

### [37] [Energy Correlators from Star Integrals via Mellin Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01071)
*Anastasia Volovich,Di Wu,Kai Yan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We develop a Mellin space representation for the collinear limit of $N$-point energy correlators in ${\cal N}=4$ super-Yang-Mills theory, expressing them as integro-differential operators acting on star integrals (one-loop $n$-gons in $n$ dimensions). For the three-point case, we connect the correlator to the massive box integral and solve the relation to reproduce known results. For the four-point case, we express it as a sum of box and hexagon integrals in special kinematics, establishing a systematic method to relate higher-point correlators to exactly known star integrals.

我们为${\cal N}=4$超规范理论中$N$点能量关联子的共线极限开发了Mellin空间表示，将其表达为作用于星积分（$n$维中的一圈$n$边形）上的积分微分算符。对于三点能量关联子，我们得到了其Mellin表示，将其与质量盒积分联系起来，并求解该关系以重现已知结果。对于四点情况，我们用Mellin表示将其写成特殊运动学下的盒和六边形积分之和，建立了将高点关联子系统性地关联到精确已知星积分的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Energy correlators in quantum field theories, especially in conformal theories like ${\cal N}=4$ super-Yang-Mills, provide valuable insights into dynamics and symmetries. The collinear limit simplifies their structure, making them amenable to exact analysis. However, extending such analyses beyond low-point correlators remains challenging. A systematic framework in Mellin space could unlock exact results for higher-point functions by leveraging the known exact forms of star integrals.

量子场论中的能量关联子，特别是在如${\cal N}=4$超规范理论这样的共形场论中，提供了对动力学和对称性的深刻理解。共线极限简化了它们的结构，使其适合精确分析。然而，将此类分析扩展到低点以上仍具挑战性。Mellin空间中的系统框架可以通过利用星积分的精确形式来揭示高点函数的精确结果。

Method: We employ Mellin space techniques to represent $N$-point energy correlators in the collinear limit. These are expressed as integro-differential operators acting on star integrals—specifically one-loop $n$-gon diagrams in $n$ dimensions. For the three-point correlator, we derive its Mellin representation and establish a differential relation to the massive box integral, which we then solve analytically. For the four-point correlator, we construct the Mellin representation and decompose it into combinations of box and hexagon integrals under special kinematic configurations.

我们在共线极限下使用Mellin空间技术表示$N$点能量关联子，将其表达为作用于星积分（具体为$n$维中的一圈$n$边形图）上的积分微分算符。对于三点关联子，我们推导其Mellin表示，并建立其与质量盒积分的微分关系，然后进行解析求解。对于四点关联子，我们构建Mellin表示，并在特殊运动学配置下将其分解为盒和六边形积分的组合。

Result: We obtain the exact Mellin space representation of the three-point energy correlator and show that it satisfies a differential equation relating it to the massive box integral; solving this yields agreement with known results. For the four-point energy correlator, we derive its Mellin representation and express it as a sum of box and hexagon integrals in special kinematics. The general structure reveals a pattern that allows extension to higher-point correlators via star integrals.

我们获得了三点能量关联子的精确Mellin空间表示，并证明其满足一个将其与质量盒积分关联的微分方程；求解该方程与已知结果一致。对于四点能量关联子，我们推导出其Mellin表示，并在特殊运动学下将其表示为盒和六边形积分之和。一般结构揭示了一种模式，允许通过星积分将该方法推广至高点关联子。

Conclusion: The Mellin space representation provides a powerful framework for analyzing energy correlators in the collinear limit of ${\cal N}=4$ super-Yang-Mills. By expressing them as integro-differential operators on star integrals, we establish a systematic and exact method applicable to arbitrary $N$-point functions. This opens a new pathway to all-orders results using known properties of loop integrals in Mellin space.

Mellin空间表示为分析${\cal N}=4$超规范理论共线极限下的能量关联子提供了一个强大框架。通过将它们表示为作用于星积分上的积分微分算符，我们建立了一种适用于任意$N$点函数的系统且精确的方法。这开辟了一条利用Mellin空间中圈积分已知性质获得全阶结果的新途径。

Abstract: We explore the Mellin space representation for the collinear limit of $N$-point energy correlators in ${\cal N}=4$ super-Yang-Mills theory. We show that these correlators can be written as integro-differential operators acting on star integrals: one-loop $n$-gons in $n$ dimensions. For the three-point energy correlator, we obtain the Mellin representation, use it to relate the correlator to the massive box integral, and show how to solve this relation to match with the expected result. For the four-point energy correlator, we obtain the Mellin representation and use it to write the correlator to a sum of various box and hexagon integrals in special kinematics. Our results provide a systematic method to relate higher-point energy correlators in the collinear limit to star integrals, which are known exactly.

</details>


### [38] [Cosmological Wavefunctions as Amplitudes: Dual Shuffle Factorization and Uniqueness from New Hidden Zeros](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01133)
*Yang Li,Laurentiu Rodina*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper establishes a deep connection between cosmological wavefunctions in $\phi^n$ theories and flat-space scattering amplitudes, showing that wavefunction coefficients map to on-shell amplitude-like objects $\mathcal{A}_G$ via a transformation from tube variables to Mandelstam invariants. A new graph-based zero structure leads to a dual factorization principle—distinct from unitarity—that governs how wavefunctions factorize when momenta between subgraphs vanish. This dual factorization, expressed as $\mathcal{A}_G = \mathcal{A}_{G_L}\unicode{x29E2}\mathcal{A}_{G_R}$, combined with locality and hidden zeros, fully fixes tree-level wavefunctions without invoking unitarity. These zeros are linked to enhanced BCFW shift behavior, extending the zeros--BCFW correspondence to cosmology and revealing new structures in both cosmological and flat-space amplitudes.

该论文建立了 $\phi^n$ 理论中宇宙学波函数与平直空间散射振幅之间的深刻联系，表明通过将管变量映射到Mandelstam不变量，波函数系数可转化为类似振幅的在壳对象 $\mathcal{A}_G$。基于图的新零点结构引出了一个对偶因子化原理——不同于幺正性，当子图间动量消失时波函数发生因子化，表达为 $\mathcal{A}_G = \mathcal{A}_{G_L}\unicode{x29E2}\mathcal{A}_{G_R}$。结合局域性和隐藏零点，无需幺正性即可唯一确定树层级波函数。这些零点对应于BCFW移位下的增强大$z$行为，将零点-BCFW对应关系推广至宇宙学，并揭示了平直空间振幅中的新结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent advances in understanding scattering amplitudes have revealed powerful on-shell methods relying on symmetry, analyticity, and factorization. In cosmology, similar principles may govern the structure of wavefunctions of the universe, especially in simplified models like $\phi^n$ theories. However, a systematic framework linking cosmological observables to amplitude-like constructs is lacking. The authors aim to bridge this gap by showing how cosmological wavefunctions can be mapped to on-shell objects analogous to scattering amplitudes, uncovering new symmetries and constraints—such as hidden zeros and dual factorization—that could replace traditional assumptions like unitarity in fixing physical predictions.

近年来散射振幅的研究揭示了依赖于对称性、解析性和因子化的强大在壳方法。在宇宙学中，类似的原理可能支配宇宙波函数的结构，尤其是在 $\phi^n$ 等简化模型中。然而，目前尚缺乏将宇宙学观测量系统地连接到类振幅构造的框架。作者旨在通过展示宇宙学波函数如何映射到类似于散射振幅的在壳对象来弥合这一差距，并发现新的对称性和约束——如隐藏零点和对偶因子化——这些可能取代幺正性等传统假设以确定物理预言。

Method: The authors introduce a map from 'tube variables' in cosmological wavefunctions to Mandelstam invariants used in scattering amplitudes, enabling a direct identification of wavefunction coefficients $\psi_{\mathcal{G}}$ with amplitude-like objects $\mathcal{A}_G$. They analyze the graph-theoretic structure of these objects, identifying new 'graph-based hidden zeros' where $\mathcal{A}_G$ vanishes when $p_a \cdot p_b = 0$ for particles in disconnected subgraphs. They formulate a dual factorization principle: when such a zero occurs, the generating graph factorizes as $G \to G_L \times G_R$, and the amplitude satisfies a shuffle decomposition $\mathcal{A}_G = \mathcal{A}_{G_L} \unicode{x29E2} \mathcal{A}_{G_R}$. Using this structure, they prove that locality and the full set of hidden zeros uniquely fix tree-level wavefunctions without assuming unitarity. They also connect these zeros to enhanced behavior under BCFW shifts, generalizing the known zeros--BCFW correspondence.

作者引入了一种从宇宙学波函数中的“管变量”到散射振幅中使用的Mandelstam不变量的映射，使得波函数系数 $\psi_{\mathcal{G}}$ 可直接识别为类振幅对象 $\mathcal{A}_G$。他们分析了这些对象的图论结构，发现了新的“基于图的隐藏零点”，即当不连通子图中的粒子满足 $p_a \cdot p_b = 0$ 时 $\mathcal{A}_G$ 消失。他们提出了一个对偶因子化原理：当出现此类零点时，生成图分解为 $G \to G_L \times G_R$，且振幅满足shuffle分解 $\mathcal{A}_G = \mathcal{A}_{G_L} \unicode{x29E2} \mathcal{A}_{G_R}$。利用此结构，他们证明局域性与全部隐藏零点可唯一确定树层级波函数而无需假设幺正性。他们还将这些零点与BCFW移位下的增强行为联系起来，推广了已知的零点-BCFW对应关系。

Result: 1. Wavefunction coefficients in $\phi^n$ theories are mapped to on-shell amplitude-like objects $\mathcal{A}_G$ through a tube-to-Mandelstam map.
2. At tree level, $\mathcal{A}_G$ coincides with the Cachazo-He-Yuan (CHY) construction based on Cayley functions, generalizing Parke-Taylor factors.
3. New 'graph-based hidden zeros' are discovered, unifying all previously known cosmological zeros.
4. A dual factorization principle is established: zeros at $p_{a\in G_L}\!\cdot\! p_{b\in G_R}=0$ induce graph factorization $G \to G_L \times G_R$ and imply shuffle decomposition $\mathcal{A}_G = \mathcal{A}_{G_L} \unicode{x29E2} \mathcal{A}_{G_R}$.
5. Near-zero factorization emerges naturally from this structure.
6. Locality plus hidden zeros uniquely fix tree-level cosmological wavefunctions without requiring unitarity.
7. These zeros correspond to enhanced large-$z$ suppression under BCFW shifts, extending the zeros--BCFW correspondence to cosmological settings.
8. Evidence suggests the zero structure and uniqueness extend to loop level.

1. $\phi^n$ 理论中的波函数系数通过管变量到Mandelstam的映射被转化为在壳类振幅对象 $\mathcal{A}_G$。
2. 在树层级，$\mathcal{A}_G$ 与基于Cayley函数的Cachazo-He-Yuan (CHY) 构造一致，推广了Parke-Taylor因子。
3. 发现了新的“基于图的隐藏零点”，统一了所有已知的宇宙学零点。
4. 建立了对偶因子化原理：当 $p_{a\in G_L}\!\cdot\! p_{b\in G_R}=0$ 时的零点导致图分解 $G \to G_L \times G_R$，并意味着shuffle分解 $\mathcal{A}_G = \mathcal{A}_{G_L} \unicode{x29E2} \mathcal{A}_{G_R}$。
5. 近零因子化自然地从此结构中产生。
6. 局域性与隐藏零点共同唯一确定树层级宇宙学波函数，无需幺正性假设。
7. 这些零点对应于BCFW移位下增强的大-$z$ 压制，将零点-BCFW对应推广至宇宙学背景。
8. 有证据表明该零点结构与唯一性可延伸至圈层级。

Conclusion: The paper demonstrates that cosmological wavefunctions in $\phi^n$ theories exhibit rich on-shell structure analogous to scattering amplitudes, governed by graph-based hidden zeros and a novel dual factorization principle. This structure allows the complete determination of tree-level wavefunctions from locality and zero conditions alone, bypassing the need for unitarity. The results suggest that cosmology not only inherits structures from flat-space quantum field theory but also enriches them, offering a fertile ground for applying and discovering new on-shell methods. Moreover, insights gained from cosmology feed back into flat-space physics, revealing previously unknown aspects of amplitude structure.

本文表明，$\phi^n$ 理论中的宇宙学波函数展现出类似于散射振幅的丰富在壳结构，由基于图的隐藏零点和新颖的对偶因子化原理论所支配。该结构允许仅从局域性和零点条件完全确定树层级波函数，绕过了幺正性的需求。结果表明，宇宙学不仅继承了平直空间量子场论的结构，还对其进行了丰富，为应用和发现新的在壳方法提供了肥沃土壤。此外，从宇宙学获得的洞见反过来推动了平直空间物理的发展，揭示了振幅结构中此前未知的方面。

Abstract: We show that cosmological wavefunctions in $φ^n$ theories naturally generalize flat-space $\mathrm{Tr}(φ^3)$ scattering amplitudes: via a simple map from tube variables to Mandelstam invariants, each wavefunction coefficient $ψ_{\mathcal{G}}$ becomes an on-shell amplitude-like object $\mathcal{A}_G$ associated with a generating graph $G$. At tree level these objects coincide with the Cachazo-He-Yuan construction based on Cayley functions that generalizes Parke-Taylor factors. We uncover new graph-based hidden zeros that extend and unify all known cosmological zeros. Based on this zero structure, we uncover a factorization principle dual to unitarity. Instead of factorization across poles, $A\to A_L\times A_R$, a zero at $p_{a\in G_L}\!\cdot\! p_{b\in G_R}=0$ factorizes the generating graph, $G\to G_L\times G_R$, and is equivalent to the shuffle decomposition $\mathcal{A}_G=\mathcal{A}_{G_L}\unicode{x29E2}\mathcal{A}_{G_R}$. Near-zero factorization is a simple consequence of this new structure. Using dual factorization, we show that locality together with the full set of hidden zeros uniquely fixes tree-level cosmological wavefunctions without assuming unitarity. We show that these zeros are equivalent to special enhanced large-$z$ behavior under Britto-Cachazo-Feng-Witten (BCFW) shifts, extending the zeros--BCFW correspondence beyond flat-space amplitudes. We also find evidence for further extensions of the zero structure and loop-level uniqueness. Our results show that cosmology provides a natural arena for on-shell methods and even reveals new structure in flat-space amplitudes.
