### [39] [Infinite Heat Order in 3+1 Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01184)
*Borut Bajc,Giulia Muco,Francesco Sannino,Sophie Wagner*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates whether spontaneous symmetry breaking can persist at arbitrarily high temperatures in UV-complete 4D quantum field theories, focusing on asymptotically free $\mathrm{SU}(N_{c1})\times \mathrm{SU}(N_{c2})$ models with two scalars and a negative portal coupling. By extending previous large-$N$ results to finite $N$, the authors derive finite-$N$ fixed-flow equations, compute $1/N$ corrections, and numerically solve the system. They find explicit finite-$N$ theories where the potential is bounded from below, asymptotic freedom holds, and one scalar retains a negative thermal mass at all temperatures—realizing infinite heat order perturbatively.

该论文研究在四维紫外完备的量子场论中，自发对称性破缺是否能在任意高温下持续存在。作者聚焦于具有两个标量场和负门户耦合的渐近自由$\mathrm{SU}(N_{c1})\times \mathrm{SU}(N_{c2})$模型，将此前大$N$极限下的结果推广到有限色数情形。他们推导了有限$N$下的固定流方程，计算了领先的$1/N$修正，并数值求解了完整系统，找到了满足有界势、渐近自由且标量热质量始终为负的具体理论实例，实现了有限场内容下可微扰处理的无限热序现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: It is generally expected that symmetries broken at low energies are restored at sufficiently high temperatures. However, certain theoretical frameworks suggest that under special conditions—such as strong coupling or specific scalar interactions—symmetry non-restoration or even symmetry non-restoration at infinite temperature (infinite heat order) may occur. The motivation is to determine whether such phenomena can arise in controllable, ultraviolet-complete, and perturbative four-dimensional quantum field theories without relying on large-$N$ limits, thus assessing their viability beyond approximations.

通常认为在足够高的温度下，低温时破缺的对称性会被恢复。然而某些理论框架表明，在强耦合或特定标量相互作用等特殊条件下，可能存在对称性不恢复甚至在无限温度下仍保持破缺（即无限热序）。本文动机在于：探究这类现象是否能在可控、紫外完备且可微扰的四维量子场论中实现，而不依赖大$N$极限，从而评估其在超越近似方案后的实际可行性。

Method: The authors consider $\mathrm{SU}(N_{c1}) \times \mathrm{SU}(N_{c2})$ gauge theories with two complex scalars, each charged under one gauge group and singlet under the other, coupled via a negative quartic portal. They analyze the renormalization group (RG) flow of couplings at finite $N_{ci}$ and $N_f$, deriving finite-$N$ fixed-flow equations that generalize the large-$N$ Veneziano limit. They compute leading $1/N$ corrections analytically and perform full numerical solutions of the RG equations to identify trajectories where one scalar develops a negative thermal mass at all temperatures. Boundedness of the scalar potential and asymptotic freedom are imposed as physical constraints.

作者研究了$\mathrm{SU}(N_{c1}) \times \mathrm{SU}(N_{c2})$规范理论，包含两个复标量场，每个场分别在一个规范群下为基本表示而在另一个下为单态，通过负四次门户耦合连接。他们在有限$N_{ci}$和$N_f$下分析耦合常数的重整化群（RG）流动，推导出有限$N$下的固定流方程，推广了大$N$ Veneziano极限的结果。通过解析计算领先的$1/N$修正并数值求解完整的RG方程，寻找使某一标量在所有温度下均具有负热质量的轨迹。同时施加标量势有界性和渐近自由作为物理约束条件。

Result: Explicit finite-$N$ theories are found where: (i) the scalar potential is bounded from below, (ii) the gauge sector remains asymptotically free, and (iii) one scalar field acquires a negative thermal mass that persists at arbitrarily high temperatures. These results go beyond the large-$N$ approximation and demonstrate the existence of fixed-flow trajectories in fully resummed perturbation theory. This constitutes a perturbative realization of infinite heat order in a four-dimensional, ultraviolet-complete QFT with finite field content.

发现了具体的有限$N$理论，满足：(i) 标量势下方有界；(ii) 规范部门保持渐近自由；(iii) 某一标量场获得并在任意高温下维持负热质量。这些结果超越了大$N$近似，在完全重求和的微扰理论中展示了固定流轨迹的存在性。这构成了在四维、紫外完备、有限场内容的量子场论中可微扰实现无限热序的首个明确例子。

Conclusion: Spontaneous symmetry breaking can persist into the infinite-temperature limit in certain perturbative, ultraviolet-complete four-dimensional quantum field theories. The mechanism relies on a negative portal coupling and precise RG running that maintains a negative thermal mass for one scalar field. This work establishes the first concrete example of infinite heat order in a finite-$N$, finite-field-content QFT, demonstrating that symmetry non-restoration can occur in controlled, weakly-coupled settings without invoking large-$N$ limits or non-perturbative assumptions.

在某些可微扰且紫外完备的四维量子场论中，自发对称性破缺可以延续至无限温度极限。该机制依赖于负门户耦合并通过精确的RG运行维持一个标量场的负热质量。本工作建立了在有限$N$、有限场内容的QFT中无限热序的首个具体实例，证明对称性不恢复可在无需大$N$极限或非微扰假设的弱耦合可控环境中发生。

Abstract: We investigate whether spontaneous symmetry breaking can persist up to arbitrarily high temperature in ultraviolet-complete quantum field theories in four spacetime dimensions. We focus on completely asymptotically free models with gauge group $\mathrm{SU}(N_{c1})\times \mathrm{SU}(N_{c2})$ and two complex scalar fields, each transforming in the fundamental representation of one gauge factor and singlet under the other. The scalar potential contains quartic self-interactions together with a negative portal coupling between the two sectors. In the Veneziano limit, this class of theories was previously shown to admit fixed-flow trajectories for which one scalar acquires a negative thermal mass at asymptotically large temperature, leading to symmetry non-restoration. Here we extend that analysis to finite numbers of colours and flavours. We derive the finite-$N$ fixed-flow equations, compute the leading $1/N$ corrections to the large-$N$ solutions, and solve the full finite-$N$ system numerically. We find explicit finite-$N$ benchmark theories for which the scalar potential remains bounded from below, the gauge sector is asymptotically free, and one scalar thermal mass stays negative at arbitrarily high temperature. This provides an explicit perturbative example of infinite heat order in a four-dimensional ultraviolet-complete quantum field theory with a finite field content.

</details>


### [40] [On Generalised Discrete Torsion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01225)
*Philip Boyle Smith,Yuji Tachikawa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: A generalization of discrete torsion in 2d gauged sigma models with discrete gauge group $G$ is proposed, where local discrete torsion phases are assigned to singular loci of the orbifold $M/G$ via $H^2_G(M; U(1))$. This framework consistently implements Gaberdiel-Kaste's prescription at higher genus and determines resulting smooth Calabi-Yau and $G_2$ geometries for $T^6/\mathbb{Z}_2^2$ and $T^7/\mathbb{Z}_2^3$, revealing constrained Betti numbers in $G_2$ resolutions.

提出了一种在具有离散规范群 $G$ 的二维规范sigma模型中推广离散扭转的方案，通过 $H^2_G(M; U(1))$ 为轨道簇 $M/G$ 的不同奇点赋予局部离散扭转相。该框架在高属曲面上一致实现了Gaberdiel-Kaste的手动插入方法，并确定了 $T^6/\mathbb{Z}_2^2$ 和 $T^7/\mathbb{Z}_2^3$ 轨道共形场论所对应的光滑Calabi-Yau与$G_2$几何结构，揭示了$G_2$消解中Betti数的受限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Vafa's original discrete torsion $H^2(BG; U(1))$ assigns a single global phase to the entire orbifold theory, but cannot account for spatially varying torsion effects at different singular loci. The motivation is to generalize this to allow position-dependent discrete torsion phases in a way that remains consistent under modular transformations and higher-genus amplitudes, particularly for applications to string compactifications on $T^6/\mathbb{Z}_2^2$ and $T^7/\mathbb{Z}_2^3$ orbifolds.

Vafa提出的原始离散扭转 $H^2(BG; U(1))$ 仅为整个轨道理论分配一个全局相位，无法描述不同奇点处的空间变化扭转效应。本文旨在推广这一概念，允许位置依赖的离散扭转相，并在模变换和高属振幅下保持一致性，尤其适用于 $T^6/\mathbb{Z}_2^2$ 与 $T^7/\mathbb{Z}_2^3$ 轨道上的弦紧化应用。

Method: The authors use equivariant cohomology $H^2_G(M; U(1))$ to classify generalized discrete torsion, which naturally incorporates the geometry of the target space $M$ and its $G$-action. They apply this to orbifold CFTs by assigning distinct local $U(1)$ phases to twisted sectors associated with fixed loci, ensuring consistency via the cocycle condition in equivariant cohomology. The formalism is tested on $T^6/\mathbb{Z}_2^2$ and $T^7/\mathbb{Z}_2^3$, computing the resulting topological data (e.g., Betti numbers) of desingularized Calabi-Yau and $G_2$ manifolds.

作者使用等变上同调 $H^2_G(M; U(1))$ 对广义离散扭转进行分类，自然地结合了目标空间 $M$ 及其 $G$-作用的几何结构。他们通过为与固定轨迹相关的扭 sector 分配不同的局部 $U(1)$ 相位来应用于轨道共形场论，并利用等变上同调中的上循环条件保证一致性。该形式体系被应用于 $T^6/\mathbb{Z}_2^2$ 与 $T^7/\mathbb{Z}_2^3$ 案例，计算消奇异后Calabi-Yau和$G_2$流形的拓扑数据（如Betti数）。


Result: Generalized discrete torsion in $H^2_G(M; U(1))$ allows distinct local phases at different singular loci while maintaining consistency in higher-genus amplitudes. For $T^6/\mathbb{Z}_2^2$, different choices yield known Calabi-Yau threefolds. For $T^7/\mathbb{Z}_2^3$, the resulting $G_2$ holonomy manifolds have Betti numbers that are not fully independent: only 3 out of 9 possible Betti number configurations predicted by Joyce's construction are realized by the orbifold CFTs.

广义离散扭转 $H^2_G(M; U(1))$ 允许在不同奇点处设置不同的局部相位，同时保持高属振幅的一致性。对于 $T^6/\mathbb{Z}_2^2$，不同选择可得到已知的Calabi-Yau三维流形；而对于 $T^7/\mathbb{Z}_2^3$，所得具有 $G_2$ 和乐性的流形其Betti数并非完全独立——Joyce构造预测的9种可能Betti数组合中，仅有3种能由轨道共形场论实现。

Conclusion: The generalized discrete torsion in $H^2_G(M; U(1))$ provides a physically consistent and mathematically natural extension of Vafa's discrete torsion, enabling spatially varying torsion phases in orbifold CFTs. However, it imposes nontrivial constraints on the topology of resolved geometries, indicating that not all geometric possibilities from mathematical constructions (e.g., Joyce's $G_2$ resolutions) can be realized in string-derived orbifold theories.

$H^2_G(M; U(1))$ 中的广义离散扭转为Vafa的离散扭转提供了物理上自洽且数学上自然的推广，使得轨道共形场论中可存在空间变化的扭转相。然而，它对消奇后的几何拓扑施加了非平庸限制，表明并非所有数学构造（如Joyce的 $G_2$ 消解）中的几何可能性都能在弦论导出的轨道理论中实现。

Abstract: For a 2d gauged sigma model with target space $M$ and discrete gauge group $G$, we consider a generalisation of Vafa's discrete torsion $H^2(BG; U(1))$ that assigns different local discrete torsion phases to different singular loci of the orbifold $M/G$. Our generalised discrete torsion lives in $H^2_G(M; U(1))$, and gives a consistent implementation of Gaberdiel and Kaste's prescription for inserting such local discrete torsion phases by hand at higher genus. We revisit the original application to $T^6/\mathbb{Z}_2^2$ and $T^7/\mathbb{Z}_2^3$ orbifold CFTs, and determine what smooth Calabi-Yau and $G_2$ geometries result from different choices of the generalised discrete torsion. We find that the local discrete torsion phases can be different from each other, but are not completely independent either; in the $T^7/\mathbb{Z}_2^3$ case for example, the orbifold CFTs only realise 3 out of the 9 possible Betti numbers of $G_2$ resolutions constructed by Joyce.

</details>

### [41] [Non-Cold Dark Matter from Memory-Burdened Primordial Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00090)
*Valentin Thoss,Laura Lopez-Honorez,Florian Kühnel,Marco Hufnagel*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper investigates how the memory-burden effect—delaying the full evaporation of primordial black holes (PBHs)—impacts the production and constraints of non-cold dark matter (NCDM) particles, particularly via Lyman-$\alpha$ forest data. By modeling PBH evaporation in two phases (semi-classical and memory-burden dominated), the authors compute NCDM phase-space distributions using \texttt{BlackHawk} and \texttt{CLASS}, finding distinct velocity dispersions that affect the matter power spectrum. They reinterpret thermal warm dark matter bounds to constrain mixed dark matter scenarios and map out viable parameter space in terms of particle mass, PBH initial conditions, and memory effects.

本文研究了“记忆负担效应”（延迟原初黑洞完全蒸发）如何影响非冷暗物质（NCDM）粒子的产生及其通过莱曼-α森林数据的限制。通过将PBH蒸发建模为两个阶段（半经典和记忆负担主导），作者使用\texttt{BlackHawk}和\texttt{CLASS}计算了NCDM的相空间分布，发现不同的速度弥散会影响物质功率谱。他们重新解释了热温暗物质的限制，以约束混合暗物质情景，并绘制出关于粒子质量、PBH初始条件和记忆效应的可行参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Primordial black holes (PBHs) are a compelling candidate for early-universe physics and can source non-cold dark matter (NCDM) through Hawking radiation during evaporation. However, if evaporation is delayed by quantum memory effects (the so-called 'memory burden'), the resulting NCDM has modified kinematic properties, which can weaken or alter existing cosmological bounds such as those from the Lyman-$\alpha$ forest. Understanding how this mechanism changes the phase-space distribution of dark matter is crucial for correctly interpreting observational constraints, especially when NCDM constitutes only a fraction of the total dark matter.

原初黑洞（PBHs）是早期宇宙物理的有力候选者，可通过霍金辐射在蒸发过程中产生非冷暗物质（NCDM）。然而，如果由于量子记忆效应（即“记忆负担”）导致蒸发被延迟，则所产生的NCDM具有改变的动力学特性，可能削弱或改变现有的宇宙学限制（如莱曼-α森林的限制）。理解该机制如何改变暗物质的相空间分布，对于正确解释观测限制至关重要，尤其是在NCDM仅占总暗物质一部分的情况下。

Method: The authors model PBH evaporation in two stages: an initial semi-classical Hawking phase followed by a memory-burden-dominated phase that delays complete evaporation. Using the \texttt{BlackHawk} code, they compute the energy spectra and abundance of emitted NCDM particles. The resulting phase-space distribution function $f(p)$ is then interfaced with the \texttt{CLASS} Boltzmann solver to compute modifications to the linear matter power spectrum. They derive constraints from Lyman-$\alpha$ data by mapping the NCDM scenario onto an effective thermal warm dark matter model with equivalent free-streaming scale, and also perform a direct comparison of suppressed power at small scales. This allows them to set limits on both dominant and subdominant NCDM components.

作者将PBH蒸发建模为两个阶段：初始的半经典霍金相，随后是记忆负担主导的相，后者延迟了完全蒸发。使用\texttt{BlackHawk}代码，他们计算了发射出的NCDM粒子的能量谱和丰度。然后将得到的相空间分布函数$f(p)$与\texttt{CLASS}玻尔兹曼求解器结合，计算线性物质功率谱的修正。他们通过将NCDM情景映射到具有等效自由流尺度的有效热温暗物质模型上，从莱曼-α数据推导出限制，并直接比较小尺度上抑制的功率。这使他们能够对主导和次主导的NCDM组分设定限制。

Result: The study finds that PBH evaporation with memory burden produces two distinct populations of NCDM particles with different velocity dispersions, leading to a characteristic suppression in the matter power spectrum at small scales. Using \texttt{CLASS} and \texttt{BlackHawk}, they show that even subdominant NCDM components (e.g., $\Omega_{\rm NCDM}/\Omega_{\rm DM} \ll 1$) can be constrained by Lyman-$\alpha$ data, depending on particle mass and PBH initial mass function. The memory-burden effect softens the high-energy tail of emissions, weakening constraints compared to pure semi-classical evaporation. However, full dark matter realization via NCDM from PBHs is only possible if PBHs do not dominate the energy density of the early universe, consistent with previous results.

研究发现，带有记忆负担的PBH蒸发会产生两组速度弥散不同的NCDM粒子，导致小尺度物质功率谱出现特征性抑制。使用\texttt{CLASS}和\texttt{BlackHawk}，他们表明即使次主导的NCDM组分（例如$\Omega_{\rm NCDM}/\Omega_{\rm DM} \ll 1$）也能被莱曼-α数据限制，具体取决于粒子质量和PBH初始质量函数。记忆负担效应会软化辐射的高能尾部，相比纯半经典蒸发情况削弱了限制。然而，只有当PBH不主导早期宇宙能量密度时，才能通过来自PBH的NCDM实现全部暗物质，这与先前结果一致。

Conclusion: The memory-burden effect in primordial black hole evaporation modifies the phase-space distribution of non-cold dark matter, leading to observable imprints on the matter power spectrum. These imprints can be probed via Lyman-$\alpha$ forest data, allowing robust constraints even on subdominant NCDM components. The work highlights the importance of accurately modeling late-time evaporation physics for deriving cosmological bounds on dark matter candidates from PBHs. It confirms that NCDM from fully evaporated PBHs can account for all dark matter only in non-PBH-dominated cosmologies.

原初黑洞蒸发中的记忆负担效应会改变非冷暗物质的相空间分布，从而在物质功率谱上留下可观测印记。这些印记可通过莱曼-α森林数据探测，即使对次主导的NCDM组分也能施加稳健限制。本工作强调了为从PBH产生的暗物质候选者推导宇宙学限制时，精确建模晚期蒸发物理的重要性。它证实，仅在非PBH主导的宇宙学中，来自完全蒸发PBH的NCDM才能构成全部暗物质。

Abstract: Non-cold dark matter particles can arise from the evaporation of primordial black holes (PBHs). In this paper, we further investigate how the memory-burden effect, which delays the full evaporation of black holes, affects the Lyman-$α$ bound on such non-cold dark matter (NCDM) particles. We mainly focus on scenarios in which PBHs have fully evaporated by today, undergoing a semi-classical evaporation phase followed by a memory-burden dominated phase. In this framework, PBH evaporation generically leads to two distinct dark-matter populations with different velocity dispersions, which can imprint observable signatures on the matter power spectrum. We compute the resulting NCDM phase-space distribution and its impact on small-scale overdensities using the $\texttt{BlackHawk}$ and $\texttt{CLASS}$ codes. This is then used to reinterpret Lyman-$α$ forest constraints for thermal warm dark matter, deriving both a velocity-dispersion-based and a matter-power-spectrum-based estimate. In particular, we discuss how we obtain constraints on scenarios in which NCDM particles constitute only a fraction of the total relic dark matter. Finally, we discuss the viable parameter space as a function of dark matter masses, PBH initial conditions, and memory-burden parameters. We show that even subdominant NCDM components from PBH evaporation can be constrained, and confirm that NCDM can only account for all of the dark matter in the absence of PBH domination, as in the semi-classical case.

</details>


### [42] [Lagrangian Bias as a Gaussian Random Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00097)
*Arka Banerjee*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We propose a new framework in which halo bias is not merely a set of perturbative coefficients but arises from a well-defined, scale-independent Lagrangian bias field inherent to every point in a Gaussian density field. This bias field is further extended via linear operators, forming secondary bias fields. Halos emerge through geometric selection of regions in this pre-existing field, offering an ab initio explanation for the $b(M)$ relation, the Gaussian scatter in bias at fixed mass, and assembly bias.

我们提出一种新框架，其中晕偏差不仅是微扰展开的系数，而是源自高斯密度场中每一点都具有的明确定义、尺度无关的拉格朗日偏差场。该偏差场可通过线性算符扩展形成次级偏差场。晕通过在此预先存在的场中几何选区形成，从而为$b(M)$关系、固定质量下偏差的高斯分布以及组装偏差提供了从头计算的解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional treatments of halo bias rely on perturbative expansions with bias coefficients fitted from simulations or observations. However, these approaches do not explain the origin of the bias or its statistical properties—such as the distribution of bias values at fixed halo mass (Gaussian scatter) and assembly bias. The motivation is to develop a more fundamental theory in which halo bias emerges from the structure of the initial Gaussian density field, rather than being imposed ad hoc after collapse.

传统晕偏差处理依赖于需从模拟或观测中拟合的微扰展开系数，但这些方法无法解释偏差的起源及其统计特性——例如固定晕质量下偏差值的分布（高斯散射）和组装偏差。动机是发展一种更基本的理论，使晕偏差源于初始高斯密度场的结构，而非在坍缩后人为设定。

Method: We consider the initial Lagrangian density field as a Gaussian random field. Using the fact that any point in such a field can be assigned a unique, scale-independent Lagrangian bias through conditional expectation, we define a bias field over all space. This construction is generalized to arbitrary linear operators acting on the field, generating secondary bias fields (e.g., tidal, Laplacian). Halo formation is modeled as a geometric selection—based on local density and other bias-related variables—within this multi-field setup, without invoking gravitational collapse dynamics explicitly. Predictions for $b(M)$ and bias statistics are derived analytically using the multivariate Gaussian statistics of the underlying fields.

我们将初始拉格朗日密度场视为高斯随机场。利用此类场中任意点均可通过条件期望赋予唯一、尺度无关的拉格朗日偏差的事实，我们在全空间定义偏差场。此构造可推广至作用于场的任意线性算符，生成次级偏差场（如潮汐、拉普拉斯）。晕形成被建模为在此多场设置中基于局部密度及其他偏差相关变量的几何选区，无需显式引入引力坍缩动力学。利用底层场的多元高斯统计性质，解析推导出$b(M)$及偏差统计量的预测。

Result: The framework successfully predicts the nonlinear $b(M)$ relation observed in simulations across a range of halo masses. It naturally explains why halo bias at fixed mass follows a Gaussian distribution: because it results from conditioning a multivariate Gaussian field on mass. Furthermore, known forms of assembly bias—such as age and spin dependence—are explained as correlations between the primary bias field and secondary bias fields (e.g., Laplacian or tidal fields). No free parameters beyond those in the initial power spectrum are introduced.

该框架成功预测了在不同晕质量范围内模拟中观测到的非线性$b(M)$关系。它自然解释了为何固定质量下的晕偏差呈高斯分布：这是由于对质量条件化的多元高斯场所致。此外，已知的组装偏差形式（如年龄和自旋依赖性）被解释为初级偏差场与次级偏差场（如拉普拉斯或潮汐场）之间的相关性。除初始功率谱中的参数外，未引入额外自由参数。

Conclusion: Halo bias originates from the geometry of the initial Gaussian density field and does not require generation during collapse. The bias field is an intrinsic property of the linear Lagrangian universe, and halos sample this field geometrically. This reframing provides a deeper theoretical foundation for bias and enables ab initio predictions of clustering, paving the way for combining this approach with physical models of halo formation for fully predictive cosmology.

晕偏差起源于初始高斯密度场的几何结构，无需在坍缩过程中产生。偏差场是线性拉格朗日宇宙的内在属性，晕通过几何方式采样该场。这一重构为偏差提供了更深的理论基础，并实现了对成团性的从头预测，为将此方法与晕形成物理模型结合以实现完全可预测的宇宙学铺平道路。

Abstract: Halo bias is typically treated as a set of coefficients in a perturbative expansion. We show instead that every point in a Gaussian density field has a well-defined scale-independent Lagrangian bias, thereby defining a bias field. This property can be extended to any linear operator acting on the Lagrangian density field, generating secondary bias fields. Halo bias then arises from geometric selection of Lagrangian patches within this pre-existing field, rather than being generated by collapse. We demonstrate that this framework predicts the measured $b(M)$ relation for halos. The multivariate Gaussian structure of the fields naturally explains the Gaussian distribution of halo bias at fixed mass and assembly bias. The results presented here motivate combining this framework with a forward model of halo collapse, yielding an ab initio model for halo clustering.

</details>


### [43] [Eppur non si trovano Vol. 2: No Planetary-mass Primordial Black Holes toward the Andromeda Galaxy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00111)
*Przemek Mróz,Andrzej Udalski*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The study reanalyzes twelve short-timescale microlensing candidates in M31 reported by Sugiyama et al. using an independent photometric pipeline and finds that all candidates are instead variable stars (ten RR Lyrae, one eclipsing binary, one unclassified), not microlensing events. Thus, there is no evidence for a large population of planetary-mass primordial black holes (PBHs) as dark matter.

该研究使用独立的测光管道重新分析了Sugiyama等人报告的M31中十二个短时标微引力透镜候选体，发现所有候选体均为变星（十个RR Lyrae星、一个食双星和一个未分类变星），而非微引力透镜事件。因此，没有证据支持行星质量原初黑洞（PBHs）作为暗物质的主要成分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The original claim by Sugiyama et al. of detecting numerous short-timescale microlensing events attributed to planetary-mass PBHs—potentially accounting for all dark matter—stands in strong tension with prior null results from surveys like OGLE toward the Magellanic Clouds. Additionally, the spatiotemporal distribution of the candidates appeared inconsistent with expected microlensing signatures, motivating an independent reanalysis to verify the astrophysical nature of these events.

Sugiyama等人声称探测到大量归因于行星质量原初黑洞（PBHs）的短时标微引力透镜事件，这些黑洞可能构成全部暗物质，但这一结论与OGLE等针对麦哲伦云的先前零结果存在强烈矛盾。此外，这些候选体的时空分布与预期的微引力透镜特征不符，促使我们进行独立的再分析以验证这些事件的真实天体物理性质。

Method: We perform an independent difference image analysis (DIA) of the Subaru Hyper Suprime-Cam data using a separate photometric pipeline. We examine the light curves of the twelve candidates for symmetry, timescale, and multi-night variability—key discriminants between true microlensing events and variable stars. We classify each candidate based on light curve morphology and temporal behavior, comparing against known variable star templates.

我们使用独立的测光管道对Subaru Hyper Suprime-Cam数据执行了独立的差分图像分析（DIA）。通过检查这十二个候选体的光变曲线对称性、时标和多晚变异性——这是区分真实微引力透镜事件与变星的关键判据，并根据光变曲线形态和时间行为对每个候选体进行分类，同时与已知变星模板进行比对。

Result: All twelve candidates show asymmetric light curves and/or variability across multiple nights, inconsistent with the achromatic, symmetric, single-epoch nature of microlensing. Ten are identified as RR Lyrae stars, one as an eclipsing binary, and one remains unclassified but clearly variable. No compelling microlensing event is found. The previously claimed signal for planetary-mass PBHs as dominant dark matter components is not supported.

所有十二个候选体均表现出不对称的光变曲线和/或多晚可变性，与微引力透镜的无色差、对称且单次发生的特性不一致。其中十个被识别为RR Lyrae星，一个为食双星，另一个虽未分类但明显是变星。未发现任何可信的微引力透镜事件。此前关于行星质量原初黑洞（PBHs）作为主导暗物质成分的信号未得到支持。

Conclusion: The twelve candidates reported by Sugiyama et al. are not microlensing events but classical variable stars. There is no evidence from this dataset for a significant population of planetary-mass primordial black holes contributing to dark matter. Robust rejection of variable stars is essential in high-cadence microlensing surveys with large-aperture telescopes.

Sugiyama等人报告的十二个候选体并非微引力透镜事件，而是经典的变星。该数据集未提供任何证据支持行星质量原初黑洞（PBHs）在暗物质中占据显著比例。在使用大口径望远镜开展高时序采样微引力透镜搜寻时，有效排除变星干扰至关重要。

Abstract: A recent preprint by Sugiyama et al. reported the discovery of twelve candidates for short-timescale (less than one day) gravitational microlensing events based on high-cadence photometric observations of the Andromeda Galaxy (M31) using the Subaru Hyper Suprime-Cam. These detections were attributed to a large population of planetary-mass primordial black holes (PBHs) that could account for the entirety of the dark matter in the Milky Way and M31 halos. However, these results are in clear tension with previous searches for short-timescale microlensing events toward the Magellanic Clouds, such as those by the OGLE survey. In addition, both the temporal and spatial distributions of the Subaru candidates are inconsistent with expectations for microlensing events. Here, we reanalyze the Subaru data using an independent difference image analysis photometric pipeline. We find that all twelve candidates identified by Sugiyama et al. exhibit asymmetric light curves and/or variability on multiple nights of Subaru observations. Our analysis reveals that among them ten objects are RR Lyrae stars, one is an eclipsing binary, and one is an unclassified variable star. We find no compelling evidence for short-timescale microlensing events among the candidates identified in the Subaru data set, nor for a significant population of planetary-mass PBHs as dark matter components. Our results underscore the necessity of robust variable-star rejection in high-cadence microlensing searches using large telescopes.

</details>


### [44] [Calibrating optical galaxy cluster projection effects with sparse spectroscopic samples: A clustering redshift approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00420)
*Lei Yang,Hao-Yi Wu,Tesla Jeltema,Chun-Hao To,Ross Cawthon,Shulei Cao*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We develop a clustering redshift method to quantify projection effects in optically identified galaxy clusters by cross-correlating with sparse spectroscopic samples, validated using the Cardinal simulation and applicable to future LSST cluster calibration with DESI and Roman data.

我们开发了一种成团性红移方法，通过将光学识别的星系团成员与稀疏光谱样本交叉关联来量化投影效应，该方法在Cardinal模拟中得到验证，并可用于未来LSST星系团利用DESI和Roman数据进行校准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Optically identified galaxy clusters suffer from line-of-sight projection effects due to photometric distance uncertainties, leading to contamination from unrelated galaxies. Spectroscopic follow-up can mitigate this but is observationally expensive and cannot scale with current survey growth. Meanwhile, large-scale structure spectroscopic surveys (e.g., DESI) provide abundant redshifts but sparsely sample clusters. A scalable, robust method is needed to leverage these non-targeted spectra to calibrate cluster catalogs.

光学识别的星系团由于测光距离不确定性而受到视线方向投影效应的影响，导致非相关星系的污染。光谱后随观测可缓解此问题，但观测成本高且难以跟上当前巡天的增长速度。同时，大尺度结构光谱巡天（如DESI）提供了大量红移数据，但在星系团区域采样稀疏。因此需要一种可扩展且稳健的方法，利用这些非目标导向的光谱数据来校准星系团星表。

Method: We apply a clustering redshift (CZ) technique that cross-correlates photometric galaxies associated with optically detected clusters (e.g., redMaPPer) with spectroscopic galaxies from non-cluster-targeted surveys. The redshift distribution of cluster members is inferred from angular cross-power spectra or pair counts in configuration space, leveraging large-scale structure correlations while marginalizing over selection effects. We validate the method using the Cardinal suite of cosmological simulations, which include realistic imaging and spectroscopic survey masks, noise, and galaxy-halo connections.

我们应用一种成团性红移（clustering redshift, CZ）技术，将光学探测到的星系团（如redMaPPer）相关的测光星系与非针对星系团的光谱星系巡天数据进行交叉关联。通过角交叉功率谱或构型空间中的对计数，从大尺度结构的相关性中推断星系团成员的红移分布，同时边缘化选择效应。我们使用Cardinal系列宇宙学模拟对该方法进行验证，该模拟包含真实的成像与光谱巡天掩模、噪声以及星系-晕关联模型。

Result: Our method accurately recovers the true spectroscopic redshift distribution of redMaPPer cluster members and robustly quantifies the amplitude and shape parameters of the projection effects. It is insensitive to the specific choice of spectroscopic sample (e.g., luminous red galaxies vs. emission-line galaxies), demonstrating its versatility. Validation with Cardinal confirms sub-percent level accuracy in recovering redshift distributions, even with sparse spectroscopic coverage.

我们的方法准确恢复了redMaPPer星系团成员的真实光谱红移分布，并稳健地量化了投影效应的振幅和形状参数。该方法对光谱样本的选择（例如亮红星系vs发射线星系）不敏感，表现出良好的通用性。通过Cardinal模拟的验证表明，即使在光谱覆盖稀疏的情况下，红移分布的恢复精度仍能达到千分之一水平。

Conclusion: The clustering redshift approach provides a powerful, scalable solution to calibrate projection effects in optically selected cluster samples using existing sparse spectroscopic surveys like DESI and NASA's Roman Space Telescope. This enables high-precision cosmological analyses with LSST-era cluster catalogs by mitigating photometric contamination without requiring dedicated spectroscopic follow-up.

成团性红移方法为利用现有稀疏光谱巡天（如DESI和NASA罗马太空望远镜）校准光学选星星系团样本中的投影效应提供了一种强大且可扩展的解决方案。该方法使得在无需专门光谱后随观测的情况下，即可减轻测光污染，从而实现LSST时代星系团星表的高精度宇宙学分析。

Abstract: Wide-field optical imaging surveys are efficient at identifying galaxy clusters, but optically identified clusters suffer from projection effects--physically unassociated galaxies along the line of sight can be misidentified as cluster members due to distance uncertainties. Previous studies have used spectroscopic follow-up observations of cluster members to quantify projection effects; however, such follow-up efforts cannot keep pace with the rapidly growing cluster samples. On the other hand, spectroscopic surveys designed for large-scale structure studies collect tens of millions of spectra but tend to have sparse spectra in cluster regions. To bridge this gap, we develop a clustering redshift approach that cross-correlates cluster members with sparse, non-cluster-targeted spectroscopic galaxy samples. We validate this approach using the Cardinal simulation, recovering the correct spectroscopic distribution and projection effect parameters of redMaPPer cluster members. Our approach is insensitive to the selection of the spectroscopic sample and paves the way for calibrating the upcoming LSST clusters using DESI and Roman spectroscopic samples.

</details>


### [45] [Relic Magnetic Fields from Non-Adiabatic Photon Freeze-Out at Recombination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00454)
*Hyeong-Chan Kim*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We propose a novel mechanism for generating a primordial electromagnetic relic during recombination, driven by non-adiabatic mode squeezing due to finite Thomson relaxation rates in the photon-electron plasma. The relic arises from a freeze-out of non-equilibrium dynamics and exhibits a characteristic scale set by $k^3\mathscr S_k$, peaking at $10$--$20$ Mpc today, though with negligible field strength.

我们提出了一种在复合时期产生原初电磁遗迹的新机制，该机制由光子-电子等离子体中汤姆逊弛豫率有限导致的非绝热模挤压驱动。该遗迹源于非平衡动力学的冻结，其特征尺度由$k^3\mathscr S_k$决定，今天对应的峰值尺度为$10$--$20$ Mpc，但场强极弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The origin of large-scale cosmic magnetic fields remains poorly understood, and conventional dynamo mechanisms require seed fields of unknown provenance. We aim to identify a robust physical mechanism during the well-understood epoch of recombination that can generate a primordial electromagnetic relic as a potential seed, leveraging the non-equilibrium thermodynamics of the photon gas coupled to matter.

大尺度宇宙磁场的起源仍不清楚，传统发电机机制需要来源未知的种子场。我们的目标是利用复合时期光子气体与物质耦合的非平衡热力学，在这一已被充分理解的宇宙阶段中寻找一种可靠的物理机制，以生成可能的原初电磁遗迹种子。

Method: We model the photon sector as an open quantum system interacting with the electron plasma via Thomson scattering, incorporating a time-dependent relaxation rate. Using a canonical transformation, we map the system's evolution to a forced harmonic oscillator with a smooth effective potential. This allows us to analyze the transition from adiabatic tracking to freeze-out and compute the resulting mode squeezing $\mathscr S_k$. The magnetic spectrum is then obtained by projecting the non-equilibrium relic onto the magnetic component.

我们将光子部分建模为通过汤姆逊散射与电子等离子体相互作用的开放量子系统，并引入时间依赖的弛豫率。通过正则变换，将系统的演化映射到具有平滑有效势的受迫谐振子上，从而分析从绝热跟踪到冻结的转变，并计算相应的模挤压$\mathscr S_k$。然后通过将非平衡遗迹投影到磁场分量上得到磁谱。

Result: A narrow transition layer forms during recombination where non-adiabatic effects induce finite mode squeezing. The squeezing freezes out as the system exits the relaxation regime, leaving behind a frozen non-equilibrium electromagnetic relic. The projected magnetic spectrum peaks at comoving scales of $10$--$20$ Mpc, determined by the combination $k^3\mathscr S_k$, while the present-day amplitude is extremely small, $B_0 \ll 10^{-20}$ G.

在复合期间形成一个狭窄的过渡层，非绝热效应引发有限的模挤压。当系统离开弛豫区时，挤压冻结，留下一个冻结的非平衡电磁遗迹。投影后的磁谱在共动尺度$10$--$20$ Mpc处达到峰值，由组合量$k^3\mathscr S_k$决定，而当前幅度极小，$B_0 \ll 10^{-20}$ G。

Conclusion: We identify a new physical mechanism during recombination—driven by rate-dependent non-equilibrium thermodynamics—that generates a frozen primordial electromagnetic relic with a well-defined comoving scale. While too weak to explain observed cosmic magnetic fields directly, it represents a robust prediction of non-equilibrium QED effects in the early universe and may serve as a template for relic generation in other sectors.

我们发现了复合时期一种由速率依赖的非平衡热力学驱动的新物理机制，可产生具有明确共动尺度的冻结原初电磁遗迹。尽管其强度不足以直接解释观测到的宇宙磁场，但它代表了早期宇宙中非平衡QED效应的一个稳健预测，并可能为其他领域的遗迹生成提供模板。

Abstract: We propose a new mechanism for generating a primordial electromagnetic relic during the recombination--decoupling transition, based on the rate-dependent thermodynamics of the cosmic photon gas. Treating the photon sector as an open system coupled to the electron plasma, we show that a finite Thomson relaxation rate generates a departure from instantaneous thermal equilibrium, leading to non-adiabatic mode squeezing. As this relaxation rate rapidly decreases across recombination, the system quickly loses the ability to further amplify the deviation, and the squeezing freezes out at a small but finite value. This dynamics is naturally described as a narrow transition layer between an adiabatic tracking regime and a post-relaxation freeze-out regime. By a canonical transformation, the reduced evolution equation is recast into a forced oscillator with a smooth effective potential, clarifying the origin of the squeezing and the selection of the relic scale.
  Projecting the resulting non-equilibrium electromagnetic relic onto the magnetic sector, we derive the corresponding spectrum and show that its characteristic peak is controlled not by the squeezing parameter alone but by the weighted combination \(k^3\mathscr S_k\). In representative realizations, the peak corresponds today to scales of order \(10\)--\(20\) Mpc, while the present-day field amplitude remains extremely small. The mechanism is therefore better viewed as a source of a frozen non-equilibrium electromagnetic relic than as a complete explanation of the observed cosmic magnetic fields.

</details>


### [46] [A Geometric Theory of Cosmological Structure via Entropic Curvature in Wasserstein Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00593)
*Tsutomu T. Takeuchi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We develop a geometric framework for cosmological large-scale structure using optimal transport and Wasserstein geometry, introducing effective Ricci curvatures $K_{\mathrm{eff}}^{(\infty)}$ and $K_{\mathrm{eff}}^{(N)}$ based on entropy functionals, which reduce to Hessian-based classifiers in the local quadratic limit. These curvatures are localized for observational use and exhibit a scale-dependent flow, offering a new geometric statistical description of density fields via power spectrum integrals and correlation function derivatives.

我们基于最优传输理论和Wasserstein几何构建了宇宙大尺度结构的几何框架，引入了基于熵泛函的有效Ricci曲率$K_{\mathrm{eff}}^{(\infty)}$和$K_{\mathrm{eff}}^{(N)}$，在局部二次近似下其退化为基于Hessian的分类器。这些曲率可局域化以适用于观测，并表现出尺度依赖性流，通过功率谱积分和关联函数导数提供了密度场新的几何统计描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cosmological large-scale structure is traditionally analyzed using density fields and their statistical moments, but such approaches often neglect intrinsic geometric and nonlinear aspects of structure formation. There is a need for a coordinate-invariant, geometrically meaningful framework that captures multiscale and nonlinear features beyond linear perturbation theory. Optimal transport offers a natural setting for comparing probability distributions in cosmology, motivating the development of a curvature-based geometric description.

宇宙大尺度结构传统上通过密度场及其统计矩进行分析，但这些方法常忽略结构形成的内在几何与非线性特征。需要一种坐标不变、几何意义明确的框架来捕捉超越线性微扰理论的多尺度与非线性特性。最优传输为宇宙学中概率分布的比较提供了自然背景，促使发展基于曲率的几何描述框架。

Method: We apply optimal transport theory on the space of probability measures $\mathcal{P}_2(M)$ equipped with the Wasserstein metric. Ricci curvature is defined via geodesic convexity of Kullback--Leibler and Rényi entropies, leading to effective curvatures $K_{\mathrm{eff}}^{(\infty)}$ and $K_{\mathrm{eff}}^{(N)}$ associated with CD$(K,\infty)$ and CD$(K,N)$ conditions. These are localized using reference and local measures, and approximated under a local quadratic expansion of the potential, linking to the Hessian of the log-density. Scale dependence is modeled as a 'scale flow' by varying resolution, and curvature statistics are derived from the power spectrum and two-point correlation function.

我们在配备Wasserstein度量的概率测度空间$\mathcal{P}_2(M)$上应用最优传输理论，通过Kullback-Leibler与Rényi熵的测地凸性定义Ricci曲率，得到对应于CD$(K,\infty)$与CD$(K,N)$条件的有效曲率$K_{\mathrm{eff}}^{(\infty)}$和$K_{\mathrm{eff}}^{(N)}$。使用参考与局域测度对其进行局域化，并在势的局部二次展开下逼近，联系至对数密度的Hessian矩阵。通过改变分辨率建模‘尺度流’以描述尺度依赖性，曲率统计量由功率谱与两点关联函数导出。

Result: The effective Ricci curvatures $K_{\mathrm{eff}}^{(\infty)}$ and $K_{\mathrm{eff}}^{(N)}$ provide a geometric characterization of cosmic structures, reducing to conventional Hessian-based classification (e.g., into voids, sheets, filaments, knots) in the local limit. The framework reveals a novel 'scale flow' of curvature under changing observational resolution, distinct from Ricci flow. Curvature statistics are expressed as higher-order weighted integrals of the power spectrum $P(k)$ and spatial derivatives of the correlation function $\xi(r)$, emphasizing geometric information over amplitude. This enables multiscale, nonlinear analysis of structure beyond standard EFTofLSS or N-body simulation interpretations.

有效Ricci曲率$K_{\mathrm{eff}}^{(\infty)}$和$K_{\mathrm{eff}}^{(N)}$为宇宙结构提供了几何刻画，在局域极限下退化为传统的基于Hessian的分类（如空洞、片状、纤维、节点）。该框架揭示了随观测分辨率变化的新颖‘尺度流’，不同于Ricci流。曲率统计量表示为功率谱$P(k)$的高阶加权积分与关联函数$\xi(r)$的空间导数，强调几何信息而非振幅。这使得超越标准EFTofLSS或N体模拟解释的多尺度、非线性结构分析成为可能。

Conclusion: We establish a unified geometric framework connecting optimal transport, entropy-based curvature, and cosmological large-scale structure. This approach generalizes traditional structure classification by embedding it within a rigorous Wasserstein-geometric setting, and introduces curvature as a fundamental observable with scale-dependent behavior. The framework opens new avenues for analyzing nonlinear and multiscale structure through geometric statistics, with potential applications in data analysis of galaxy surveys and simulations.

我们建立了连接最优传输、基于熵的曲率与宇宙大尺度结构的统一几何框架。该方法通过将传统结构分类嵌入严格的Wasserstein几何背景中实现推广，并将曲率作为具有尺度依赖行为的基本可观测量引入。该框架为通过几何统计分析非线性与多尺度结构开辟了新途径，在星系巡天与模拟的数据分析中具有潜在应用。

Abstract: We construct a geometric framework for cosmological large-scale structure based on optimal transport theory and Wasserstein geometry. In this framework, Ricci curvature on the probability measure space $\mathcal{P}_2(M)$ is characterized by the geodesic convexity of entropy and is formulated as the response of probability distributions to optimal transport. We introduce effective Ricci curvatures $K_{\mathrm{eff}}^{(\infty)}$ and $K_{\mathrm{eff}}^{(N)}$ associated with Kullback--Leibler-type and Rényi-type entropies, corresponding respectively to the curvature-dimension conditions CD$(K,\infty)$ and CD$(K,N)$. By localizing these curvatures to finite scales using local and reference measures, we construct curvature indicators applicable to observational data. Under a local quadratic approximation, the effective curvature reduces to the Hessian of the log-density, showing that conventional Hessian-based structure classifications arise as a limiting case of the present framework. We further show that effective curvature depends on observational scale and formulate this dependence as a scale flow, distinct from Ricci flow because it describes a change of resolution rather than a time evolution of geometry. Treating curvature as a random field then extends the statistical description of density fields: curvature statistics are given by higher-order weighted integrals of the power spectrum and by spatial derivatives of the correlation function, emphasizing geometric rather than amplitude information. This framework provides a unified connection between optimal transport geometry and cosmological structure analysis, and offers a new perspective on multiscale structure and nonlinear statistics.

</details>

*Euclid Collaboration,K. A. Bertmann,A. Porredon,V. Duret,J. Fonseca,H. Hildebrandt,I. Tutusaus,S. Camera,S. Escoffier,N. Aghanim,B. Altieri,A. Amara,S. Andreon,N. Auricchio,C. Baccigalupi,M. Passalacqua,K. Paterson,L. Patrizii,A. Pisani,D. Potter,G. W. Pratt,S. Quai,M. Radovich,K. Rojas,W. Roster,S. Sacquegna,D. B. Sanders,E. Sarpa,A. Schneider,M. Schultheis,D. Sciotti,E. Sellentin,L. C. Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The study investigates the impact of redshift uncertainties on Euclid's photometric galaxy clustering and its combination with weak lensing in the 3×2pt analysis for DR1, finding that precise knowledge of the mean redshift per bin (accurate to 0.004(1+z)) is essential to retain 80% of cosmological constraining power, while uncertainty in higher-order moments like width is negligible if the mean is well-constrained.

该研究调查了红移不确定性对Euclid巡天光度星系聚类及其与弱引力透镜联合分析（3×2pt）的影响，发现每红移bin的平均红移必须精确到0.004(1+z)才能保留80%的宇宙学约束能力，而只要均值足够精确，宽度等高阶矩的不确定性可忽略不计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: While Euclid has set photo-$z$ accuracy requirements for the weak lensing sample, no such requirements exist for the photometric galaxy clustering sample; this work aims to establish quantitative thresholds for redshift distribution accuracy—particularly in the mean and higher-order moments—to avoid biases in cosmological parameters from the 3×2pt analysis.

尽管Euclid已为弱引力透镜样本设定了光谱红移精度要求，但尚未为光度星系聚类样本设定类似标准；本工作旨在为红移分布的精度（特别是均值和高阶矩）建立量化阈值，以避免3×2pt分析中宇宙学参数出现偏差。

Method: We perform a Fisher matrix analysis of Euclid's DR1 3×2pt dataset (cosmic shear, galaxy clustering, galaxy-galaxy lensing), modeling redshift distribution uncertainties in the photometric clustering sample by varying the mean and width (second moment) of redshift bins; we assess the resulting degradation in constraints on $w_{\mathrm{0}}$ and $w_{a}$ in the $w_{\mathrm{0}}w_{a}$CDM model, defining acceptable error thresholds based on retaining 80% of the constraining power.

我们对Euclid的DR1 3×2pt数据集（宇宙剪切、星系聚类、星系-星系透镜）进行Fisher矩阵分析，通过改变红移bin的均值和宽度（二阶矩）来模拟光度聚类样本的红移分布不确定性，并评估在$w_{\mathrm{0}}w_{a}$CDM模型中对$w_{\mathrm{0}}$和$w_{a}$约束能力的退化程度，基于保留80%约束力来定义可接受的误差阈值。

Result: The mean of the redshift distribution must be known to an accuracy of $\Delta z = 0.004(1+z)$ to recover 80% of the constraining power on $w_{\mathrm{0}}$ and $w_{a}$; uncertainty in the width of the distribution has a negligible impact as long as the mean is sufficiently constrained; for most systematics, controlling the mean to this level automatically suppresses width errors below critical levels.

为恢复80%对$w_{\mathrm{0}}$和$w_{a}$的约束能力，红移分布的均值必须精确至$\Delta z = 0.004(1+z)$；只要均值被充分约束，分布宽度的不确定性影响可忽略；对于大多数系统误差，将均值控制在此水平即可自动使宽度误差低于临界水平。

Conclusion: Accurate calibration of the mean redshift in photometric clustering bins is critical for Euclid's 3×2pt cosmological analysis, while higher-order moments like the width require significantly less stringent control; this work provides concrete photo-$z$ requirements for the photometric clustering sample, filling a key gap in Euclid's observational strategy.

光度星系聚类红移bin中平均红移的精确校准对Euclid的3×2pt宇宙学分析至关重要，而宽度等高阶矩的控制要求则宽松得多；本研究为光度聚类样本提供了具体的光谱红移要求，填补了Euclid观测策略中的关键空白。

Abstract: One of the $\textit{Euclid}$ mission's key projects is the so-called 3$\times$2pt analysis, that is, the combination of cosmic shear, photometric galaxy clustering, and galaxy-galaxy lensing. Although $\textit{Euclid}$ has established quality requirements for the photo-$z$ accuracy needed for the weak lensing galaxy sample, no such requirements have been set for the photometric clustering sample. In this paper, we investigate the impact of redshift uncertainties on $\textit{Euclid}$'s photometric galaxy clustering analysis and its combination with weak gravitational lensing, focusing on data release 1 (DR1). In particular, we study whether having precise knowledge of the mean of the redshift distributions per bin is sufficient to avoid biases in the resulting cosmological constraints or whether accuracy in the higher-order moments of the distribution is required. We evaluate the results based on their constraining power on $w_{\mathrm{0}}$ and $w_{a}$ and define thresholds for the precision and accuracy of $\textit{Euclid}$'s redshift distribution of the photometric clustering sample. We find that the redshift distributions of the photometric clustering sample must be known at an accuracy of 0.004(1+$z$) in the mean in order to recover 80$\%$ of the constraining power in $\textit{Euclid}$'s DR1 $w_{\mathrm{0}}w_{a}$CDM 3$\times$2pt analysis. The impact of the uncertainty on the width is negligible, provided the mean redshift is constrained with sufficient accuracy. For most sources of redshift distribution error, attaining the requirement on the mean will also reduce uncertainty in the width well below the required level.

</details>


### [48] [Transport-Geometric Formulation of Peak Statistics: Curvature-Conditioned Point Processes and Response Hierarchy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00873)
*Tsutomu T. Takeuchi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We propose a geometric framework for peak statistics in cosmological density fields using optimal transport and entropy, where peaks are positive-curvature stationary points of the log-density field. In the Gaussian limit, it recovers the classic BBKS theory, and beyond, it systematically incorporates non-Gaussianity and nonlinearity through curvature-dependent deformations. Higher-order peak correlations emerge as response functions to long-wavelength modes, generalizing peak bias.

我们提出了一种基于最优输运和熵的宇宙密度场中峰统计的几何框架，其中峰被定义为对数密度场的正曲率驻点。在高斯极限下，该框架恢复经典的BBKS理论；在此之外，它通过曲率相关的形变系统地纳入非高斯性和非线性效应。高阶峰关联作为对长波模式的响应函数出现，推广了峰偏置的概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional peak statistics (e.g., BBKS) are limited to linear, Gaussian fields and lack a systematic extension to nonlinear and non-Gaussian regimes. A more fundamental formulation is needed to unify peak theory with modern concepts in probability geometry and information theory, enabling robust predictions for large-scale structure in the universe.

传统的峰统计（如BBKS）局限于线性高斯场，缺乏向非线性和非高斯情形系统扩展的能力。需要一个更基础的框架，将峰理论与概率几何和信息论的现代概念统一起来，以增强对宇宙大尺度结构的预测能力。

Method: We treat the cosmological density field as a probability measure and use optimal transport to define a geometric structure on Wasserstein space. The Hessian of the log-density emerges as the local response of an entropy functional, allowing peaks to be defined via curvature conditions. We derive the number density of peaks as a curvature-conditioned point process and compute higher-order statistics using conditional $n$-point correlation measures. Spectral moments govern the closure in the Gaussian limit, while deviations are modeled via deformations of the joint distribution of curvature variables.

我们将宇宙密度场视为概率测度，并利用最优输运在Wasserstein空间上定义几何结构。对数密度的Hessian作为熵泛函的局域响应出现，从而可通过曲率条件定义峰。我们推导出峰数密度为曲率条件化的点过程，并使用条件$n$-点关联测度计算高阶统计量。在高斯极限下由谱矩实现闭合，而偏离则通过对曲率变量联合分布的形变建模。

Result: The framework recovers BBKS peak statistics in the linear Gaussian limit and extends them to include nonlinear and non-Gaussian effects. The two- and three-point peak correlations are derived as curvature-conditioned $n$-point measures. The full hierarchy of peak statistics is organized as response functions to long-wavelength background modes, with conventional peak bias as the leading-order coefficient and higher-order correlations as natural extensions.

该框架在线性高斯极限下恢复BBKS峰统计，并将其扩展至包含非线性和非高斯效应。二点和三点峰关联被导出为曲率条件化的$n$-点测度。完整的峰统计层级被组织为对长波背景模式的响应函数，传统峰偏置作为最低阶系数，高阶关联为其自然延伸。

Conclusion: Peak statistics can be embedded into a unified geometric framework based on optimal transport and entropy in Wasserstein space. This provides a systematic basis for incorporating nonlinearity, non-Gaussianity, and higher-order correlations, with direct applications to cosmological observables such as galaxy clustering and weak lensing.

峰统计可被嵌入基于Wasserstein空间中最优输运和熵的统一几何框架。这为纳入非线性、非高斯性及高阶关联提供了系统基础，对星系成团性和弱引力透镜等宇宙学观测具有直接应用价值。

Abstract: We develop a geometric formulation of peak statistics in cosmological density fields based on optimal transport and entropy. In this framework, the density field is treated as a probability measure, and its local structure is characterized by the Hessian of the log-density, which arises as the local response of an entropy functional in Wasserstein space. Peaks are thereby defined as positive-curvature stationary points, and their number density is expressed as a curvature-conditioned point process. In the linear Gaussian limit, the joint distribution of local variables closes in terms of a finite set of spectral moments, recovering the standard theory of peak statistics, known as BBKS. This clarifies that BBKS corresponds to a solvable limit of a more general structure combining probability distributions, curvature constraints, and geometric measure. The framework extends naturally beyond Gaussianity and linearity. Deviations from Gaussianity are incorporated as deformations of the joint distribution of curvature variables, while nonlinear structures are described through the curvature of the log-density. We further derive the two- and three-point peak statistics as curvature-conditioned $n$-point measures, and show that the full hierarchy of peak statistics can be organized as response functions to long-wavelength background modes. In this formulation, the conventional peak bias appears as the lowest-order response coefficient, with higher-order correlations arising as its natural extensions. This work embeds peak theory into a unified geometric framework and provides a systematic basis for incorporating nonlinearity, non-Gaussianity, and higher-order statistics, with direct relevance for observational applications.

</details>


### [49] [Universal Non-Gaussian Signatures from Transient Instabilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01035)
*Shuntaro Aoki,Diederik Roest,Denis Werth*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We compute the bispectrum signatures from tachyonic instabilities of entropic fluctuations during inflation in hyperbolic field-space geometries, identifying universal features in both light and heavy mass regimes. In the light case ($m \sim H$), we find enhanced folded configurations and non-analytic squeezed limits; in the heavy case ($m \gg H$), a tachyonic resonance appears in mildly squeezed limits. No single-field effective theory fully captures the bispectrum across all scales. We provide observational templates for current and future surveys.

我们计算了在双曲场空间几何中通胀期间熵扰动的瞬态快子不稳定性所产生的 bispectrum 特征，在轻质量和重质量两种情形下识别出普适性特征。对于轻质量情况（$m \sim H$），我们发现折叠构型增强以及非解析的挤压极限行为；对于重质量情况（$m \gg H$），在弱挤压极限出现由不稳定性强度决定的“快子共振”。我们证明不存在一个单场有效理论能在所有运动学构型下准确描述该 bispectrum。我们提供了适用于当前和未来观测的简单形状模板。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Tachyonic instabilities of entropic modes in multi-field inflation are generic in negatively curved field spaces, yet their imprints on non-Gaussianity—particularly the bispectrum—remain poorly understood. A model-independent characterization is needed to connect such fundamental geometric effects to observable signatures and to test non-geodesic inflationary attractors beyond slow-roll single-field paradigms.

在负曲率场空间中的多场通胀中，熵模的快子不稳定性是普遍现象，但其对非高斯性——特别是 bispectrum——的影响仍缺乏理解。需要一种模型无关的刻画方式，将这些基本几何效应与可观测信号联系起来，并检验超越慢滚单场范式的非测地线 inflationary attractors。

Method: We perform exact numerical calculations of the bispectrum directly from the dynamics of fluctuations, without assuming a specific background trajectory. We analyze two regimes: light entropic masses ($m \sim H$) and heavy masses ($m \gg H$). We compute mode functions and three-point correlators using in-in formalism in the Schwinger-Keldysh framework. We contrast full two-field results with predictions from an integrated-out single-field EFT, testing its validity across kinematic configurations. Simple analytical templates are proposed for data analysis.

我们直接从扰动的动力学出发，进行 bispectrum 的精确数值计算，而不假设特定背景轨迹。我们分析两种情形：轻熵质量（$m \sim H$）和重质量（$m \gg H$）。使用 Schwinger-Keldysh 框架下的 in-in 形式主义计算模函数和三点关联函数。我们将完整的双场结果与积分掉熵模后的单场 EFT 预测进行对比，检验其在不同运动学构型下的有效性。提出了用于数据分析的简单解析模板。

Result: In the light mass case, we find a universal enhancement of the folded triangle configuration and the expected scaling $\propto 1/(k_{\rm sq}/k_{\ast})$ in the squeezed limit, confirming analytic expectations. For the first time, this bispectrum is computed exactly from tachyonic instability dynamics. In the heavy mass case, a novel 'tachyonic resonance' peak emerges at mild squeezing, with scale $k_{\rm res} \propto \sqrt{|\mu|}H$, where $\mu < 0$ quantifies the instability strength. The single-field EFT fails to capture the full bispectrum, especially near the resonance and folded limits, due to memory effects and non-Markovian dynamics from the integrated-out sector. Analytical shape templates are constructed that closely match the numerical results.

在轻质量情况下，我们发现折叠三角构型的普适增强，以及挤压极限下预期的 $\propto 1/(k_{\rm sq}/k_{\ast})$ 标度行为，验证了解析预言。这是首次从快子不稳定性动力学中精确计算该 bispectrum。在重质量情况下，一种新的“快子共振”峰出现在弱挤压区域，其尺度为 $k_{\rm res} \propto \sqrt{|\mu|}H$，其中 $\mu < 0$ 表征不稳定性强度。由于被积出部分的记忆效应和非马尔可夫动力学，单场 EFT 无法捕捉完整 bispectrum，尤其在共振和折叠构型附近失效。我们构建了解析形状模板，能很好拟合数值结果。

Conclusion: Tachyonic instabilities in hyperbolic field spaces generate distinct, universal bispectrum signatures that cannot be fully captured by single-field EFTs. The enhanced folded and resonant squeezed configurations serve as smoking-gun signals for strong non-geodesic motion and transient entropic sourcing. Our model-independent templates enable direct tests of such inflationary scenarios with CMB and large-scale structure surveys, opening new avenues for probing high-energy geometry through cosmological non-Gaussianity.

双曲场空间中的快子不稳定性会产生独特且普适的 bispectrum 特征，这些特征无法被单场 EFT 完全捕捉。增强的折叠构型和共振型挤压极限构型是强非测地线运动和瞬态熵源激发的标志性信号。我们的模型无关模板使得通过 CMB 和大尺度结构巡天直接检验此类 inflation 情景成为可能，为利用宇宙学非高斯性探测高能几何开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We identify universal signatures in the bispectrum arising from a transient tachyonic instability of entropic fluctuations during inflation, a phenomenon that naturally arises in hyperbolic field-space geometries. We perform exact numerical calculations directly at the level of fluctuations, without relying on a specific background model, and distinguish two cases. In the light case, with masses around the Hubble scale, our results provide the first-ever computation of the bispectrum due to such tachyonic instabilities. We find a universal magnification of the folded configuration, together with the known non-analytic scaling in the squeezed limit. As an illustrative example, we compute and analyse the bispectrum in angular inflation, demonstrating compatibility with current limits. In the heavy case, with masses well above the Hubble scale, the bispectrum exhibits a distinctive correlation between enhanced folded configurations and a `tachyonic resonance' in mildly squeezed limits, with the resonance scale set by the strength of the instability. While the main qualitative features are reproduced, we show that there exists no UV matching for which a single-field effective description, obtained by integrating out the entropic modes, accurately captures the bispectrum for all kinematic configurations. To facilitate observational applications, we introduce simple bispectrum shape templates suitable for current and forthcoming cosmological surveys. Our model-independent results allow for constraining non-standard inflationary attractors characterised by strongly non-geodesic motion.

</details>


### [50] [Curvature-induced electroweak symmetry breaking and phase transition of a Higgs-portal dark scalar field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01084)
*Andreas Mantziris*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper studies gravitational wave (GW) production from a curvature-induced phase transition of a non-minimally coupled scalar dark matter field connected via a Higgs-portal, during the inflation-to-kination transition. Kination amplifies GW signals, narrowing viable parameters, yet some regions remain detectable by future experiments.

本文研究了通过Higgs门户耦合的非最小耦合标量暗物质场在曲率诱导相变过程中产生的引力波（GW），该过程发生在通胀到急动（kination）的过渡阶段。急动放大了GW信号，缩小了可行参数空间，但部分区域仍可被未来实验探测到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The possibility that dark matter could be a scalar field non-minimally coupled to gravity, undergoing a phase transition triggered by curvature effects during cosmic evolution, motivates the study of associated gravitational wave signatures. Additionally, linking this sector to the Standard Model via a Higgs-portal opens the possibility of influencing electroweak symmetry breaking, offering testable connections between dark sectors and observable physics.

暗物质可能是与引力非最小耦合的标量场，在宇宙演化期间由曲率效应触发相变，这促使人们研究相关的引力波信号。此外，通过Higgs门户将此暗区与标准模型连接，可能影响电弱对称性破缺，为暗区与可观测物理之间提供可检验的联系。

Method: The dynamics of the phase transition were analyzed by solving the evolution equations for a scalar field $\phi$ with non-minimal coupling $\xi R \phi^2$ in curved spacetime, during the transition from inflation to kination. Different inflationary scales and values of $\xi$ (both positive and negative) were considered. The induced gravitational wave spectrum was computed from anisotropic stress perturbations using standard cosmological perturbation theory, and constraints were derived based on detectability by future observatories such as LISA, ET, and CE.

通过求解标量场$\phi$在弯曲时空中的演化方程（含非最小耦合项$\xi R \phi^2$），分析了从通胀到急动过渡期间的相变动力学。考虑了不同的通胀能标和$\xi$值（正负皆有）。利用标准宇宙学扰动理论，从各向异性应力扰动计算诱导的引力波谱，并基于LISA、ET和CE等未来观测站的可探测性推导出约束条件。

Result: Kination significantly enhances the amplitude of generated gravitational waves due to its stiff equation of state. This enhancement strongly constrains the allowed parameter space, particularly for large $|\xi|$ and high inflationary scales. However, despite these constraints, there exist regions—especially for moderate $\xi$ and intermediate inflation scales—where the GW signal falls within the sensitivity ranges of future detectors. The phase transition may also trigger electroweak symmetry breaking depending on Higgs-portal couplings.

由于急动具有刚性状态方程，显著增强了所产生的引力波振幅。这种增强强烈限制了允许的参数空间，特别是对于大的$|\xi|$和高通胀能标。然而，尽管存在这些限制，仍存在一些区域——尤其是中等$\xi$和中等通胀能标下——其GW信号落在未来探测器的灵敏度范围内。根据Higgs-门户耦合的不同，该相变也可能触发电弱对称性破缺。

Conclusion: Curvature-induced phase transitions in non-minimally coupled scalar dark matter models during inflation-kination transitions can produce observable gravitational wave signals, especially when enhanced by kination. These scenarios are tightly constrained but not ruled out, offering promising targets for future GW experiments and potential links to electroweak symmetry breaking through Higgs-portal interactions.

在通胀-急动过渡期间，非最小耦合标量暗物质模型中的曲率诱导相变可产生可观测的引力波信号，尤其是在急动增强下。这些情景虽受严格限制但尚未被排除，为未来的引力波实验提供了有希望的目标，并通过Higgs-门户相互作用与电弱对称性破缺建立潜在联系。

Abstract: This overview of the study arXiv:2407.18845, regarding the possibility of generating gravitational waves from a curvature-induced phase transition of a non-minimally coupled scalar dark matter field with a Higgs-portal, was showcased at the "Workshop on Standard Model and Beyond 2025" of the Corfu Summer Institute 2025. The phase transition dynamics during the transition from inflation to kination were calculated for various inflationary scales, considering both positive and negative values of the non-minimal coupling, while also examining the potential for triggering electroweak symmetry breaking. Notably, kination enhances the GW amplitudes, significantly restricting the viable parameter space. While the GW spectra follow the usual rule for high-frequencies from high inflationary scales, certain regions of the parameter space allow for a potential detection with future experiments.

### [51] [Cosmological zoom-in perturbation theory as a consistent beyond point-particle approximation framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01112)
*Obinna Umeh*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: Summary generation failed


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Motivation analysis unavailable

Method: Method extraction failed

Result: Result analysis unavailable

Conclusion: Conclusion extraction failed

Abstract: Modelling structure formation across the full dynamical range of the Universe remains a major challenge in cosmology. This difficulty originates from a fundamental limitation of geodesics in general relativity: a one-parameter family of geodesics can cease to be geodesic at a finite time. This implies that the conventional point-particle approximation is not the primary issue; rather, the breakdown of geodesic flow restricts a consistent description across scales. We develop a covariant multi-scale framework that resolves this problem by decomposing spacetime into hierarchical regions separated by matter horizons. We show how to match shared boundary consistently at the level of the action, leading to a covariant backreaction contribution. The resulting construction provides a first-principles theoretical foundation for cosmological zoom-in simulations and yields an effective energy-momentum tensor capturing the impact of the geometric backreaction effect. As an application, we demonstrate that this backreaction naturally produces flat galaxy rotation curves without invoking an additional dark matter component. Our results establish a new perspective on nonlinear structure formation, in which long dynamical range is resolved through a hierarchy of discrete geodesic domains.

### [52] [Cherenkov plasmons emission by primordial neutrinos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00044)
*Maxim Dvornikov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study the emission of Cherenkov plasmons by a thermal neutrino gas with nonzero chemical potential interacting with a nonrelativistic plasma of charged leptons, compute the energy emission rate for longitudinal plasmons using quantum field theory and statistical averaging, and apply the results to the cooling of neutrino clusters in the early universe mediated by a light scalar boson, identifying parameter ranges where this mechanism is efficient.

我们研究了具有非零温度和化学势的中微子气体通过非相对论性带电轻子等离子体发射切伦科夫等离激元的过程，利用量子场论矩阵元与粒子分布函数的平均计算了纵向等离激元的能量辐射率，并将结果应用于早期宇宙中由中微子与假设的轻标量玻色子相互作用形成的中微子团簇的冷却过程，确定了该冷却机制有效的参数范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Neutrino clusters may form in the early universe via interactions with a hypothetical light scalar boson; understanding their cooling mechanisms is essential for assessing their cosmological impact. Since standard model interactions are weak, novel energy loss channels—such as Cherenkov emission of plasmons by neutrinos in a background plasma—are worth exploring.

中微子团簇可能通过与假设的轻标量玻色子相互作用在早期宇宙中形成；理解其冷却机制对于评估其宇宙学影响至关重要。由于标准模型中的相互作用较弱，探索新的能量损失通道（例如中微子在背景等离子体中切伦科夫发射等离激元）具有重要意义。

Method: We calculate the neutrino emissivity by averaging the quantum field theory matrix element for the process $\nu \to \nu + \text{plasmon}$ over Fermi-Dirac distribution functions of incoming and outgoing neutrinos, taking into account temperature and chemical potential. The polarization tensor of the plasma is computed to derive plasmon dispersion relations and form factors. Longitudinal plasmon modes in a nonrelativistic electron plasma are considered, and the Cherenkov condition for emission is imposed.

我们通过对过程 $\nu \to \nu + \text{plasmon}$ 的量子场论矩阵元在入射和出射中微子的费米-狄拉克分布函数上进行平均来计算中微子辐射率，同时考虑温度和化学势的影响。计算了等离子体的极化张量以推导等离激元的色散关系和形状因子，考虑了非相对论性电子等离子体中的纵向等离激元模式，并施加了切伦科夫辐射条件。

Result: The energy emission rate for longitudinal plasmons is derived analytically. We identify the temperature range $T \sim 10^2 - 10^4\,\text{eV}$ where the cooling mechanism is efficient for plausible cluster parameters. The emissivity depends strongly on the neutrino chemical potential and plasma frequency. Calculations of the polarization tensor and plasmon dispersion relations confirm the existence of propagating longitudinal modes satisfying the Cherenkov condition.

推导出了纵向等离激元的能量辐射率的解析表达式。我们确定了在合理团簇参数下该冷却机制有效的温度范围 $T \sim 10^2 - 10^4\,\text{eV}$。辐射率强烈依赖于中微子化学势和等离子体频率。对极化张量和等离激元色散关系的计算证实了满足切伦科夫条件的传播纵向模式的存在。

Conclusion: Cherenkov plasmon emission provides an efficient cooling mechanism for neutrino clusters in the early universe under specific conditions involving a light scalar mediator. This process can significantly influence the thermal evolution of such clusters and should be included in models of exotic dark sector dynamics.

在涉及轻标量媒介子的特定条件下，切伦科夫等离激元辐射为早期宇宙中的中微子团簇提供了一种高效的冷却机制。该过程可显著影响此类团簇的热演化，应被纳入奇异暗区动力学模型中。

Abstract: We study the emission of Cherenkov plasmons by the gas of neutrinos with nonzero temperature and chemical potential. The background plasma, consisting of charged leptons, is taken to be nonrelativistic. The energy emission rate is obtained for longitudinal plasmons. To get the neutrino emissivity we average quantum field theory matrix element over the distribution functions of incoming and outgoing particles. Our results are applied for the description of the cooling down of a neutrino cluster formed in the early universe. Such clusters can exist owing to the neutrino interaction with a hypothetical light scalar boson. Using particular cluster parameters, we demonstrate that the proposed cooling mechanism is efficient for some clusters. We find the temperature range where the proposed cooling channel is valid. Some useful calculations of the polarization tensor, as well as the plasmon form factors and their dispersion relations are also provided.

### [53] [Sterile Neutrinos as a Dynamical Cosmological Fluid: Implications for the Expansion History and Matter-Radiation Equality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00062)
*Poulastya Kar,Bipin Singh Koranga*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We develop an analytic framework modeling sterile neutrinos as a dynamical cosmological fluid with a time-dependent equation of state, going beyond the standard $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ approximation. By solving the Boltzmann equation in an FLRW background, we show that incomplete thermalization leads to a suppressed Fermi-Dirac distribution and compute the resulting energy density and pressure. Sterile neutrinos exhibit relativistic, transition, and matter-like phases, with GeV-scale species behaving effectively as matter at matter-radiation equality, shifting this epoch proportionally to their energy fraction.

我们提出一个解析框架，将惰性中微子建模为具有时变状态方程的动力学宇宙流体，超越了标准的$\Delta N_{\rm eff}$近似。通过在FLRW背景下求解玻尔兹曼方程，我们发现不完全热化导致被抑制的费米-狄拉克分布，并计算相应的能量密度和压强。惰性中微子表现出相对论性、过渡和类物质行为三个阶段，GeV尺度的惰性中微子在物质-辐射等时期表现为有效类物质，使其能量分数成比例地改变等时期。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Sterile neutrinos are well-motivated extensions of the Standard Model, potentially affecting early universe cosmology. The standard treatment assumes a constant $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ with a radiation-like equation of state, but this is insufficient for massive, incompletely thermalized sterile neutrinos whose equation of state evolves. A more accurate description connecting microphysical production mechanisms to cosmological observables is needed.

惰性中微子是标准模型自然的扩展，可能影响早期宇宙演化。标准处理采用恒定$\Delta N_{\rm eff}$并假设类辐射状态方程，但对于质量有限且未完全热化的惰性中微子而言，其状态方程随时间演化，该近似不再适用。需要一个更精确的描述，将微观产生机制与宇宙学观测量联系起来。

Method: Starting from the Boltzmann equation in a Friedmann-Lemaitre-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) universe, we model active-sterile neutrino oscillations with suppressed mixing, leading to partial thermalization. We derive a reduced Fermi-Dirac distribution characterized by a thermalization parameter $\xi < 1$. From this distribution, we compute the time-dependent energy density $\rho_s(a)$ and pressure $p_s(a)$, and incorporate them into the modified Friedmann equations. We analyze the equation of state $w(a) = p_s/\rho_s$ to identify distinct cosmological regimes.

从弗里德曼-勒梅特-罗伯逊-沃尔克（FLRW）宇宙中的玻尔兹曼方程出发，我们建模被抑制的正反中微子-惰性中微子振荡，导致部分热化。我们推导出由热化参数$\xi < 1$表征的被抑制费米-狄拉克分布。由此分布计算时变能量密度$\rho_s(a)$和压强$p_s(a)$，并将其纳入修正的弗里德曼方程。通过分析状态方程$w(a) = p_s/\rho_s$识别不同的宇宙学相态。

Result: We find that sterile neutrinos undergo three phases: (i) an early relativistic phase with $w \approx 1/3$, (ii) a transition phase as they become non-relativistic, and (iii) a late matter-like phase with $w \ll 1$. For GeV-scale sterile neutrinos, they behave effectively as matter at matter-radiation equality, contributing an energy fraction $\Omega_s$ that shifts the equality redshift $z_{\rm eq}$. The shift scales as $\Delta z_{\rm eq} \propto \Omega_s$, differing from the $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ scenario. Current observational bounds constrain $\Omega_s$ to be small.

我们发现惰性中微子经历三个阶段：(i) 早期相对论相态，$w \approx 1/3$；(ii) 过渡相态，当其变为非相对论性时；(iii) 晚期类物质相态，$w \ll 1$。对于GeV尺度惰性中微子，在物质-辐射等时期表现为准类物质，其能量分数$\Omega_s$改变等时期的红移$z_{\rm eq}$，偏移量按$\Delta z_{\rm eq} \propto \Omega_s$缩放，不同于$\Delta N_{\rm eff}$情形。当前观测限制要求$\Omega_s$很小。

Conclusion: The cosmological impact of sterile neutrinos cannot always be captured by a constant $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$. A dynamical fluid description with a time-dependent equation of state is required for massive, partially thermalized species. This framework bridges microphysical production mechanisms and cosmological expansion history, enabling more precise constraints from CMB and large-scale structure observations.

惰性中微子的宇宙学效应不能总是用恒定$\Delta N_{\rm eff}$描述。对于大质量且部分热化的惰性中微子，必须采用具有时变状态方程的动力学流体模型。该框架连接了微观产生机制与宇宙膨胀历史，使来自CMB和大尺度结构观测的更精确限制成为可能。

Abstract: Sterile neutrinos arise naturally in extensions of the Standard Model and can affect cosmological evolution even with subdominant abundance. Their impact is often described by a constant shift in the effective number of relativistic species, Delta Neff, assuming a radiation-like equation of state. However, for finite mass sterile neutrinos with incomplete thermalization, the equation of state evolves with time. In this work, we develop an analytic framework treating sterile neutrinos as a dynamical cosmological fluid with a time-dependent equation of state. Starting from the Boltzmann equation in an expanding Friedmann-Lemaitre-Robertson-Walker background, we show that suppressed active-sterile oscillations lead to a reduced Fermi-Dirac distribution characterized by a thermalization parameter less than unity. We compute the resulting energy density and pressure and incorporate them into the Friedmann equations. We identify distinct regimes, including a relativistic phase, a transition phase, and a matter-like behavior. For GeV scale sterile neutrinos, their contribution at matter-radiation equality is effectively matter-like, shifting the equality epoch in proportion to their energy fraction. Observational constraints indicate that this fraction remains small. This framework connects microscopic production physics to cosmological expansion and goes beyond the standard Delta Neff description.

</details>


### [54] [Improving parton shower predictions via precision moments of energy flow polynomials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00084)
*Benoît Assi,Kyle Lee,Jesse Thaler*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper proposes a maximum-entropy reweighting method to improve parton-shower event samples using high-accuracy theoretical constraints, ensuring positive weights and event exclusivity while enabling broad observational improvements through energy flow polynomials (EFPs).

本文提出了一种基于最大熵重加权的方法，利用高精度理论约束改进部分子喷注事件样本，确保权重为正且保持事件排他性，并通过能量流多项式（EFPs）实现对可观测量的广泛提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Parton showers in event generators often lack precision compared to higher-order calculations; this work aims to bridge the gap by incorporating accurate theoretical constraints into existing shower samples without regenerating events.

事件生成器中的部分子喷注通常缺乏高阶计算的精度；本研究旨在通过将高精度理论约束融入现有喷注样本而不重新生成事件来弥合这一差距。

Method: The authors apply maximum-entropy reweighting with infrared- and collinear-safe constraints built from Energy Flow Polynomials (EFPs), using precision calculations as input to correct a deliberately degraded parton-shower prior. They analyze information transfer to unconstrained observables and test basis reductions guided by collinear power counting.

作者应用基于能量流多项式（EFPs）构建的红外安全和共线安全约束进行最大熵重加权，利用高精度计算作为输入来修正故意降级的部分子喷注先验，并分析信息向未约束可观测量的传递，测试由共线幂次计数指导的基底约化方法。

Result: Even with a degraded parton-shower model, a small set of EFP-based constraints restores physical accuracy across a wide range of observables. Information saturates rapidly, and mixed moments (polynomial + logarithmic) outperform pure bases. Basis reductions via collinear power counting maintain performance.

即使使用降级的部分子喷注模型，少量基于EFP的约束也能恢复大范围可观测量的物理准确性。信息迅速饱和，混合矩（多项式+对数）优于纯基底，通过共线幂次计数的基底约化保持了性能。

Conclusion: Maximum-entropy reweighting with physically motivated, systematically organized constraints (e.g., EFPs) offers a robust and efficient way to upgrade parton-shower predictions, enabling direct use of high-precision theory in full-event simulations.

使用物理动机明确、系统组织的约束（如EFPs）进行最大熵重加权，为提升部分子喷注预测提供了一种稳健高效的方法，使高精度理论可直接用于全事件模拟。

Abstract: In this paper, we study various conceptual and practical aspects of using maximum-entropy reweighting to upgrade parton-shower event samples based on higher-accuracy theoretical constraints. Our approach produces strictly positive per-event weights that improve parton-shower predictions while preserving full event-level exclusivity, allowing any observable to be computed on the reweighted sample without rebinning or regeneration. On the conceptual side, we explain how theoretical principles can help determine which constraints to use and which kinds of priors lead to efficient reweighting. On the practical side, we perform a proof-of-concept study with hemisphere observables in $e^+e^-\!\to$ hadrons, and show that even when the parton-shower prior is purposefully degraded by removing the non-singular parts of the QCD splitting functions, a small set of precision calculations can nevertheless restore the desired physical behavior. We use energy flow polynomials (EFPs) as a systematic basis to organize infrared- and collinear-safe constraints, and study how information transfers from constrained observables to unconstrained ones. We find rapid information saturation, where constraints from a compact set of EFP moments achieve broad improvements across observable space, including for standard hemisphere observables never used in training. Physics-motivated basis reductions guided by collinear power counting achieve comparable performance to complete bases, and mixed moments combining polynomial and logarithmic terms outperform pure alternatives. These results suggest a systematic approach to improving parton-shower event generators, where theoretical constraints of highest accuracy can be translated into full phase-space predictions of experimental relevance.

### [55] [Light-by-light scattering: asymptotic expansions, Coulomb resummation and NLO corrections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00099)
*Ajjath A H,Ekta Chaubey,Hua-Sheng Shao*

光致光散射是QED的基本预言，也是量子场论的敏感探针。LHC上的最新实验观测以及自由电子激光设施即将开展的测量，要求理论预测必须包含完整的质量依赖性、高阶修正以及阈值附近的非微扰效应。

Method: We compute the full fermion-mass-dependent two-loop QED and QCD helicity amplitudes using asymptotic expansions in the high- and low-energy limits. We perform Coulomb resummation in the threshold region to capture bound-state and rescattering effects. The results are implemented in a new Monte Carlo event generator, LbLatNLO, enabling realistic simulations for collider and laser experiments.

Result: We provide improved theoretical predictions for LbL scattering cross sections across a wide energy range, including accurate descriptions near the production threshold. The new event generator LbLatNLO enables NLO-accurate Monte Carlo simulations with full fermion mass dependence and resummed threshold effects.

我们在宽能量范围内提供了改进的光致光散射截面理论预测，包括在产生阈值附近更精确的描述。新的事件生成器LbLatNLO支持具有完整费米子质量依赖性和阈值重求和效应的NLO精度蒙特卡洛模拟。

Conclusion: Our refined calculations and the LbLatNLO generator significantly enhance the precision of LbL scattering predictions in the Standard Model, facilitating comparisons with current and future experiments at the LHC and laser facilities.

我们的改进计算和LbLatNLO生成器显著提升了标准模型中光致光散射预测的精度，有助于与LHC及激光设施当前和未来的实验进行对比。

Abstract: Light-by-light (LbL) scattering is one of the earliest predictions of quantum electrodynamics (QED). Interest in this process has been renewed following its experimental observation at the LHC and the prospects of future measurements at free-electron laser facilities. In this paper, we refine theoretical predictions for LbL scattering by improving the full fermion-mass-dependent two-loop QCD and QED helicity amplitudes using high- and low-energy asymptotic expansions, and by performing Coulomb resummation in the threshold region.
