### [56] [Full positivity bounds for anomalous quartic gauge couplings in SMEFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00107)
*Fu-Ming Chang,Zhuo-Yan Chen,Shuang-Yong Zhou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We derive complete positivity bounds for 22 dimension-8 anomalous quartic gauge couplings (aQGCs) in the SMEFT framework by incorporating all electroweak boson modes, constructing extremal rays of the positivity cone via group theory, and providing a Python package SMEFTaQGC for numerical verification and optimization.

我们通过包含所有电弱玻色子模式，利用群论构建正性锥的极射线，导出了SMEFT框架中22个维度-8反常四规范子耦合（aQGC）的完整正性边界，并提供了用于数值验证和优化的Python工具包SMEFTaQGC。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Deviations in quartic gauge couplings are key signatures of new physics beyond the Standard Model. Previous positivity bounds were limited to transverse vector bosons and incomplete operator sets, leaving gaps in theoretical consistency checks for full SMEFT aQGCs.

四规范子耦合的偏差是超出标准模型新物理的关键信号。以往的正性边界仅限于横向矢量玻色子和不完整的算符集，导致对完整SMEFT aQGC的理论一致性检验存在空白。

Method: We employ a group-theoretic framework to construct the extremal rays (ERs) of the positivity cone for all electroweak boson modes. Two independent methods—direct construction and Casimir operator analysis—are used to handle parity-violating operators and continuous degeneracies. We also develop a Python package, SMEFTaQGC, to automate numerical positivity tests and bound optimization.

我们采用群论框架为所有电弱玻色子模式构建正性锥的极射线（ERs）。使用两种独立方法——直接构造法和Casimir算符分析法——来处理宇称破坏算符和连续简并性。我们还开发了一个Python工具包SMEFTaQGC，以自动化数值正性检验和边界优化。

Result: We obtain the complete set of positivity bounds for all 22 dimension-8 aQGC coefficients. The physically allowed parameter space is reduced to only $0.0313\%$ of the naive total space. We derive analytical linear bounds for various operator combinations and provide algorithms to compute optimized bounds numerically.

我们获得了全部22个维度-8 aQGC系数的完整正性边界。物理允许的参数空间被压缩至仅占原始总空间的$0.0313\%$。我们推导了多种算符组合的解析线性边界，并提供了计算优化边界的算法。

Conclusion: The inclusion of all electroweak boson modes and full group structure leads to significantly stronger positivity constraints on aQGCs, enhancing the predictive power of SMEFT. Our results provide robust theoretical priors for LHC searches and are implemented in the publicly available SMEFTaQGC package for broader application.

包含所有电弱玻色子模式和完整群结构导致对aQGC的正性约束显著增强，提升了SMEFT的预测能力。我们的结果为LHC搜索提供了坚实的理论先验，并已实现在公开可用的SMEFTaQGC工具包中以便广泛应用。

Abstract: Electroweak boson scattering at the LHC provides a crucial avenue for probing physics beyond the Standard Model, particularly regarding deviations in quartic gauge couplings. We derive the complete set of positivity bounds for the $22$ dimension-$8$ anomalous quartic gauge coupling (aQGC) coefficients within the Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT). Moving beyond previous studies limited to transverse vector bosons, our analysis incorporates all electroweak boson modes, explicitly constructing the extremal rays (ERs) of the positivity cone through a group theoretic framework. We utilize two independent methods--direct construction and Casimir operator analysis--to determine these rays, addressing complexities such as parity-violating operators and continuous parameter degeneracies. Our results indicate that the positivity bounds impose severe constraints, restricting the physically viable parameter space to approximately $0.0313\%$ of the naive total space. Furthermore, we derive linear analytical bounds for various operator combinations and provide an easy-to-use Python package, {\tt SMEFTaQGC}, which implements algorithms to numerically verify positivity and compute the optimized positivity bounds for general aQGC configurations.

Result: The notes demonstrate that compact objects serve as powerful natural detectors for WISPs. For axions, resonant conversion in neutron star magnetospheres can produce observable radio signals. Superradiance can lead to massive boson clouds emitting gravitational waves. White dwarfs offer enhanced sensitivity due to high photon-axion mixing in their cores. For HFGWs, novel detection strategies leveraging quantum sensors and astrophysical amplification mechanisms are outlined.

讲义表明，致密天体是探测WISP的强大天然探测器。对于轴子，中子星磁层中的共振转换可产生可观测的无线电信号；超辐射可能导致玻色子云发射引力波；白矮星因其核心的高光子-轴子混合而具有更高灵敏度。对于HFGW，提出了利用量子传感器和天体物理放大机制的新探测策略。

Conclusion: Compact objects provide unique and sensitive probes for axions, ALPs, and high-frequency gravitational waves. The inclusion of exercises enhances their utility for training researchers in the growing field of WISP cosmology.

致密天体为探测轴子、ALP和高频引力波提供了独特且敏感的手段。这些讲义总结了关键理论框架和现象学特征，强调天体物理观测与实验室启发式探测技术之间的协同作用。附带的练习增强了其在WISP宇宙学这一快速发展领域中培训研究人员的实用性。

Abstract: This document is based on lectures delivered at a recent COSMIC WISPers COST Action training school in Annecy in September 2025. They are accompanied by a set of practical exercises. Comments on these notes are gratefully received.

### [58] [A Pati-Salam realization of the Nelson-Barr mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00166)
*Clara Murgui*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper proposes a UV completion of the Standard Model based on SU(4) color unification, where quarks and leptons are unified in a real antisymmetric fermionic representation. This framework simultaneously addresses the strong CP problem via the Nelson-Barr mechanism and corrects down-quark and charged-lepton mass relations for the heaviest generations. The model predicts neutron decay into $K^+ \ell^-$ ($\ell = e, \mu$), testable in Hyper-Kamiokande and DUNE.

本文提出了一种基于SU(4)色统一的Standard Model紫外完备化，其中夸克与轻子通过一个实反对称费米子表示统一。该框架通过Nelson-Barr机制解决强CP问题，并同时修正Pati-Salam理论对最重两代下型夸克与带电轻子质量关系的预言。模型预言了中子衰变$n \to K^+ \ell^-$（$\ell = e, \mu$），可在Hyper-Kamiokande和DUNE实验中检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The strong CP problem and incorrect mass predictions in conventional grand unified theories (e.g., Pati-Salam) motivate the construction of a new UV-complete framework. The authors aim to unify quarks and leptons under SU(4) while solving these issues within a single coherent structure, avoiding fine-tuning and introducing testable predictions.

强CP问题以及传统大统一理论（如Pati-Salam）中不正确的质量预言促使作者构建新的紫外完备框架。目标是在SU(4)下统一夸克与轻子，同时在一个自洽结构中解决这些问题，避免精细调节并引入可检验的预言。

Method: The model extends the Standard Model gauge group with SU(4)$_C$ unification, embedding quarks and leptons into a single real antisymmetric fermion representation. The Nelson-Barr mechanism is implemented via spontaneous CP violation, generating a naturally small effective $\theta$-parameter. Mass corrections arise from symmetry-breaking patterns and Yukawa couplings. Constraints from baryon number violation, neutrino masses, and flavor physics are used to determine key scales: the unification scale, vector-like quark mass, and CP-breaking scale.

该模型通过SU(4)$_C$统一扩展Standard Model规范群，将夸克与轻子嵌入单一实反对称费米子表示。利用自发CP破缺实现Nelson-Barr机制，自然产生小的有效$\theta$参数。质量修正来自对称性破缺模式与Yukawa耦合。通过重子数破缺、中微子质量与味物理的限制确定关键能标：统一能标、矢量型夸克质量与CP破缺能标。

Result: The interplay between the quality of the Nelson-Barr mechanism and absence of observed baryon-number violation fixes the scale of spontaneous CP violation and the mass of the new vector-like down quark. The measured down-quark mass and neutrino mass bounds set the quark-lepton unification scale. The model predicts the observable decay channel $n \to K^+ \ell^-$ ($\ell = e, \mu$), within reach of Hyper-Kamiokande and DUNE.

Nelson-Barr机制的质量与未观测到的重子数破缺过程之间的权衡决定了自发CP破缺能标与新矢量型下夸克的质量。测量得到的下夸克质量与中微子质量上限设定了夸克-轻子统一能标。模型预言可观测的衰变道$n \to K^+ \ell^-$（$\ell = e, \mu$），在Hyper-Kamiokande与DUNE的探测范围内。

Conclusion: The proposed SU(4)$_C$ unified model provides a compelling UV completion of the Standard Model that solves the strong CP problem via the Nelson-Barr mechanism and improves fermion mass predictions. It makes falsifiable predictions for nucleon decay, linking high-scale physics to low-energy observables in a testable way.

所提出的SU(4)$_C$统一模型为Standard Model提供了一个有吸引力的紫外完备化，通过Nelson-Barr机制解决强CP问题并改进费米子质量预言。它对核子衰变做出可证伪的预言，将高能标物理与低能可观测量以可检验的方式联系起来。

Abstract: We present a UV completion of the Standard Model in which quarks and leptons are unified under color SU(4). A single fermionic representation, the real antisymmetric, provides the building blocks to address the strong CP problem via the Nelson-Barr mechanism, while simultaneously correcting the charged-lepton and down-quark mass relations predicted by Pati-Salam theories for the two heaviest generations. We show that the characteristic scales of the theory are strongly constrained by its phenomenology. The interplay between the quality of the Nelson-Barr mechanism and the non-observation of baryon-number-violating processes determines the scale of spontaneous CP violation and the mass of the new vector-like down quark, while the mass of the Standard Model down quark and the upper bound on neutrino masses fix the quark-lepton unification scale. The theory predicts a distinctive baryon-number-violating decay mode of the neutron, $n \to K^+ \ell^-$ (with $\ell = e,μ$), which lies within the projected sensitivity of upcoming nucleon-decay experiments such as Hyper-Kamiokande and DUNE.

### [59] [Next-to-Minimal Freeze-in Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00210)
*Nicolás Bernal,Sagnik Mukherjee,James Unwin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper explores next-to-minimal extensions of Minimal Freeze-in (MFI) Dark Matter, focusing on electroweak doublet and higher SU(2)$_L$ representation fermionic dark matter. It investigates the impact of non-instantaneous reheating and pre-reheating matter-dominated eras on dark matter production, showing how Boltzmann suppression enables revival of otherwise excluded WIMP models and enhances detectability of freeze-in scenarios.

本文探讨了最小冻结产生（Minimal Freeze-in, MFI）暗物质的次最小扩展，聚焦于电弱二重态及更高SU(2)$_L$表示的费米型暗物质。研究了非瞬时再加热以及再加热前宇宙处于物质主导 era 的情景对暗物质产生的影响，表明玻尔兹曼压制机制可复活被排除的WIMP模型，并提升冻结产生类模型的可探测性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard thermal dark matter scenarios face growing experimental constraints, pushing model-building into extreme parameter regimes. The authors aim to revive interest in theoretically well-motivated but experimentally excluded models—such as electroweak doublet fermion dark matter (e.g., Wino-like)—by considering non-standard cosmological histories where the reheating temperature is lower than the dark matter mass, leading to Boltzmann-suppressed production. This opens a new window for both reviving disfavored WIMPs and enhancing the observability of freeze-in dark matter.

标准热暗物质模型面临日益严格的实验限制，迫使理论构建进入极端参数区域。作者旨在通过考虑非标准宇宙学历史——特别是再加热温度低于暗物质质量的情形——来复兴那些理论上有吸引力但被实验排除的模型（如电弱二重态费米子暗物质，例如类似Winio的粒子），此时暗物质产生受到玻尔兹曼压制。这为复活不受欢迎的WIMP模型和增强冻结产生暗物质的可观测性开辟了新窗口。

Method: The authors extend the Minimal Freeze-in (MFI) framework by incorporating time-dependent reheating dynamics, modeling the transition from inflaton domination to radiation domination with arbitrary reheating duration and equation of state. They solve the coupled Boltzmann equations for dark matter number density including inverse decays and scattering processes. For higher SU(2)$_L$ representations, they compute the thermal cross sections and relic abundance using standard finite-temperature field theory techniques, and assess current LHC and direct detection constraints as well as future sensitivities from experiments like HL-LHC and DARWIN.

作者通过引入时间依赖的再加热动力学来扩展最小冻结产生（MFI）框架，模拟从暴胀子主导到辐射主导的转变过程，允许任意的再加热持续时间和状态方程。他们求解包含逆衰变和散射过程的暗物质数密度耦合玻尔兹曼方程。对于更高的SU(2)$_L$表示，使用标准有限温度场论技术计算热截面和遗迹丰度，并评估当前LHC和直接探测实验的限制以及HL-LHC和DARWIN等未来实验的探测灵敏度。

Result: For non-instantaneous reheating, especially in matter-dominated pre-reheating scenarios, the dark matter yield can be significantly enhanced due to prolonged periods of low temperature, amplifying Boltzmann-suppressed production. For $\mathbf{5}$ and $\mathbf{7}$-plet fermionic dark matter under SU(2)$_L$, the correct relic abundance can be achieved with masses around several TeV, evading current LHC bounds while remaining within reach of future direct detection experiments such as DARWIN. The interplay between cosmological history and particle physics allows previously excluded parameter space to become viable.

在非瞬时再加热情形下，特别是在再加热前物质主导的情况下，由于长时间低温环境，暗物质产额显著增加，从而放大了玻尔兹曼压制下的产生效应。对于SU(2)$_L$下的五重态（$\mathbf{5}$）和七重态（$\mathbf{7}$）费米子暗物质，可在数TeV质量附近实现正确的遗迹丰度，避开当前LHC限制的同时仍处于DARWIN等未来直接探测实验的可达范围。宇宙学历史与粒子物理之间的协同作用使得此前被排除的参数空间重新变得可行。

Conclusion: Boltzmann-suppressed dark matter production in non-standard cosmological histories provides a compelling alternative to conventional thermal freeze-out and freeze-in mechanisms. Next-to-minimal extensions of MFI dark matter, particularly with larger SU(2)$_L$ representations and realistic reheating dynamics, open new avenues for model building and experimental discovery. These scenarios predict potentially observable signals in upcoming colliders and direct detection experiments, bridging high-scale particle theory with cosmological observations.

在非标准宇宙学历史中，受玻尔兹曼压制的暗物质产生机制为传统的热冻结和冻结产生机制提供了有吸引力的替代方案。MFI暗物质的次最小扩展，特别是结合更大的SU(2)$_L$表示和更真实的再加热动力学，为模型构建和实验发现开辟了新途径。这些情景预测了在未来的对撞机和直接探测实验中可能观测到的信号，连接了高能粒子理论与宇宙学观测。

Abstract: If the dark matter mass exceeds the highest temperature of the thermal bath, then dark matter production is Boltzmann suppressed. This opens new possibilities for dark matter model building. In particular, WIMP models that are experimentally excluded can be revived in this setting; conversely, freeze-in models, which would typically be beyond experimental reach, are potentially discoverable in the Boltzmann suppressed regime. In a recent letter, we highlighted these aspects for the case of electroweak doublet fermion dark matter assuming instantaneous inflationary reheating. Due to its elegance and simplicity, we coin this {\em Minimal Freeze-in} (MFI) Dark Matter. Here we consider next-to-minimal extensions of MFI dark matter. We present the implications for non-instantaneous reheating, including scenarios beyond the standard picture in which the Universe is initially matter dominated prior to reheating. Furthermore, we explore model variations within the electroweak dark matter scenario. Specifically, we consider fermion dark matter in higher representations of SU(2)${}_L$, exploring the current limits and the near-future discovery potential.

</details>


### [60] [Number Theory in Quantum Physics: Minicharged Particles and the Prouhet-Tarry-Escott Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12320)
*Junseok Lee,Fuminobu Takahashi,Yu-Dai Tsai*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper establishes a novel connection between anomaly cancellation in quantum gauge theories and the degree $k=3$ Prouhet-Tarry-Escott problem in number theory, showing that at least four minicharged states are required in the hidden sector.

本文建立了一个量子规范理论中反常相消与数论中$k=3$阶Prouhet-Tarry-Escott问题之间的新联系，表明隐藏部门必须包含至少四个微小电荷态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the constraints on light minicharged particles from quantum consistency (anomaly cancellation) in gauge theories, and to explore whether mathematical structures in number theory can provide insight into viable particle spectra.

为了从量子一致性（反常相消）的角度理解轻微小电荷粒子所受的限制，并探索数论中的数学结构是否能为可行的粒子谱提供洞见。

Method: The authors map the anomaly cancellation conditions in a phenomenologically motivated model of minicharged particles to Diophantine equations, identifying them with the Prouhet-Tarry-Escott problem of degree $k=3$. They analyze minimal ideal solutions to this number-theoretic problem and relate them to the required number and mass structure of minicharged states.

作者将一个现象学动机下的微小电荷粒子模型中的反常相消条件映射到丢番图方程，识别出其等价于$k=3$阶Prouhet-Tarry-Escott问题。他们分析了该数论问题的最小理想解，并将其与所需微小电荷态的数量和质量结构相关联。

Result: Anomaly cancellation is equivalent to solving the $k=3$ Prouhet-Tarry-Escott problem, which requires at least four minicharged states. Minimal ideal solutions predict a near-degenerate doublet mass spectrum, suggesting that discovering one minicharged particle implies the existence of a partner with nearly the same mass and identical minicharge.

反常相消等价于求解$k=3$阶Prouhet-Tarry-Escott问题，这要求至少存在四个微小电荷态。最小理想解预言了一种近简并双重态的质量谱，意味着发现一个微小电荷粒子即暗示着另一个具有相近质量和相同微小电荷的伴粒存在。

Conclusion: There is a deep and unexpected connection between quantum consistency in gauge theories and number theory. This correspondence constrains model building with minicharged particles and predicts specific spectral patterns—such as near-degenerate doublets—that could guide future experimental searches.

规范理论中的量子一致性与数论之间存在深刻且意外的联系。这一对应关系约束了微小电荷粒子的模型构建，并预言了诸如近简并双重态等特定谱型，可指导未来的实验搜索。

Abstract: In quantum gauge theories, anomaly cancellation severely restricts the allowed patterns of chiral charges. Here we show that, in a phenomenologically motivated framework for light minicharged particles, the anomaly cancellation conditions are equivalent to the degree $k=3$ Prouhet-Tarry-Escott problem in number theory. This correspondence immediately implies that the hidden sector must contain at least four minicharged states. For constructions based on minimal ideal solutions, the mass spectrum generically exhibits a near-degenerate doublet structure, so that the discovery of one minicharged particle would point to a partner state with the same minicharge and a nearby mass. Our results uncover an unexpected link between quantum consistency and number theory, with direct implications for model building and future searches.

### [61] [Dilepton Correlations from Heavy Flavor Decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00367)
*T. Dahms,R. Vogt*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This study extends previous analyses of heavy flavor hadron correlations in $p+p$ collisions to lepton pairs from semileptonic decays, using the \textsc{HVQMNR} code at RHIC and LHC energies. It finds that NLO calculations reproduce PHENIX data, with a shift in azimuthal correlation peak from $\Delta\phi \sim \pi$ to $\sim 0$ as $p_T$ increases at 13 TeV, and that bottom quark contributions dominate. The effect of $k_T$ broadening is reduced by decay kinematics, yet decay leptons retain memory of initial hadronic correlations.

本研究将此前在$p+p$碰撞中对重味强子关联的分析扩展到半轻衰变产生的轻子对，使用\textsc{HVQMNR}代码在RHIC和LHC能量下进行计算。研究发现NLO计算结果与PHENIX数据趋势一致，在13 TeV时随着$p_T$增加，方位角关联峰从$\Delta\phi \sim \pi$移至$\sim 0$，底夸克贡献占主导。$k_T$展宽效应因衰变运动学而减弱，但衰变轻子仍保留了初态强子关联的部分记忆。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to extend baseline studies of heavy flavor hadron azimuthal correlations in $p+p$ collisions to dileptons from semileptonic decays, providing a foundation for investigating such signals in $p+A$ and $A+A$ collisions where thermal dilepton production is a key probe of early-time medium dynamics. Understanding these correlations helps disentangle prompt heavy-flavor signals from thermal background in heavy-ion collisions.

研究动机是将此前在$p+p$碰撞中关于重味强子方位角关联的研究基线扩展到半轻衰变产生的双轻子，为在$p+A$和$A+A$碰撞中研究此类信号奠定基础，其中热双轻子产生是探测介质早期动力学的关键手段。理解这些关联有助于在重离子碰撞中区分来自热背景的本底与重味信号。

Method: Azimuthal correlations between leptons from semileptonic decays of heavy flavor hadrons are calculated using the exclusive \textsc{HVQMNR} code, which includes next-to-leading order (NLO) QCD contributions. Calculations are performed within PHENIX acceptance at $\sqrt{s} = 200$~GeV and for dielectron measurements in ALICE at $\sqrt{s} = 13$~TeV. Like-sign lepton pairs are used to subtract $b\bar{b}$ decay backgrounds from opposite-sign signals, and the sensitivity to $k_T$ broadening is examined.

使用包含下圈（NLO）QCD贡献的专用\textsc{HVQMNR}程序计算来自重味强子半轻衰变的轻子间方位角关联。计算在PHENIX接受度下于$\sqrt{s} = 200$~GeV进行，并针对ALICE在$\sqrt{s} = 13$~TeV下的双电子测量开展。利用同号轻子对减除$b\bar{b}$衰变对异号信号的背景贡献，并研究信号对$k_T$展宽的敏感性。

Result: Next-to-leading order calculations describe the trends in PHENIX data well. At $\sqrt{s} = 13$~TeV, increasing the dielectron $p_T$ shifts the $\Delta\phi$ correlation peak from $\sim\pi$ to $\sim0$, indicating a transition in the dominant production mechanism. Bottom quark decays become increasingly dominant at higher $p_T$. The sensitivity to $k_T$ broadening — previously noted in hadron-level studies — is significantly reduced due to decay kinematics, though some memory of the parent hadron correlations persists in the lepton correlations.

下圈计算较好地再现了PHENIX数据的趋势。在$\sqrt{s} = 13$~TeV时，随着双电子$p_T$增加，$\Delta\phi$关联峰从$\sim\pi$移向$\sim0$，表明主导产生机制发生转变。高$p_T$下底夸克衰变贡献逐渐占优。尽管此前在强子层面观察到显著的$k_T$展宽敏感性，但由于衰变运动学效应，该敏感性在轻子层面大幅降低，然而轻子关联中仍保留部分母强子关联的记忆。

Conclusion: The study concludes that while $k_T$ broadening effects are suppressed in dilepton correlations due to decay dynamics, azimuthal correlations between decay leptons still reflect those of their parent heavy flavor hadrons in $p+p$ collisions. However, in $A+A$ collisions, extracting this signal requires separation from thermal dilepton production in the same low-mass region, posing a challenge for future heavy-ion measurements.

研究得出结论：尽管由于衰变动学，$k_T$展宽效应在双轻子关联中被抑制，但衰变轻子间的方位角关联仍能反映其母体重味强子在$p+p$碰撞中的关联特性。然而，在$A+A$碰撞中提取该信号需将其与同一低质量区域内的热双轻子产生区分开来，这对未来的重离子测量提出了挑战。

Abstract: Background: Azimuthal correlations between heavy flavor hadrons have been previously studied in $p+p$ collisions (Phys. Rev. C {\bf 98}, 034907 (2018), {\bf 101}, 034910 (2020)). These studies found good agreement with the data and provide a baseline for further studies in $p+A$ and $A+A$ collisions. Purpose: This work extends those studies to heavy flavor hadron decays to low mass lepton pairs. The low mass dilepton region is important for heavy ion collisions because of the interest in thermal dilepton production as a signature of the early time dynamics of the medium. Methods: Building on previous work, azimuthal correlations between leptons from semileptonic decays of heavy flavor hadrons are examined. The exclusive \textsc{HVQMNR} code is used in the calculations, made in the PHENIX acceptance at $\sqrt{s} = 200$~GeV and for dielectrons in ALICE at $\sqrt{s} = 13$~TeV. The $b \overline b$ decay contributions subtract like-sign lepton pairs from the opposite-sign signal. Results: The next-to-leading order calculations reproduce the trends of the PHENIX data. The calculations at 13~TeV show a change in signal as electron pair $p_T$ is increased, with the peak of the $Δφ$ distribution moving from $Δφ\sim π$ to $\sim 0$ and the contribution from bottom decays becoming dominant. The sensitivity of the signal to $k_T$ broadening is also studied and found to be small. Conclusions: It is found that the dependence on $k_T$ broadening previously observed is significantly reduced by the decay process. Despite this, the correlations between decay leptons retains some memory of the correlations between the parent hadrons in $p+p$ collisions. However, to study these correlations in heavy-ion collisions, it is necessary to separate them from thermal dilepton production in the same mass region.

</details>


### [62] [Motivation and design of a yotta-eV $τ^+τ^-$ collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00440)
*Matt Bellis,Matthew Carberg,Chester Gould,Jackson Ingenito,Fasiha Khaliq,Emely Kintzel,Shane Kirschmann,Neha Matta,Sophia Pavia,Emmett Pearl,Payton Ramsdill,Grace Scherer,Cullen Wright*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper proposes a futuristic tau-collider colliding oppositely-charged $\tau$-leptons at yotta-eV energies, with a potential location in the Oort cloud, arguing it should become the long-term focus of the particle physics community despite requiring advanced technological development.

本文提出了一种未来的陶子对撞机（tau-collider），在yotta-eV能量下对撞带相反电荷的$\tau$轻子，可能位于奥尔特云中，尽管需要先进的技术发展，但仍主张粒子物理界应将其作为长期发展目标。

动机是追求超越当前及近期对撞机（如LHC和HL-LHC）能力的希格斯物理精确研究和新粒子搜索，主张比拟议中的缪子对撞机更宏大的长期愿景。

Method: The method involves a conceptual design of a $\tau^+\tau^-$ collider operating at yotta-eV ($10^{24}$ eV) energy scales, potentially situated in the Oort cloud, leveraging the unique properties of $\tau$-leptons for high-energy collisions. 方法包括在yotta-eV（$10^{24}$ eV）能量尺度上运行的$\tau^+\tau^-$对撞机的概念设计，可能位于奥尔特云中，利用$\tau$轻子的独特性质进行高能碰撞，并考虑文明级别的技术进步（卡尔达肖夫I/II级）。

Result: No experimental results are presented; the paper establishes a speculative but physically motivated proposal for a future collider that would require breakthroughs in accelerator technology, space engineering, and possibly human civilization advancement.

未提供实验结果；本文提出了一个具有物理动机但属推测性的未来对撞机方案，其实现需要加速器技术、空间工程乃至人类文明发展的重大突破。

Conclusion: The authors conclude that the particle physics community should begin R\&D toward a tau-collider now, despite its immense technical challenges and distant timeline, because of its unparalleled discovery potential for fundamental physics.

作者得出结论：尽管陶子对撞机面临巨大技术挑战且时间遥远，但由于其在基础物理发现方面的无与伦比潜力，粒子物理界应立即启动相关研发工作。

Abstract: Two significant goals of the particle physics community is the precision study of the Higgs boson and the search for new particles. The Large Hadron Collider (LHC) is the current high-energy collider, soon to be superseded by the High-Luminosity LHC (HL-LHC). Much of the community has rallied around a muon-collider, though that is most likely 25 years in the future. In this paper, we argue for a bolder approach: {\it a tau-collider}, in which oppositely-charged $τ$-leptons are collided with energies on the yotta-eV scale and a potential radius that places it in the Oort cloud. Given the long time-scale and significant construction challenges, we strongly suggest the focus of the community shift to this discovery machine. We acknowledge that the technology necessary may require humanity to evolve to a Kardashev Level-I or Level-II civilization, which is all the more reason to begin R\&D now.

### [63] [Universal features of high-energy scattering of Laguerre-Gaussian states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00575)
*Yaoqi Yang,Igor P. Ivanov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This work systematically studies scattering of high-energy vortex states using paraxial Laguerre-Gaussian wave packets colliding with non-zero impact parameter $b$, focusing on the dependence of the differential cross section on the total final transverse momentum $P_\perp$. It identifies universal kinematic features arising from the wave packet structure, highlighting the importance of $b$ as a probe of vortex states.

本文系统研究了具有非零碰撞参数$b$的抛物线近似拉盖尔-高斯波包在高能涡旋态散射中的应用，重点关注微分截面对最终总横向动量$P_\perp$的依赖性。研究识别出来自波包结构的普适运动学特征，强调$b$作为探测涡旋态的重要工具而非干扰因素的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Vortex states offer new degrees of freedom in scattering experiments due to their orbital angular momentum; however, most theoretical treatments rely on idealized assumptions not easily realizable experimentally. This paper aims to re-analyze vortex-state scattering under more realistic conditions—specifically, using Laguerre-Gaussian (LG) wave packets with non-zero impact parameter $b$—to bridge theory and future experimental feasibility.

涡旋态因其轨道角动量为散射实验提供了新的自由度；然而，大多数理论处理基于理想化假设，难以在实验中实现。本文旨在更现实的条件下重新分析涡旋态散射——特别是使用具有非零碰撞参数$b$的拉盖尔-高斯（LG）波包——以弥合理论与未来实验可行性之间的差距。

Method: The authors employ paraxial Laguerre-Gaussian (LG) wave packets to model vortex states and calculate the differential cross section for scattering processes with non-zero impact parameter $b$. They analyze how the total final transverse momentum $P_\perp$ depends on both the geometry of the collision (via $b$) and the shape of the wave packets, separating universal kinematic effects from process-specific dynamics.

作者采用抛物线近似下的拉盖尔-高斯（LG）波包来建模涡旋态，并计算具有非零碰撞参数$b$的散射过程的微分截面。他们分析了最终总横向动量$P_\perp$如何依赖于碰撞几何（通过$b$）和波包形状，将普适的运动学效应与特定过程的动力学分开。

Result: The study reveals that non-trivial $P_\perp$-dependent features in the differential cross section arise from the structure of LG wave packets, even without considering specific scattering dynamics. The non-zero impact parameter $b$ plays a significant role in shaping these features, making it a valuable experimental observable rather than a complication.

研究表明，即使不考虑具体的散射动力学，拉盖尔-高斯波包的结构也会在微分截面中产生显著的$P_\perp$相关特征。非零碰撞参数$b$在形成这些特征中起着重要作用，使其成为有价值的可观测量而非复杂性来源。

Conclusion: The impact parameter $b$ is a crucial variable in vortex-state scattering, enabling the observation of universal kinematic features in the $P_\perp$-dependence of the differential cross section. This paves the way for more realistic theoretical modeling of vortex-particle collisions and highlights $b$ as a useful probe in future experiments.

碰撞参数$b$是涡旋态散射中的关键变量，能够揭示微分截面$P_\perp$依赖关系中的普适运动学特征。这为更现实的涡旋粒子碰撞理论建模铺平了道路，并凸显$b$在未来实验中作为有效探针的价值。

Abstract: Vortex states of photons, electrons, and other particles are wave packets that carry intrinsic orbital angular momentum (OAM) and exhibit other features unavailable for plane waves. Collisions of high-energy vortex states can become a promising tool for nuclear and particle physics, once experimental challenges are overcome. An extensive literature exists on scattering processes involving vortex states; however, most works rely on assumptions that will be challenging to achieve in experiment. In this work, we initiate a systematic re-analysis of vortex-state scattering processes using paraxial Laguerre-Gaussian (LG) wave packets colliding at a non-zero impact parameter $b$. Since the total final transverse momentum $P_\perp$ is no longer fixed, we focus on how the differential cross section depends on $P_\perp$. We emphasize that non-trivial $P_\perp$-dependent features can originate either from the shape of the LG wave packets or from the dynamics of the scattering process under interest. Here, we focus on the former source and explore in detail these universal kinematic features, while the study of process-specific modifications, along with the novel insights they may bring, is delegated to a future work. Interestingly, the non-zero impact parameter $b$ plays a key role in many $P_\perp$-dependent effects, making it a useful probe of vortex states, not a nuisance factor as often assumed.

### [64] [Searching for New Physics Inside Jets with the Herwig 7 Generalised Parton Shower](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00617)
*Taehee Kim,Joon-Bin Lee,M. R. Masouminia,Michael H. Seymour,Un-ki Yang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper explores the production of a massive $Z'$ boson within parton showers in both the Standard Model (SM) and beyond-the-Standard-Model (BSM) contexts, using the Herwig 7 framework. Unlike conventional direct production, $Z'$ bosons produced via shower emissions appear inside jets, enabling new search strategies through jet substructure. The study focuses on the $U(1)_{B{\rm -}L}$ model, evaluates SM/BSM shower interplay, and identifies discriminants against QCD and other backgrounds, projecting detectability at current and future colliders.

本文研究了在部分子喷注（parton shower）演化中产生大质量$Z'$玻色子的现象，涵盖标准模型（SM）和超出标准模型（BSM）辐射。与传统直接产生机制不同，$Z'$可通过喷注内的后续辐射在喷注内部产生，从而通过喷注子结构开辟新的新物理探测途径。研究采用Herwig 7框架，在$U(1)_{B{\rm -}L}$模型下分析SM与BSM喷注的相互作用，识别出可区分于QCD等背景的独特运动学特征，并评估了LHC及未来对撞机的探测灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional searches for $Z'$ bosons rely on resonant production in the hard scattering process, limiting sensitivity to high-mass or strongly coupled scenarios. However, weakly coupled or lower-mass $Z'$ bosons may evade detection if produced outside isolated leptonic channels. Allowing $Z'$ radiation in the parton shower enables access to otherwise inaccessible parameter space, particularly where logarithmic enhancements amplify BSM emission rates. This motivates a systematic study of $Z'$ production within jets, leveraging modern event generators and jet substructure techniques to uncover hidden signatures.

传统$Z'$搜索依赖于硬散射过程中的共振产生，限制了对高能或强耦合情形的敏感性。然而，弱耦合或低质量$Z'$若不在孤立轻子道中产生则可能逃逸探测。允许$Z'$在部分子喷注中辐射可打开新的参数空间，特别是在对数增强显著提升BSM辐射率的情况下。因此，亟需系统研究喷注内$Z'$产生的现象学，利用现代事例生成器和喷注子结构技术挖掘隐藏信号。

Method: The study employs the Herwig 7 Monte Carlo event generator, extended to support BSM parton showers, to simulate $Z'$ emission within QCD-like shower evolution. A minimal $U(1)_{B{\rm -}L}$ model is used as a benchmark, with $Z'$ coupling to baryon minus lepton number. Full event simulation includes both SM and BSM shower branching, interference effects, and hadronization. Jet clustering is performed using the anti-$k_t$ algorithm, and substructure variables (e.g., $N$-subjettiness, energy correlation functions) are computed. Backgrounds from QCD, top-quark, and Drell-Yan processes are simulated for comparison. Statistical significance is estimated using asymptotic formulae based on signal and background yields in optimized selection windows.

研究采用支持BSM部分子喷注的Herwig 7蒙特卡洛事例生成器，模拟在类QCD喷注演化中$Z'$的辐射。以最小$U(1)_{B{\rm -}L}$模型为基准，其中$Z'$耦合到重子数减去轻子数。完整事例模拟包含SM与BSM喷注分支、干涉效应及强子化过程。使用anti-$k_t$算法进行喷注聚类，并计算子结构变量（如$N$-subjettiness、能量关联函数）。同时模拟QCD、顶夸克和Drell-Yan过程作为背景。基于优化选择窗口内的信号与背景产额，采用渐近公式估算统计显著性。

Result: It is found that $Z'$ bosons can be efficiently radiated within jets when kinematically allowed, particularly in the low-to-moderate transverse momentum regime ($p_T \sim 100~\mathrm{GeV} - 1~\mathrm{TeV}$). These $Z'$-induced jets exhibit distinct substructure due to the two-body decay of the $Z'$, enhancing sensitivity to $N$-subjettiness ratios and energy correlation functions. Discrimination from QCD jets is achievable with moderate background rejection. For the $U(1)_{B{\rm -}L}$ model, LHC with $3000~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ could probe $Z'$ masses up to $\sim 2.5~\mathrm{TeV}$ and couplings down to $g_{B{\rm -}L} \sim 0.1$, while future $10~\mathrm{TeV}$ proton-proton colliders may extend reach to $\sim 8~\mathrm{TeV}$.

研究发现，当运动学允许时，$Z'$可在喷注内高效辐射，尤其在中低横动量区域（$p_T \sim 100~\mathrm{GeV} - 1~\mathrm{TeV}$）。由$Z'$两体衰变导致的喷注表现出明显的子结构特征，体现在$N$-subjettiness比值和能量关联函数上，可实现对QCD喷注的适度本底抑制。对于$U(1)_{B{\rm -}L}$模型，LHC在$3000~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$积分亮度下可探测至$Z'$质量约$2.5~\mathrm{TeV}$、耦合强度低至$g_{B{\rm -}L} \sim 0.1$，而未来的$10~\mathrm{TeV}$质子对撞机可将探测上限扩展至约$8~\mathrm{TeV}$。

Conclusion: Parton shower production of $Z'$ bosons provides a novel and complementary channel for BSM searches, especially for weakly coupled or lower-mass states that avoid traditional resonance searches. The implementation of BSM showers in Herwig 7 enables realistic simulations of such scenarios. Jet substructure observables offer powerful discrimination tools, and projections indicate significant discovery potential at current and future colliders, motivating dedicated experimental analyses targeting non-isolated, internally decaying BSM bosons in jets.

部分子喷注中产生$Z'$玻色子为BSM搜索提供了新颖且互补的通道，尤其适用于逃逸传统共振搜索的弱耦合或低质量态。Herwig 7中BSM喷注的实现使得此类情景的精确模拟成为可能。喷注子结构观测量提供了强大的区分能力，预测显示当前及未来对撞机具有显著的发现潜力，激励实验界开展专门针对喷注内非孤立、内部衰变BSM玻色子的分析。

Abstract: This study investigates parton shower evolution incorporating both Standard Model (SM) and beyond-the-Standard-Model (BSM) radiation, focusing on the phenomenology of a massive $Z'$ boson. While traditional approaches typically assume direct $Z'$ production in the hard process, the possibility of $Z'$ production within jets, enabled by subsequent emissions in the parton shower, offers a complementary opportunity to probe new physics through jet substructure and event topology. The newly developed Herwig 7 framework supporting BSM parton showers enables efficient simulation of $Z'$ production in the logarithmically enhanced regime. Using a simple BSM benchmark, the minimal $U(1)_{B{\rm -}L}$ extension of the SM, the interplay between the SM and BSM showers is evaluated to identify kinematic features that distinguish $Z'$-induced jets from conventional signatures. BSM-radiation signatures are contrasted with SM backgrounds such as QCD, top-quark, and Drell-Yan production, identifying potential discriminants for experimental searches. Experimental sensitivity at the LHC and prospective future colliders is estimated via statistical-significance projections. We find that $Z'$ bosons produced through parton shower radiation populate non-isolated regions inside jets, providing an avenue for new-physics searches overlooked in traditional analyses.

</details>


### [65] [Hyperon non-leptonic decays in relativistic Chiral Perturbation Theory with resonances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00646)
*Nora Salone,Fernando Alvarado,Stefan Leupold,Andrzej Kupsc*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Non-leptonic hyperon decays are computed in relativistic Chiral Perturbation Theory at next-to-leading order (NLO), including explicit loop corrections and resonance saturation of weak low-energy constants using $1/2^-$ and excited $1/2^+$ octets; a combined fit to $s$- and $p$-wave amplitudes is achieved, highlighting the importance of resonances.

非轻子超子衰变在相对论性手征微扰理论的下一阶（NLO）中首次被计算，包括基于$1/2^-$和激发态$1/2^+$八重态的显式圈图修正和弱低能常数的共振饱和；通过对$s$波和$p$波振幅的联合拟合，突出了共振态的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent experimental advances in measuring non-leptonic hyperon decays motivate a more precise theoretical treatment within Chiral Perturbation Theory, particularly using a relativistic framework beyond previous heavy-baryon approaches.

最近在非轻子超子衰变测量方面的实验进展，促使在手征微扰理论中采用更精确的理论处理方法，特别是使用超越以往重子重子方法的相对论框架。

Method: The calculation is performed in relativistic Baryon Chiral Perturbation Theory at NLO, including loop contributions from ground-state octet and decuplet baryons. The NLO weak-transition low-energy constants (LECs) are estimated via resonance saturation using $1/2^-$ and excited $1/2^+$ resonance octets, inspired by non-relativistic tree-level results. Remaining parameters are fitted to experimental decay amplitudes.

该计算在相对论性重子手征微扰理论的NLO下进行，包含来自基态八重态和十重态重子的圈图贡献。NLO弱跃迁低能常数（LECs）通过使用$1/2^-$和激发态$1/2^+$共振八重态的共振饱和来估计，灵感来自非相对论性树图结果。剩余参数通过拟合实验衰变振幅确定。

Result: A good combined fit to both $s$- and $p$-wave amplitudes is achieved, though the constraints on parameters are not very tight. Resonance contributions, especially from $1/2^-$ and excited $1/2^+$ states, are found to be crucial for describing the data.

对$s$波和$p$波振幅的联合拟合效果良好，尽管参数约束并不十分紧密。共振贡献，特别是来自$1/2^-$和激发态$1/2^+$态的贡献，对于描述数据至关重要。

Conclusion: Relativistic Chiral Perturbation Theory at NLO provides a viable framework for non-leptonic hyperon decays. Resonance saturation plays a key role in estimating LECs, and further experimental precision will help tighten constraints on the unknown parameters. Open questions remain regarding convergence and the inclusion of higher-order effects.

NLO下的相对论性手征微扰理论为非轻子超子衰变提供了一个可行的框架。共振饱和在估计低能常数（LECs）中起着关键作用，未来更高的实验精度将有助于收紧对未知参数的约束。关于收敛性和高阶效应的纳入仍存在开放性问题。

Abstract: Motivated by recent experimental advances in the corresponding measurements, non-leptonic hyperon decays are calculated, for the first time in a relativistic manner, in Chiral Perturbation Theory at next-to-leading order (NLO). On the one hand, relativistic loop corrections are computed explicitly based on the ground-state octet and decuplet fields. On the other hand, the NLO weak-transition low-energy constants are estimated by resonance saturation, inspired by the non-relativistic tree-level computation of Ref. [1]. In particular, the $1/2^-$ and the (excited) $1/2^+$ resonance octets are utilized. The remaining unknown parameters are fitted to the decay amplitudes. A good combined fit to both $s$- and $p$-wave amplitudes is achieved with the caveat of not being very tightly constrained. The role of the resonances is found to be crucial. Consequences for further investigations and open questions are addressed.

### [66] [Baryogenesis in $SU(2)_{L}$ multiplet models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00649)
*Kiyoto Ogawa,Masanori Tanaka*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study baryogenesis in SM extensions with new $SU(2)_L$ multiplet fields via sphalerogenesis, where the baryon asymmetry is generated through CP-violating electroweak sphaleron-like processes. The presence of CP-violating Yukawa couplings generates a dimension-six operator involving $SU(2)_L$ gauge fields, enabling successful baryogenesis at the TeV scale. Models with fermionic quintuplets and septuplets are analyzed, yielding testable predictions for EDMs and collider searches.

我们研究了通过新引入的$SU(2)_L$多重态场实现标准模型扩展中的重子生成，聚焦于‘ sphalerogenesis’机制——即宇宙重子不对称性（BAU）由CP破坏的电弱 sphaleron 类过程逐渐解耦而产生。当新场具有CP破坏的Yukawa相互作用时，会在低能下留下涉及$SU(2)_L$规范场的CP破坏六维算符，从而再生观测到的BAU。以费米型五重态和七重态为例，发现这些场的质量需为$\mathcal{O}(1)\,\mathrm{TeV}$量级。参数空间与当前电子电偶极矩限制一致，并可在ACME III和HL-LHC单轻子搜寻中被充分探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The origin of the baryon asymmetry of the Universe (BAU) remains unexplained within the Standard Model (SM), which fails to satisfy all three Sakharov conditions. We aim to construct a viable baryogenesis mechanism by extending the SM with $SU(2)_L$ multiplet fields, leveraging enhanced sphaleron-like dynamics and new sources of CP violation beyond the CKM phase.

宇宙重子不对称性（BAU）的起源在标准模型（SM）内无法解释，因SM不能满足全部三个Sakharov条件。我们的目标是通过引入$SU(2)_L$多重态场扩展SM，利用增强的sphaleron类动力学以及超出CKM相位的新CP破坏源，构建一个可行的重子生成机制。

Method: We consider SM extensions with heavy fermionic $SU(2)_L$ multiplets (e.g., quintuplets and septuplets) that have CP-violating Yukawa interactions. Integrating out these fields generates a CP-violating dimension-six operator $\frac{\alpha_2}{8\pi} \frac{\phi}{f} W_{\mu\nu}^a \tilde{W}^{a\mu\nu}$, which modifies the sphaleron energy barrier and induces a bias in baryon number violation. The time evolution of this axion-like field $\phi$ during EW symmetry breaking leads to a net BAU via adiabatic turning off of sphaleron transitions. Boltzmann equations are solved to track the asymmetry generation, while constraints from electron EDM and HL-LHC mono-lepton searches are evaluated.

我们考虑包含具有CP破坏Yukawa相互作用的重费米型$SU(2)_L$多重态（如五重态、七重态）的标准模型扩展。积出这些场后生成一个CP破坏的六维算符 $\frac{\alpha_2}{8\pi} \frac{\phi}{f} W_{\mu\nu}^a \tilde{W}^{a\mu\nu}$，该算符修改sphaleron能垒并在重子数破坏过程中引入偏向。在电弱对称性破缺期间，类轴子场$\phi$的时间演化导致sphaleron跃迁被绝热关闭，从而产生净BAU。通过求解Boltzmann方程追踪不对称性的生成，并评估来自电子电偶极矩和HL-LHC单轻子搜寻的限制。

Result: Successful baryogenesis requires the mass scale of the new $SU(2)_L$ multiplets to be $\mathcal{O}(1)\,\mathrm{TeV}$, making them accessible at current and future colliders. The generated BAU matches observations for reasonable values of CP-violating phases. The model predicts observable electron EDM signals within reach of ACME III, while remaining consistent with current limits. Mono-lepton + missing energy signatures at HL-LHC provide complementary probes.

成功的重子生成要求新的$SU(2)_L$多重态质量在$\mathcal{O}(1)\,\mathrm{TeV}$量级，使其可在当前及未来的对撞机上探测。对于合理的CP破坏相位值，所生成的BAU与观测一致。该模型预测的电子电偶极矩信号可被ACME III探测，同时仍符合当前实验限制。HL-LHC上的单轻子+缺失能量信号提供了互补探测手段。

Conclusion: Sphalerogenesis in $SU(2)_L$ multiplet extensions provides a testable ultraviolet completion of baryogenesis, linking TeV-scale physics to the observed BAU. The interplay between low-energy precision tests (e.g., EDMs) and high-energy collider searches offers a powerful avenue for probing such scenarios.

在$SU(2)_L$多重态扩展中的sphalerogenesis为重子生成提供了一个可检验的紫外完成方案，将TeV尺度物理与观测到的BAU联系起来。低能精密测量（如EDMs）与高能对撞机搜寻之间的协同作用为此类情景提供了强有力的探测途径。

Abstract: We investigate baryogenesis in Standard Model (SM) extensions with new $SU(2)_L$ multiplet fields. We focus on sphalerogenesis, in which the baryon asymmetry of the Universe (BAU) is generated through the gradual decoupling of CP-violating electroweak (EW) sphaleron-like processes. We show that the observed BAU can be reproduced when the new fields possess CP-violating Yukawa interactions, which leave a CP-violating dimension-six operator involving the $SU(2)_L$ gauge fields at low energies. As representative examples, we study models with fermionic $SU(2)_L$ quintuplets and septuplets, and find that these field masses should be $\mathcal{O}(1)\,\mathrm{TeV}$ to explain the BAU. We also show that viable parameter regions for the BAU are consistent with current bounds on the electron electric dipole moment and thoroughly probed by future measurements such as ACME III and by mono-lepton searches at the HL-LHC. Our results provide a concrete and phenomenologically testable ultraviolet completion of sphalerogenesis.

</details>


### [67] [Charged current induced electron-proton scattering and the axial vector form factor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00764)
*A. Fatima,M. Sajjad Athar,S. K. Singh*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study various observables in weak charged current electron-proton scattering, including cross sections and spin asymmetries, with and without assuming time-reversal (T) invariance, focusing on the polarization of the final neutron and sensitivities to axial vector and weak electric form factors. The results are relevant for experiments at JLab and MAMI and may help constrain the axial vector form factor used in neutrino oscillation studies.

我们研究了弱带电流电子-质子散射中的多个可观测量，包括截面和自旋不对称性，在假设和不假设时间反演（T）不变性的情况下，重点关注末态中子的极化以及对轴矢量和弱电形式因子的敏感性。该研究对JLab和MAMI实验具有参考价值，并有助于约束中微子振荡研究中的轴矢量形式因子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The axial vector form factor in nucleon weak interactions has significant uncertainties, affecting precision tests in neutrino physics. By analyzing polarized electron-proton scattering at low energies, this work aims to provide complementary constraints on the axial vector and weak electric form factors through precise measurements of spin asymmetries and polarization observables, especially in light of ongoing experiments at JLab and MAMI.

核子弱相互作用中的轴矢量形式因子存在较大不确定性，影响中微子物理的精确检验。本研究旨在通过在JLab和MAMI进行的低能极化电子-质子散射实验，利用自旋不对称性和极化观测量的精确测量，为轴矢量及弱电形式因子提供补充约束。

Method: We compute the total and differential cross sections, spin asymmetries ($A_L$, $A_P$), and neutron polarization components ($P_L$, $P_P$, $P_T$) in the weak charged current $e^- + p \rightarrow \nu_e + n$ process. Calculations are carried out both under T-invariant assumptions and with possible T-violating contributions, which allow a transverse neutron polarization $P_T$. The dependence of these observables on the axial vector form factor $F_A(Q^2)$ and weak electric form factor $F_W(Q^2)$ is analyzed using theoretical models and numerical simulations.

我们在T不变假设下以及允许T破坏（从而出现横向中子极化$P_T$）的情况下，计算了弱带电流过程$e^- + p \rightarrow \nu_e + n$的总截面、微分截面、自旋不对称性（$A_L$, $A_P$）和中子极化分量（$P_L$, $P_P$, $P_T$）。利用理论模型和数值模拟，分析这些观测量对轴矢量形式因子$F_A(Q^2)$和弱电形式因子$F_W(Q^2)$的依赖关系。

Result: Numerical predictions are provided for all observables across relevant kinematic ranges. We find that $A_L$, $A_P$, and the polarization components $P_L$, $P_P$, $P_T$ exhibit significant sensitivity to $F_A(Q^2)$, while $P_T$ (if observed) could signal T violation or constrain new physics. The differential cross section and $P_L$ are particularly useful for constraining the shape of $F_A(Q^2)$, offering an alternative method to neutrino scattering experiments.

在相关运动学范围内给出了所有观测量的数值预测。我们发现$A_L$、$A_P$及极化分量$P_L$、$P_P$、$P_T$对$F_A(Q^2)$具有显著敏感性，而若观测到$P_T$可能指示T破坏或限制新物理。微分截面和$P_L$特别适用于约束$F_A(Q^2)$的形状，为中微子散射实验提供了替代方法。

Conclusion: Precision measurements of spin and polarization observables in polarized $e^-p$ scattering can provide valuable constraints on the nucleon axial vector form factor, reducing uncertainties in neutrino-nucleus interaction models. The inclusion of T-noninvariant terms allows for tests of fundamental symmetries and potential discovery of new physics beyond the Standard Model.

对极化$e^-p$散射中自旋和极化观测量的精确测量可有效约束核子轴矢量形式因子，降低中微子-原子核相互作用模型的不确定性。引入非T不变项可用于检验基本对称性，并探索标准模型之外的新物理。

Abstract: We investigate the total scattering cross section ($σ$), differential cross section ($\frac{dσ}{dQ^2}$), the longitudinal ($A_L(E_e,Q^2)$) and perpendicular ($A_P(E_e,Q^2)$) spin asymmetries of the polarized target proton, as well as the longitudinal ($P_L(E_e,Q^2)$), perpendicular ($P_P(E_e,Q^2)$), and transverse ($P_T(E_e,Q^2)$) polarization components of the final neutron, in the weak charged current induced electron-proton scattering relevant to the experiments being performed at the Thomas Jefferson National Accelerator Facility (JLab) and Mainz Microtron (MAMI). The analysis is performed assuming time-reversal (T) invariance as well as without assuming T invariance, allowing for a nonvanishing transverse polarization component of the final nucleon, perpendicular to the production plane. Numerical results are presented for all observables, and their sensitivities to the axial vector and weak electric form factors are examined. This study may be useful in the neutrino oscillation experiments to provide an alternative constrain on the parameterization of axial vector form factor, which currently has large uncertainties.

</details>


### [68] [Signatures of Long-Lived Heavy Neutral Leptons from Neutrinophilic Charged Higgs Pair Production at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00866)
*Nobuchika Okada,Prasenjit Sanyal,Ravindra Kumar Verma*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: In the neutrinophilic Higgs doublet model, charged Higgs bosons decay dominantly into heavy neutral leptons (HNLs) and charged leptons, enabling unsuppressed HNL production. We study displaced vertex signatures at the HL-LHC from pair-produced charged Higgs bosons, finding that one displaced vertex can be observed with high significance for cross sections above $\mathcal{O}(1)$ fb, while two displaced vertices are challenging even at $\mathcal{O}(10)$ fb.

在中微子亲和性希格斯二重态模型中，带电希格斯玻色子主要衰变为重中性轻子（HNL）和带电轻子，从而实现未被压低的HNL产生。我们在HL-LHC上研究了来自成对产生的带电希格斯玻色子衰变的位移顶点信号，发现当截面大于$\mathcal{O}(1)$ fb时，单个位移顶点可观测且统计显著性高，而两个位移顶点即使在$\mathcal{O}(10)$ fb下也难以观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The smallness of neutrino masses in the standard seesaw mechanism typically leads to highly suppressed couplings and production cross sections for heavy neutral leptons (HNLs). The neutrinophilic Higgs doublet framework allows for larger Dirac Yukawa couplings due to a small vacuum expectation value, enabling unsuppressed HNL production through charged Higgs decays. This motivates exploring novel collider signatures, particularly displaced vertices from long-lived HNLs.

标准跷跷板机制中微小的中微子质量通常导致重中性轻子（HNL）的耦合和产生截面严重压低。中微子亲和性希格斯二重态框架由于较小的真空期望值允许更大的狄拉克约科瓦耦合，从而通过带电希格斯衰变实现未被压低的HNL产生。这激励我们探索新的对撞机信号，特别是来自长寿命HNL的位移顶点。

Method: We consider pair production of neutrinophilic charged Higgs bosons at the HL-LHC, followed by their decays into HNLs and charged leptons. Assuming one lightest neutrino is very light, the corresponding HNL becomes long-lived, leading to displaced vertices. We simulate both single and double displaced vertex topologies, modeling detector resolution and background rejection, to assess observability at $\sqrt{s} = 14$ TeV with integrated luminosity of 3 ab$^{-1}$.

我们在HL-LHC上考虑中微子亲和性带电希格斯玻色子的成对产生，随后其衰变为HNL和带电轻子。假设最轻的中微子非常轻，则对应的HNL为长寿命粒子，导致位移顶点。我们模拟了单个和双位移顶点拓扑结构，建模探测器分辨率和本底抑制，以评估在$\sqrt{s} = 14$ TeV、积分亮度为3 ab$^{-1}$下的可观测性。

Result: For charged Higgs pair production cross sections greater than $\mathcal{O}(1)$ fb, the single displaced vertex signature yields high statistical significance ($\gtrsim 5\sigma$) at the HL-LHC. However, the double displaced vertex signature remains challenging due to low reconstruction efficiency and small event rates, requiring $\mathcal{O}(10)$ fb cross sections for potential observation, which may not be achievable within current experimental sensitivities.

当带电希格斯成对产生截面大于$\mathcal{O}(1)$ fb时，单个位移顶点信号在HL-LHC上可达到高统计显著性（$\gtrsim 5\sigma$）。然而，由于重建效率低和事例率小，双位移顶点信号仍具挑战性，需要$\mathcal{O}(10)$ fb的截面才可能被观测，这可能超出当前实验灵敏度范围。

Conclusion: The neutrinophilic Higgs doublet model provides a compelling portal for producing detectable long-lived HNLs at the LHC. While single displaced vertex searches offer promising discovery potential for charged Higgs masses accessible at the HL-LHC, double displaced vertex searches are limited by low statistics. Future improvements in displaced track reconstruction could enhance sensitivity to such scenarios.

中微子亲和性希格斯二重态模型为在LHC上产生可探测的长寿命HNL提供了一个有吸引力的通道。虽然单个位移顶点搜索对HL-LHC可及的带电希格斯质量具有良好的发现潜力，但双位移顶点搜索受限于统计量不足。未来对位移轨迹重建的改进有望提升对此类情景的灵敏度。

Abstract: In the neutrinophilic Higgs doublet framework, the neutrino Dirac Yukawa couplings can be sizable because of the small vacuum expection value of the extra Higgs doublet, even for a low seesaw scale. Due to this structure, the neutrinophilic charged Higgs bosons, once created, decay dominantly into heavy neutral leptons (HNLs) and charged leptons. This is a new mechanism to produce a gauge singlet HNL without suppressed cross sections. In the standard seesaw, one HNL can be long-lived, when the lightest neutrino is sufficiently light. We investigate displaced vertex signatures of the long-lived HNLs produced from the decays of the charged Higgs pair at the high luminosity LHC. We consider one displaced vertex as well as two displaced vertices signatures and perform a dedicated simulation to identify the displaced leptons. We find that high statistical significance can be achieved for the observation of one displaced vertex for charged Higgs pair production cross section $>\mathcal{O}(1)$ fb. On the other hand, the observation of two displaced vertices is challenging even for charged Higgs pair production cross section of $\mathcal{O}(10)$ fb.

</details>


### [69] [$t\bar t$ production as a probe of dimension-6 SMEFT at higher orders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00902)
*Nikolaos Kidonakis,Kaan Şimşek*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study $t\bar{t}$ production in SMEFT at dimension 6, focusing on the top chromomagnetic operator $C_{tG}$ and four-quark operators, using NNLO SM + aNNLO SMEFT predictions. Higher-order QCD corrections improve stability and reduce degeneracies, enabling sensitivity to scales up to 3.9 TeV when combining 13 and 13.6 TeV data.

我们研究了在维度6的标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）中，顶夸克对产生过程，重点关注顶色磁矩算符$C_{tG}$和与非极化$t\bar{t}$产生相关的四夸克算符，结合NNLO标准模型和近似NNLO的SM-SMEFT干涉修正。高阶QCD修正提高了理论稳定性并减少了参数简并性，在结合13和13.6 TeV数据后，对有效能标敏感度可达3.9 TeV。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Top-quark pair production is a key probe of new physics beyond the Standard Model (BSM). The chromomagnetic dipole operator $C_{tG}$ is particularly sensitive to BSM dynamics coupling to the top quark. However, leading-order SMEFT interpretations suffer from theoretical instabilities and strong parameter degeneracies. We aim to improve the robustness of SMEFT constraints by including higher-order QCD corrections, which are crucial for precise and reliable phenomenology.

顶夸克对产生是探测超出标准模型（BSM）新物理的关键过程。其中顶色磁矩算符$C_{tG}$对耦合到顶夸克的BSM动力学特别敏感。然而，基于领头阶的SMEFT分析存在理论不稳定性与强参数简并问题。我们旨在通过引入高阶QCD修正来提升SMEFT限制的稳健性，这对精确可靠的唯象研究至关重要。

Method: We employ a combined NNLO QCD calculation for SM $t\bar{t}$ production and approximate NNLO (aNNLO) corrections for the interference between SM and dimension-6 SMEFT operators, specifically $C_{tG}$ and relevant four-quark operators ($C_{qq}^{(1,3)}, C_{qt}^{(1,8)}$). We compute single-differential distributions in top $p_T$ and $y$, and double-differential $p_T \times y$ distributions at 13 TeV, and project results to 13.6 TeV with identical binning. Theoretical uncertainties are estimated via scale variation, and limits on Wilson coefficients are derived using profile likelihood fits.

我们采用NNLO QCD计算标准模型下的$t\bar{t}$产生，并结合近似NNLO（aNNLO）修正处理SM与维度6 SMEFT算符（特别是$C_{tG}$及相关的四夸克算符$C_{qq}^{(1,3)}, C_{qt}^{(1,8)}$）之间的干涉项。我们计算了在13 TeV下顶夸克的单微分横动量$p_T$和快度$y$分布，以及双微分$p_T \times y$分布，并使用相同分箱投影至13.6 TeV。理论不确定性通过尺度变化估计，威尔逊系数的限制通过轮廓似然拟合得出。

Result: Higher-order QCD effects significantly stabilize the SMEFT interpretation, reducing scale uncertainties and weakening degeneracies among Wilson coefficients. The strongest constraints are obtained on $C_{tG}$, due to its impact on high-$p_T$ tails. Combining 13 TeV data and 13.6 TeV projections at highest order, we achieve sensitivity to $\Lambda_{\rm eff} \sim 3.9~{\rm TeV}$ for $C_{tG}$, representing a substantial improvement over lower-order analyses.

高阶QCD效应显著稳定了SMEFT解释，减小了尺度不确定性，并削弱了威尔逊系数间的简并性。对$C_{tG}$的限制最强，因其显著影响高$p_T$尾部区域。在结合13 TeV结果与13.6 TeV投影的最高阶分析中，我们对$C_{tG}$的有效能标敏感度达到约3.9 TeV，相比低阶分析有显著提升。

Conclusion: Differential measurements of $t\bar{t}$ production at NNLO + aNNLO accuracy provide a theoretically robust and sensitive probe of SMEFT operators, especially $C_{tG}$. Including higher-order corrections is essential for reliable EFT interpretations at the LHC. Our results highlight the importance of precision theory in BSM searches using top-quark observables.

在NNLO+aNNLO精度下的微分$t\bar{t}$产生测量为探测SMEFT算符（尤其是$C_{tG}$）提供了理论上稳健且高度敏感的手段。包含高阶修正是LHC上实现可靠EFT解释的关键。我们的结果凸显了在利用顶夸克观测量进行BSM搜索时，精确理论计算的重要性。

Abstract: We study top-antitop pair production in proton-proton collisions within the Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT) at dimension 6. We focus on the top chromomagnetic operator $C_{tG}$ together with the four-quark operators relevant for unpolarized $t{\bar t}$ production. We analyze the top-quark single-differential transverse-momentum ($p_T$) and rapidity ($y$) distributions and the double-differential distributions in $p_T$ and $y$ ($p_T\times y$) at 13~TeV, and we present projections for 13.6~TeV using the same binning. Our highest-order setup combines next-to-next-to-leading-order (NNLO) Standard Model (SM) predictions with approximate NNLO (aNNLO) SM--SMEFT interference corrections. We find that higher-order QCD effects are essential for a stable SMEFT interpretation, yielding substantially more robust bounds and milder parameter degeneracies. The strongest sensitivity is obtained for $C_{tG}$. In the combined highest-order analysis of the 13-TeV results and 13.6-TeV projections, we obtain sensitivity to effective scales up to 3.9~TeV. Our results show that higher-order differential top-pair production provides a precise and theoretically controlled probe of the top chromomagnetic interaction.

</details>


### [70] [Renormalization-group-improved constraints on dimension-7 baryon-number-violating operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00952)
*Yi Liao,Xiao-Dong Ma,Xiang Zhao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We analyze dimension-7 SMEFT baryon-number-violating operators and show that renormalization group (RG) running effects significantly strengthen constraints on all 297 Wilson coefficients, especially enabling sensitivity to operators involving second and third generation fermions via Yukawa-induced mixings.

我们分析了维度-7 SMEFT 中的重子数破坏算符，表明重整化群（RG）跑动效应显著加强了对全部 297 个威尔森系数的限制，特别是通过汤川耦合混合使对涉及第二和第三代费米子的算符具备间接探测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Baryon-number-violating operators in the Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT) can lead to nucleon decays, which are highly constrained by experiment. While tree-level analyses typically constrain only operators involving first- and second-generation fermions due to experimental limits on proton and neutron decays, operators involving third-generation fermions remain weakly constrained. This work aims to include full RG running effects to extend sensitivity to otherwise inaccessible Wilson coefficients, particularly those involving heavier fermion generations.

标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）中的重子数破坏算符可能导致核子衰变，实验对此有严格限制。虽然树图层次的分析通常仅能约束涉及第一代和第二代费米子的算符，但涉及第三代费米子的算符仍缺乏约束。本工作旨在引入完整的RG跑动效应，以扩展对原本无法探测的威尔森系数的敏感性，特别是涉及更重费米子代的算符。

Method: We compute the one-loop renormalization group equations (RGEs) for dimension-7 baryon-number-violating operators in the SMEFT, including their mixing with lower-dimensional operators and among themselves. We evolve the Wilson coefficients from a high new physics scale $\Lambda$ down to the electroweak scale using the full RGE framework, incorporating Yukawa couplings of quarks and leptons. Matching at the electroweak scale to low-energy effective theories allows us to relate high-scale coefficients to nucleon decay rates, which are then compared with experimental bounds from Super-Kamiokande and other experiments.

我们计算了SMEFT中维度-7重子数破坏算符的一圈重整化群方程（RGE），包括它们与低维算符及其他自身之间的混合。利用完整的RGE框架，结合夸克和轻子的汤川耦合，我们将威尔森系数从高能新物理尺度$\Lambda$跑动至电弱尺度。在电弱尺度匹配到低能有效理论，从而将高能标系数与核子衰变率关联，并与Super-Kamiokande等实验的观测界限进行比较。

Result: Full RG running induces significant mixing between dimension-7 operators involving third-generation fermions and those accessible through nucleon decay experiments. As a result, stringent bounds are obtained on all 297 independent Wilson coefficients at the high scale $\Lambda$, improving over tree-level limits by several orders of magnitude for many coefficients. In particular, Yukawa-enhanced RG effects enable indirect probes of top- and bottom-quark-involved operators through light-quark nucleon decays.

完整的RG跑动在涉及第三代费米子的维度-7算符与可通过核子衰变实验探测的算符之间诱导出显著混合。结果，在高能标$\Lambda$处对全部297个独立的威尔森系数获得了严格限制，许多系数的界限比树图层次提升了若干数量级。特别是，由汤川耦合增强的RG效应使得通过轻夸克核子衰变间接探测涉及顶夸克和底夸克的算符成为可能。

Conclusion: Renormalization group running, especially through Yukawa interactions, plays a crucial role in connecting high-scale baryon-number-violating physics to low-energy observables. Our analysis demonstrates that even operators not directly coupled to first-generation fermions can be strongly constrained via RG evolution, thereby enhancing the reach of nucleon decay experiments to a complete set of dimension-7 SMEFT operators.

重整化群跑动，尤其是通过汤川相互作用，在连接高能标重子数破坏物理与低能可观测量方面起着关键作用。我们的分析表明，即使不直接耦合到第一代费米子的算符，也可通过RG演化受到强烈限制，从而扩展了核子衰变实验对完整一组维度-7 SMEFT算符的探测能力。

Abstract: We study constraints on dimension-7 SMEFT baryon-number-violating operators from nucleon decays by incorporating full renormalization group (RG) running effects. At high new physics scales, we demonstrate that RG running effects help set stringent bounds on all 297 Wilson coefficients compared to the tree-level analysis in which only coefficients involving the first and second fermion generations could be constrained. Our findings highlight that the RG running effects through Yukawa mixings are particularly important for indirectly probing operators involving the second and third generation fermions.

### [71] [Baryonic form factors of light pseudoscalar mesons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00959)
*A. S. Miramontes,J. M. Morgado,J. Papavassiliou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We compute the space-like baryonic form factor of pion and kaon using the Bethe-Salpeter formalism, finding a nonzero signal due to $m_d - m_u$ breaking of $G$-parity; the pion baryonic radius is $\langle r_{\! B}^2\rangle_{π^+}^{1/2} = 0.043(2)$ fm, consistent with dispersive results, while kaon radii are larger: $\langle r_{\!B}^2\rangle_{K^+}^{1/2} = 0.265(7)$ fm and $\langle r_{\!B}^2\rangle_{K^0}^{1/2} = 0.262(7)$ fm, in agreement with chiral QCD models.

采用Bethe-Salpeter方法计算了π介子和K介子的类空重子形状因子，发现由于$m_d - m_u$导致$G$宇称破缺而出现非零信号；π介子的重子半径为$\langle r_{\! B}^2\rangle_{π^+}^{1/2} = 0.043(2)$ fm，与色散基准一致，而K介子半径更大：$\langle r_{\!B}^2\rangle_{K^+}^{1/2} = 0.265(7)$ fm 和 $\langle r_{\!B}^2\rangle_{K^0}^{1/2} = 0.262(7)$ fm，与手征QCD模型相符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The baryonic form factor for pseudoscalar mesons like the pion and kaon vanishes in the exact isospin-symmetric limit due to $G$-parity conservation; thus, its nonzero value directly probes $m_d - m_u$, offering a sensitive test of isospin violation in QCD. This provides insight into light quark mass differences, which are fundamental parameters in the Standard Model.

在精确的同位旋对称极限下，由于$G$宇称守恒，π介子和K介子等赝标量介子的重子形状因子为零；因此，其非零值可直接探测$m_d - m_u$，为QCD中的同位旋破缺提供敏感检验。这有助于理解标准模型中的轻夸克质量差这一基本参数。

Method: We employ the Bethe-Salpeter formalism within a Poincaré-covariant framework, computing the baryonic form factor in the impulse approximation. Fully dressed quark propagators, meson Bethe-Salpeter amplitudes, and a vector Ward-Takahashi identity-constrained baryon-current vertex are used to ensure gauge invariance and dynamical consistency. The calculation is performed in the space-like momentum regime.

我们在Poincaré协变框架下采用Bethe-Salpeter方法，在冲量近似中计算重子形状因子。使用完全缀饰的夸克传播子、介子Bethe-Salpeter振幅以及满足矢量Ward-Takahashi恒等式的重子流顶点，以保证规范不变性和动力学自洽性。计算在类空动量区域进行。

Result: For the pion, we obtain $\langle r_{\! B}^2\rangle_{π^+}^{1/2} = 0.043(2)$ fm, in agreement with dispersive estimates. For kaons, we predict $\langle r_{\!B}^2\rangle_{K^+}^{1/2} = 0.265(7)$ fm and $\langle r_{\!B}^2\rangle_{K^0}^{1/2} = 0.262(7)$ fm—significantly larger than the pion case—indicating greater spatial distribution of baryon number. These kaon results currently lack dispersive counterparts but are compatible with chiral QCD model predictions.

对于π介子，我们得到$\langle r_{\! B}^2\rangle_{π^+}^{1/2} = 0.043(2)$ fm，与色散估计一致。对于K介子，预测值为$\langle r_{\!B}^2\rangle_{K^+}^{1/2} = 0.265(7)$ fm 和 $\langle r_{\!B}^2\rangle_{K^0}^{1/2} = 0.262(7)$ fm，显著大于π介子，表明重子数的空间分布更广。这些K介子结果目前尚无对应的色散计算，但与手征QCD模型预测相符。

Conclusion: The nonzero baryonic form factors of pion and kaon, enabled by $m_d - m_u$, serve as direct probes of isospin symmetry breaking in QCD. Our results confirm the smallness of this effect in the pion via agreement with dispersive methods, while providing new quantitative predictions for kaons that can be tested in future lattice QCD or effective field theory studies.

由$m_d - m_u$引起的π介子和K介子非零重子形状因子是QCD中同位旋对称性破缺的直接探针。我们的结果通过与色散方法的一致性验证了该效应在π介子中的微弱性，同时为K介子提供了新的定量预测，可供未来格点QCD或有效场论研究检验。

Abstract: Employing the Bethe-Salpeter formalism, we present a computation of the space-like baryonic form factor for the pion and kaon. In the exact isospin-symmetric limit this observable is forbidden by $G$-parity, so that any nonzero signal constitutes a direct probe of the quark mass difference $m_d - m_u$. The form factors are evaluated in the impulse approximation using fully dressed quark propagators, meson Bethe-Salpeter amplitudes, and a dressed baryon-current vertex constrained by the vector Ward-Takahashi identity. The baryonic radius computed with this method for the pion is given by $\langle r_{\! B}^2\rangle_{π^+}^{1/2} = 0.043(2)$ fm, and is consistent with the available dispersive benchmarks. Our predictions for the kaons, namely $\langle r_{\!B}^2\rangle_{K^+}^{1/2} = 0.265(7)$ fm and $\langle r_{\!B}^2\rangle_{K^0}^{1/2} = 0.262(7)$ fm, indicate a larger spatial extent than in the pion case; these results have no dispersive counterparts, and are compatible with chiral QCD models.

### [72] [Mass relations in heavy hadrons from Jensen-like inequalities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00962)
*Wen-Xuan Zhang,Wen-Nian Liu,Duojie Jia*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper establishes that mass inequalities in heavy hadrons originate from the concavity of binding energies as a function of inverse reduced quark mass, supported by empirical data and leading to model-independent predictions for unobserved baryon masses.

本文通过结合实验数据与夸克模型，论证了重味强子质量不等式源于结合能对约化质量倒数的凹性，并据此预测了尚未观测到的重子质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the origin of empirical mass inequalities in hadrons containing heavy quarks and provide a model-independent framework grounded in experimental data rather than specific dynamical assumptions.

旨在理解含重夸克强子中经验质量不等式的起源，并建立一个基于实验数据而非特定动力学假设的模型无关框架。

Method: Extracted spin-averaged two-body binding energies $B_{i\bar{j}}$ from experimental meson masses; analyzed their dependence on reduced mass $\mu_{ij}$; used concavity of $B(1/\mu)$ to derive Jensen-type inequalities under flavor permutations; validated decomposition $\Delta M_{\mathrm{EXP}} \approx \Delta B + \Delta C$; promoted inequalities to equalities for mass predictions.

从实验介子质量中提取自旋平均的两体结合能 $B_{i\bar{j}}$；分析其对约化质量 $\mu_{ij}$ 的依赖关系；利用 $B(1/\mu)$ 的凹性在味置换下推导出Jensen型不等式；验证质量分解 $\Delta M_{\mathrm{EXP}} \approx \Delta B + \Delta C$；将不等式提升为等式以进行质量预测。

Result: Identified a critical confinement scale of 1.34~fm where binding becomes positive; derived concave dependence of $B(1/\mu)$ explaining hadronic mass inequalities such as $m_{x\bar{y}} > \frac{1}{2}(m_{x\bar{x}} + m_{y\bar{y}})$ and baryon analogs; achieved high-precision mass decomposition with $\sigma \sim 2.07$~MeV; predicted masses for unobserved baryons: $M(Ω_{b}^{*})=6076.6$~MeV, $M(Ξ_{cc}^{*})=3703.6$~MeV, $M(Ω_{cc}^{*})=3802.4$~MeV.

确定了一个1.34 fm的临界禁闭尺度，在此尺度下结合能变为正值；发现 $B(1/\mu)$ 的凹性可解释诸如 $m_{x\bar{y}} > \frac{1}{2}(m_{x\bar{x}} + m_{y\bar{y}})$ 及其重子类似形式的质量不等式；实现了精度高达 $\sigma \sim 2.07$ MeV的质量分解；预测了未观测重子的质量：$M(Ω_{b}^{*})=6076.6$ MeV，$M(Ξ_{cc}^{*})=3703.6$ MeV，$M(Ω_{cc}^{*})=3802.4$ MeV。

Conclusion: Hadron mass inequalities are fundamentally rooted in the concavity of binding energy due to QCD-inspired interactions (Coulombic + confinement), which can be empirically verified and exploited to make precise, model-independent predictions for unknown hadron masses.

强子质量不等式本质上源于由QCD启发的相互作用（库仑+禁闭）导致的结合能凹性，这种性质可通过实验验证，并可用于对未知强子质量做出精确且模型无关的预测。

Abstract: We demonstrate that mass inequalities for hadrons with one or more heavy quarks arise primarily from the concavity of binding energies in the quark model, reflecting short-range Coulombic interactions and long-range confinement. Empirical two-body bindings $B_{i\bar{j}}$ are extracted from spin-averaged meson masses, ensuring model independence and direct use of experimental data. Fitting these as functions of reduced mass $μ_{ij}$ reveals a critical confinement scale of 1.34~fm where bindings turn positive. The concave $B(1/μ)$ justifies Jensen-like inequalities under flavor permutation, reproducing relations like $m_{x\bar{y}} > \frac{1}{2}(m_{x\bar{x}} + m_{y\bar{y}})$ and baryon analogs, including $m_{xyz} > \frac{1}{3}(m_{xxx} + m_{yyy} + m_{zzz})$. Hadron mass decomposition validates $ΔM_{\textrm{EXP}} \approx ΔB + ΔC$ with $σ\sim 2.07$~MeV for mesons and baryons. Promoting inequalities to equalities, we predict masses for unobserved heavy baryons (e.g., $M(Ω_{b}^{\ast})=6076.6\,$MeV, $M(Ξ_{cc}^{\ast})=3703.6\,$MeV and $M(Ω_{cc}^{\ast})=3802.4\,$MeV) and identify favored quark-exchange scattering channels.

味相关的Bethe-Salpeter框架为跨越整个夸克质量谱的赝标量介子电磁性质提供了稳健且具有预测性的描述，支持其作为连续QCD中强子结构研究工具的应用。

### [74] [How uncertain are model predictions for the muon content of extensive air showers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00975)

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates the connection between model predictions of muon content in extensive air showers (EAS) and the underlying hadron-air interaction mechanisms, using a new Monte Carlo generator QGSb to analyze the impact of specific interaction processes on predicted muon numbers, with considerations from accelerator data constraints.

观测到的EAS中μ子含量与现有模型预测之间存在差异，表明在极高能区强子相互作用建模可能存在缺陷；明确哪些相互作用机制对μ子产生影响最大，对于改进EAS模拟和解释宇宙线数据至关重要。

Method: A new Monte Carlo generator, QGSb, is developed and employed to simulate cosmic ray interactions; the sensitivity of predicted EAS muon numbers to variations in specific hadronic interaction mechanisms (e.g., multiparticle production, cross sections, strangeness enhancement) is systematically studied; results are compared with available accelerator data to assess physical consistency.

开发并使用了一种新的蒙特卡洛生成器QGSb来模拟宇宙线相互作用；系统研究了预测的EAS μ子数对特定强子相互作用机制（如多粒子产生、截面、奇异性增强等）变化的敏感性；并将结果与现有的加速器数据进行比较，以评估物理一致性。

Result: The QGSb simulations reveal that the muon content in EAS is particularly sensitive to the treatment of high-multiplicity hadronic events and the energy dependence of hadronic cross sections; models that better describe LHC forward particle production tend to predict higher muon densities, closer to EAS observations; accelerator constraints disfavor extreme enhancements in diffractive or soft processes.

QGSb模拟显示，EAS中的μ子含量对高多重性强子事件的处理方式以及强子截面的能量依赖性特别敏感；能更好描述LHC前向粒子产生的模型倾向于预测更高的μ子密度，更接近EAS观测结果；加速器约束排除了衍射或软过程的极端增强。

Conclusion: Accurate modeling of high-energy hadronic interactions, especially multiparticle dynamics and cross-section growth, is crucial for resolving the 'muon puzzle' in EAS; the QGSb generator provides a valuable tool for testing hadronic interaction models against both collider and cosmic ray data.

精确建模高能强子相互作用，特别是多粒子动力学和截面增长，对于解决EAS中的“μ子疑难”至关重要；QGSb生成器为利用对撞机和宇宙线数据检验强子相互作用模型提供了有力工具。

Abstract: The relation of model predictions for muon content of extensive air showers (EAS) to particular properties of hadron-air interactions is discussed. Further, using a new Monte Carlo generator of cosmic ray interactions, QGSb, the relevance of particular interaction mechanisms to the predicted EAS muon number is studied in some detail. The corresponding constraints imposed by accelerator measurements are discussed as well.

</details>


### [75] [Quantum effects on neutrino parameters from a flavored gauge boson](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.00990)
*Alejandro Ibarra,Lukas Treuer*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We compute the one-loop renormalization group equations (RGEs) for the neutrino mass matrix in an extension of the Standard Model with a massive gauge boson having family-dependent couplings to left-handed leptons. We find that this new gauge boson induces rank enhancement of the neutrino mass matrix at one-loop level—unlike the Standard Model, where such effects occur only at two loops. This opens the possibility of radiatively generating realistic neutrino masses and mixings from a rank-zero tree-level mass matrix.

我们计算了在标准模型基础上引入一个与左手轻子具有代依赖耦合的重规范玻色子后，中微子质量矩阵的一圈重整化群方程（RGE）。我们发现，这种新规范玻色子在一圈水平诱导出中微子质量矩阵的秩提升——而标准模型中的场只能在两圈水平实现这一效应。这使得从树图水平秩为零的质量矩阵出发，通过辐射修正生成符合观测的中微子质量和混合角成为可能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In the Standard Model (SM), radiative corrections to the neutrino mass matrix are highly suppressed, and rank-preserving effects dominate at low orders. A zero-rank neutrino mass matrix at tree level remains approximately zero unless higher-loop effects (e.g., two-loop) are considered. However, current neutrino oscillation data require non-degenerate masses and large mixing angles, suggesting possible new physics beyond the SM that can generate these features dynamically. Introducing a massive gauge boson $Z'$ with family-non-universal couplings offers a well-motivated extension, as such models arise naturally in theories addressing anomalies in B-physics or through gauged $L_\mu - L_\tau$ symmetries. The motivation is to investigate whether such a $Z'$ can induce significant quantum corrections to the neutrino mass matrix at lower loop order than in the SM.

在标准模型（SM）中，中微子质量矩阵的辐射修正被严重压低，低阶修正通常保持质量矩阵的秩不变。若树图水平质量矩阵秩为零，则需依赖高圈图效应（如两圈）才能产生非零质量。然而当前中微子振荡实验要求非简并的质量和大混合角，暗示可能存在能够动态生成这些特征的新物理。引入一个具有代非普适耦合的重规范玻色子$Z'$是一个有理论动机的扩展，此类模型自然出现在解释B物理反常或基于$gauge\ L_\mu - L_\tau$对称性的理论中。本文动机是探究此类$Z'$是否能在比标准模型更低的圈图阶数下诱导出显著的中微子质量矩阵量子修正。

Method: We extend the Standard Model by introducing a new massive gauge boson $Z'$ that couples chirally and family-dependently to left-handed leptons. Starting with a neutrino mass matrix of rank zero at tree level (e.g., due to an underlying symmetry), we compute the one-loop quantum corrections to the effective neutrino mass matrix using the renormalization group equations (RGEs). The beta function for the neutrino Yukawa coupling is derived by calculating relevant Feynman diagrams involving $Z'$ exchange and lepton doublets, and we extract the contribution to the mass matrix running. We analyze the structure of the generated mass matrix, focusing on its rank and eigenvalues, and assess whether observed mass-squared differences ($\Delta m_{21}^2$, $\Delta m_{31}^2$) and PMNS mixing angles can be reproduced under normal and inverted ordering assumptions.

我们在标准模型中引入一个新的重规范玻色子$Z'$，其手征性地且代依赖地耦合到左手轻子上。假设树图水平中微子质量矩阵秩为零（例如源于某种底层对称性），我们利用重整化群方程（RGE）计算有效中微子质量矩阵的一圈量子修正。通过计算涉及$Z'$交换和轻子二重态的相关费曼图，推导中微子Yukawa耦合的beta函数，并提取对质量矩阵跑动的贡献。我们分析所生成质量矩阵的结构，重点关注其秩和本征值，并检验在正常序和反常序假设下能否复现观测到的质量平方差（$\Delta m_{21}^2$、$\Delta m_{31}^2$）和PMNS混合角。

Result: The one-loop RGE induced by the $Z'$ boson generates off-diagonal and diagonal contributions to the neutrino mass matrix that were absent at tree level, increasing its rank from zero to full rank (three) in generic cases. This rank enhancement occurs due to chiral and family-non-universal interactions mediated by the $Z'$, which break lepton universality and allow mixing between generations. Numerical analysis shows that, for reasonable choices of $Z'$ mass ($M_{Z'} \sim 1-1000$ TeV) and coupling strengths ($g' \sim 10^{-4}-10^{-2}$), the observed mass-squared splittings and mixing angles can be dynamically generated via RG evolution from high-scale symmetric initial conditions. Both normal and inverted mass orderings are found to be viable, depending on the flavor structure of the $Z'$ couplings.

由$Z'$玻色子诱导的一圈RGE在原本为零的中微子质量矩阵中生成了非对角项和对角项贡献，在一般情况下使其秩从零提升至满秩（三）。这种秩提升源于$Z'$介导的手征性和代非普适相互作用，破坏了轻子普适性并允许代间混合。数值分析表明，对于合理的$Z'$质量（$M_{Z'} \sim 1-1000$ TeV）和耦合强度（$g' \sim 10^{-4}-10^{-2}$），通过从高能标对称初态的RG演化，可以动态生成观测到的质量平方分裂和混合角。根据$Z'$耦合的味结构不同，正常质量和反常质量顺序均可实现。

Conclusion: The introduction of a massive gauge boson with family-dependent couplings to left-handed leptons significantly alters the renormalization group behavior of the neutrino mass matrix. Unlike in the Standard Model, where rank-enhancing effects enter only at two loops, the new $Z'$ enables rank enhancement already at one loop. This provides a novel mechanism for radiatively generating realistic neutrino masses and mixings from highly symmetric (e.g., rank-zero) initial conditions. Such scenarios are testable through precision measurements of lepton flavor violation, $Z'$ searches at colliders, and cosmological observations constraining extra relativistic degrees of freedom.

引入一个与左手轻子具有代依赖耦合的重规范玻色子显著改变了中微子质量矩阵的重整化群行为。与标准模型中秩提升效应仅出现在两圈不同，新的$Z'$使得秩提升在一环即可发生。这为从高度对称（例如秩为零）的初始条件辐射生成真实的中微子质量和混合提供了一种新机制。此类情景可通过轻子味破坏的精确测量、对撞机上的$Z'$搜索以及限制额外相对论自由度的宇宙学观测加以检验。

Abstract: We calculate the one-loop renormalization group equations of the neutrino mass matrix when the Standard Model particle content is extended with a massive gauge boson which has family-dependent couplings to the left-handed leptons. We show that quantum effects induced by the extra gauge boson increase the rank of the neutrino mass matrix at the one-loop level, in contrast to the well-known result that Standard Model fields can only increase the rank at the two-loop level. We also discuss the possibility of generating dynamically the measured mass differences and mixing angles between the active neutrinos in scenarios with normal and inverted mass ordering.

Result: The resulting solution accurately satisfies the axial Ward-Takahashi identities, demonstrating consistency with chiral symmetry. The use of modern QCD correlation functions leads to a more reliable description of the pion's structure and dynamics in the chiral limit.

所得解精确满足轴向Ward-Takahashi恒等式，表明与手征对称性一致。使用现代QCD关联函数使得对手征极限下π介子结构和动力学的描述更加可靠。

Conclusion: The novel Bethe-Salpeter approach successfully incorporates fundamental QCD symmetries and provides a robust framework for studying light mesons in the chiral limit, paving the way for more accurate studies of hadron physics from first principles.

这种新颖的Bethe-Salpeter方法成功地结合了基本的QCD对称性，为在手征极限下研究轻介子提供了一个稳健的框架，为从第一性原理出发更精确地研究强子物理铺平了道路。

Abstract: We present a novel version of the pion Bethe-Salpeter equation in the chiral limit, solved using as ingredients state-of-the-art QCD correlation functions. The constraints imposed by the axial Ward-Takahashi identities are exactly fulfilled, both formally and numerically.
