### [77] [Precise theoretical prediction on branching fractions and polarizations of $D \to V V$ decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01008)
*Jing Ou-Yang,Hui Zheng,Run-Hui Li,Si-Hong Zhou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We perform a systematic analysis of $D \to VV$ decays using the factorization-assisted topological-amplitude (FAT) approach, fitting 10 nonfactorizable parameters to 36 experimental data points with $\chi^2/\mathrm{d.o.f.} = 8.43$. The framework includes SU(3) symmetry breaking and explains anomalies such as $f_\parallel > f_L$ via strong phase interference and $D$-wave dominance over $S$-wave due to $|S| < |D|$. Predictions for 28 modes are made, guiding future measurements at BESIII, STCF, Belle II, and LHCb.

我们利用因子化辅助拓扑振幅（FAT）方法对 $D \to VV$ 衰变进行了系统分析，通过拟合36个实验数据点提取了10个非因子化参数，$\chi^2/\mathrm{d.o.f.} = 8.43$。该框架包含SU(3)对称性破缺效应，通过强相位干涉解释了 $f_\parallel > f_L$ 等反常现象，并因 $|S| < |D|$ 导致D波分支比超过S波。我们预测了28个衰变道的分支比和极化，为BESIII、STCF、Belle II和LHCb的未来测量提供了指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The $D \to VV$ decays provide a sensitive probe of charm physics, but theoretical predictions are challenged by nonfactorizable strong interaction effects. Current experimental data are limited, necessitating a robust phenomenological framework like the FAT approach to extract dynamical information and predict unmeasured modes. Discrepancies with naive factorization—such as anomalous polarization patterns ($f_\parallel > f_L$) and unexpected $D$-wave dominance—call for a systematic treatment incorporating SU(3) flavor symmetry breaking and global fits to data.

$D \to VV$ 衰变为研究粲物理提供了敏感探针，但非因子化强相互作用效应给理论预测带来挑战。当前实验数据有限，亟需如FAT方法之类的稳健唯象框架来提取动力学信息并预测未观测衰变道。与朴素因子化模型的偏差——如反常极化模式（$f_\parallel > f_L$）和意外的D波主导——要求系统性地引入SU(3)味对称性破缺并进行全局数据拟合。

Method: We employ the factorization-assisted topological-amplitude (FAT) approach to parameterize $D \to VV$ decay amplitudes, decomposing them into topological diagrams ($C$, $E$, $S$, $D$, etc.) where nonfactorizable contributions are encoded in universal complex parameters. SU(3) flavor symmetry breaking is incorporated by allowing different magnitudes and phases for otherwise symmetric amplitudes. A global $\chi^2$ fit is performed using 36 available experimental branching fractions and polarization measurements to determine 10 nonfactorizable parameters associated with $C$ and $E$ diagrams. Polarization amplitudes are computed including strong phases, and predictions are made for both measured and unmeasured decay channels.

我们采用因子化辅助拓扑振幅（FAT）方法对 $D \to VV$ 衰变振幅进行参数化，将其分解为拓扑图（$C$、$E$、$S$、$D$ 等），其中非因子化贡献被编码为普适复参数。通过允许原本对称的振幅具有不同的大小和相位来引入SU(3)味对称性破缺。利用36个现有的实验分支比和极化测量值进行全局 $\chi^2$ 拟合，确定与 $C$ 和 $E$ 图相关的10个非因子化参数。计算包含强相位的极化振幅，并对已测和未测衰变道做出预测。

Result: From the global fit, we obtain 10 nonfactorizable parameters with $\chi^2/\mathrm{d.o.f.} = 8.43$. A large strong phase in the longitudinal $E$ amplitude leads to destructive interference with the $C$ longitudinal component, resulting in $f_\parallel > f_L$, in contrast to naive factorization. For $E$-diagram-dominated modes, the hierarchy $|S| < |D|$ implies larger $D$-wave than $S$-wave branching fractions, explaining recent observations that violate $S$-wave dominance. Predicted branching ratios and polarization fractions for 28 decay modes are consistent with current data. Several unobserved modes with $\mathcal{B} \sim 10^{-3}\text{--}10^{-2}$, $D$-wave dominance, or $f_\parallel > f_L$ are identified for future tests.

通过全局拟合，我们得到10个非因子化参数，$\chi^2/\mathrm{d.o.f.} = 8.43$。纵向 $E$ 振幅中的大强相位导致其与 $C$ 的纵向分量发生相消干涉，产生 $f_\parallel > f_L$，与朴素因子化结果相反。对于由 $E$ 图主导的衰变道，$|S| < |D|$ 的振幅层级意味着D波分支比大于S波，解释了违反S波主导的最新观测。对28个衰变道预测的分支比和极化分数与现有数据一致。若干未观测的衰变道，其分支比约为 $10^{-3}\text{--}10^{-2}$，或表现为D波主导或 $f_\parallel > f_L$，可在未来实验中检验。

Conclusion: The FAT approach provides a precise and predictive framework for $D \to VV$ decays, successfully describing current data and resolving long-standing puzzles such as anomalous vector meson polarizations and $D$-wave dominance. The inclusion of SU(3) breaking and strong phases is essential. Future measurements of predicted modes at BESIII, STCF, Belle II, and LHCb will further test the FAT paradigm and deepen our understanding of nonperturbative dynamics in charm decays.

FAT方法为 $D \to VV$ 衰变提供了一个精确且具有预测能力的框架，成功描述了现有数据并解决了诸如矢量介子极化反常和D波主导等长期存在的难题。引入SU(3)对称性破缺和强相位至关重要。BESIII、STCF、Belle II和LHCb对未来预测衰变道的测量将进一步检验FAT范式，并深化我们对粲介子衰变中非微扰动力学的理解。

Abstract: We present a precise and systematic analysis of $D \to V V$ decays within the factorization-assisted topological-amplitude (FAT) approach, where $D$ denotes the set $\{D^0, \, D^+,\, D^+_s\}$ and $V$ represents the vector mesons $ρ, K^*, ω$, and $φ$. Given the limited current experimental data, the FAT approach serves as a available phenomenological framework for predicting charmed meson decays to both vector mesons. In this framework, incorporating flavor SU(3) symmetry breaking effects, we can express nonfactorizable contributions of different modes as a minimal set of universal parameters globally fitted to experimental data. Utilizing 36 experimental data points for $D \to VV$ decays, we precisely extract 10 nonfactorizable parameters associated with the $C$ and $E$ topological diagrams with $χ^2/\mathrm{d.o.f.}=8.43$. We find that a large strong phase in the longitude $E$ amplitude cause strong destructive interference with the $C$ longitudinal component, yielding $f_\parallel >f_L $, contrary to the naive factorization predictions. Additionally, for modes processing exclusively by the $E$ diagram, the amplitude hierarchy $|S|<|D|$ leads to a $D$-wave branching fraction larger than that of the $S$-wave. This explains recent observations that contradict $S$-wave dominance predictions. The predicted branching fractions and polarizations for 28 decay modes are consistent with existing experimental data.
  Unobserved modes, especially those with branching fractions of order
  $10^{-3}\sim10^{-2}$, the $D$-wave dominated modes, and modes exhibiting
  $f_\parallel >f_L $, await measurement by BESIII, STCF, Belle II and LHCb.

### [78] [Mass Hierarchies Without Mixing: Abelian Froggatt-Nielsen Models with Uncharged Left-Handed Doublets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01055)
*Navid Ardakanian*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Abelian discrete Froggatt-Nielsen models with uncharged left-handed fermions yield Haar-random CKM and PMNS matrices, predicting no structure in mixing angles due to excessive free parameters from one-dimensional representations; while the mass hierarchy problem is avoidable for $\mathbb{Z}_N$ with $N \geq 4$, the mixing problem is universal and irreducible, necessitating non-abelian symmetries like $A_4$ for predictive mixing patterns.

Abelian离散Froggatt-Nielsen模型中，若左手费米子无荷，则导致CKM和PMNS矩阵呈Haar随机分布，无法生成混合角结构，根源在于一维表示带来的过多自由参数；虽然质量等级问题在$\mathbb{Z}_N$（$N \geq 4$）中可避免，但混合角问题普遍存在且不可消除，必须引入如$A_4$等非Abel对称性以获得可预测的混合模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand whether abelian discrete flavor symmetries in Froggatt-Nielsen models can explain the observed quark and lepton mixing patterns, particularly why the CKM matrix exhibits small mixing angles while the PMNS matrix shows large ones. The work specifically investigates the role of charge assignments, especially when left-handed fermions are uncharged, a well-motivated setup in many UV-complete models.

旨在理解Abel离散味对称性（如Froggatt-Nielsen模型）是否能解释观测到的夸克与轻子混合模式，尤其是为何CKM矩阵混合角小而PMNS矩阵混合角大。本文特别研究了电荷分配的作用，重点关注左手费米子无荷的情形——这在许多紫外完备模型中是自然的设定。

Method: We prove analytically that all abelian discrete Froggatt-Nielsen models with uncharged left-handed doublets produce Haar-distributed random unitary matrices for both CKM and PMNS, due to the independence of generations as one-dimensional representations. We perform numerical scans over $\mathbb{Z}_3$ to $\mathbb{Z}_7$ groups with 12 distinct charge assignments each, using $10^5$ Monte Carlo samples to generate mass matrices and compute mixing angles and mass splittings. We analyze the statistical distributions of $\sin^2\theta_{ij}$ and $\Delta m^2$ ratios, comparing them to experimental data and Haar-random expectations.

通过解析证明：由于代之间作为一维表示相互独立，所有左手二重态无荷的Abel离散Froggatt-Nielsen模型均产生Haar分布的随机酉矩阵（CKM与PMNS）。我们对$\mathbb{Z}_3$至$\mathbb{Z}_7$群进行数值扫描，每种选取12种不同荷分配，并使用$10^5$次蒙特卡洛采样生成质量矩阵，计算混合角和质量分裂。分析$\sin^2\theta_{ij}$与$\Delta m^2$比值的统计分布，并与实验数据及Haar随机预期比较。

Result: The seesaw-induced suppression of $\Delta m^2_{21}/\Delta m^2_{31}$ to $\sim 10^{-11}$ is found only in $\mathbb{Z}_3$ models and is avoidable for $N \geq 4$. However, the mixing angles in all abelian models are statistically indistinguishable from Haar-random unitaries: median values are $\sin^2\theta_{12} \approx \sin^2\theta_{23} \approx 0.50$, $\sin^2\theta_{13} \approx 0.31$, incompatible with the observed small CKM mixing. The probability of reproducing the observed CKM pattern from $O(1)$ coefficients is less than $2 \times 10^{-6}$. This universality arises because abelian groups admit only 1D representations, leading to 18 free parameters in Dirac mass matrices versus only 10 physical observables.

仅在$\mathbb{Z}_3$模型中发现seesaw机制导致$\Delta m^2_{21}/\Delta m^2_{31}$被压低至$\sim 10^{-11}$，而$N \geq 4$时可避免。然而所有Abel模型的混合角统计上无法与Haar随机酉矩阵区分：中位数为$\sin^2\theta_{12} \approx \sin^2\theta_{23} \approx 0.50$，$\sin^2\theta_{13} \approx 0.31$，与观测到的小CKM混合严重不符。由$O(1)$系数重现CKM模式的概率小于$2 \times 10^{-6}$。此普适性源于Abel群仅有1维表示，导致狄拉克质量矩阵有18个自由参数，远超10个物理可观测量。

Conclusion: The inability of abelian discrete flavor symmetries to generate realistic mixing patterns is a fundamental algebraic obstruction arising from their one-dimensional representations. While higher-order $\mathbb{Z}_N$ ($N \geq 4$) can resolve the mass hierarchy problem previously seen in $\mathbb{Z}_3$, they cannot fix the mixing angle problem. Predictive mixing structures require non-abelian flavor symmetries such as $A_4$, which reduce the number of free parameters via irreducible multi-dimensional representations. This conclusion applies specifically to models with uncharged left-handed fields; assigning charges to both chiralities may evade this issue.

Abel离散味对称性无法生成真实混合模式，其根本原因在于一维表示带来的代数障碍。尽管高阶$\mathbb{Z}_N$（$N \geq 4$）可解决此前$\mathbb{Z}_3$中的质量等级问题，但无法修复混合角问题。要获得可预测的混合结构，必须采用具有不可约高维表示的非Abel味对称性，如$A_4$。此结论仅适用于左手场无荷的模型；若对左右手场均赋荷，则可能规避该问题。

Abstract: Abelian flavor charges on right-handed fermions produce left-handed anarchy: we prove that all abelian discrete Froggatt-Nielsen models with uncharged left-handed doublets yield Haar-random PMNS and CKM matrices, regardless of $\mathbb{Z}_N$ group order, charge assignment, or Majorana mass structure. Scanning $\mathbb{Z}_3$ through $\mathbb{Z}_7$ with 12 charge assignments and $10^5$ Monte Carlo samples each, we demonstrate that the mass spectrum failure previously identified for $\mathbb{Z}_3$ -- the seesaw over-suppression mechanism that pushes $Δm^2_{21}/Δm^2_{31}$ to $\sim 10^{-11}$ -- is specific to $\mathbb{Z}_3$ and avoidable for $N \geq 4$. The mixing angle failure, however, is universal and irreducible. The PMNS angles from every abelian model are statistically consistent with Haar-random unitary matrices, with median $\sin^2θ_{12} \approx \sin^2θ_{23} \approx 0.50$ and $\sin^2θ_{13} \approx 0.31$ across all models tested. The same applies to the CKM: the joint probability of achieving CKM-like mixing from generic $O(1)$ coefficients is $< 2 \times 10^{-6}$. We identify the algebraic origin of this obstruction: abelian groups have only one-dimensional representations, so each generation transforms as an independent singlet with 18 free parameters for three Dirac mass matrices -- far exceeding the 10 physical observables. The transition to non-abelian flavor symmetries such as $A_4$, whose triplet representation reduces free parameters to 4 at leading order, is required specifically for mixing structure. This obstruction applies to the well-motivated subclass of models where left-handed fields are uncharged; models that assign abelian charges to both left- and right-handed fields can evade it.

</details>


### [79] [Production of $K^* Σ$ and $D^* Σ_c$ in pion-induced reactions off the nucleon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01074)
*Sang-Ho Kim*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study strangeness production in $\pi^- p \to K^{*0} \Sigma^0$ and $\pi^- p \to K^{*+} \Sigma^-$ within a hybrid Regge framework combining effective Lagrangians and Reggeized exchanges, identifying dominant nonresonant mechanisms and the key role of the $\Delta(2150)1/2^-$ resonance near threshold; we also predict highly suppressed charm-production cross sections for $\pi^- p \to D^{*-} \Sigma_c^+$ and $\pi^- p \to D^{*0} \Sigma_c^0$.

我们通过结合有效拉格朗日量与Regge化交换的混合Regge框架，研究了$\pi^- p \to K^{*0} \Sigma^0$和$\pi^- p \to K^{*+} \Sigma^-$反应中的奇异产生机制，识别出主导的非共振机制以及$\Delta(2150)1/2^-$共振态在阈值附近的主导作用；同时预测了$\pi^- p \to D^{*-} \Sigma_c^+$和$\pi^- p \to D^{*0} \Sigma_c^0$反应中显著压低的粲产生截面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the dynamics of strangeness production in hadronic reactions is essential for probing QCD in the nonperturbative regime. The near-threshold region is particularly sensitive to baryon resonances, yet their contributions remain poorly constrained. A unified description of both strangeness and charm production can test the universality of Regge mechanisms across different quark flavors.

理解强子反应中奇异产生的动力学对探测非微扰QCD至关重要。阈值附近区域对重子共振态贡献尤为敏感，但目前其贡献仍缺乏充分约束。统一描述奇异与粲产生过程可检验Regge机制在不同夸克味之间的普适性。

Method: A hybrid Regge model is employed, combining effective Lagrangian vertices with Reggeized propagators for $t$-channel $K$ and $K^*$ exchanges, $u$-channel $\Sigma$ and $\Lambda$ exchanges, and $s$-channel nucleon/$\Delta$ exchanges. $N^*$ and $\Delta^*$ resonances are included via relativistic Breit-Wigner amplitudes in the $s$ channel. Model parameters, including Regge trajectories and energy scales, are fixed using a QGSM-motivated prescription. Cross sections and spin-density matrix elements (SDMEs) are computed and compared to data.

采用混合Regge模型，结合有效拉格朗日顶点与Regge化传播子，包含$t$-道$K$和$K^*$交换、$u$-道$\Sigma$和$\Lambda$交换以及$s$-道核子/$\Delta$交换。通过相对论性Breit-Wigner振幅在$s$-道引入$N^*$和$\Delta^*$共振态。模型参数（包括Regge轨迹和能量尺度）由基于QGSM的方案固定。计算截面与自旋密度矩阵元（SDMEs）并与实验数据比较。

Result: The model successfully describes total and differential cross sections and SDMEs for both strangeness channels. The $\Delta(2150)1/2^-$ resonance dominates near threshold. Nonresonant contributions differ significantly between the two channels due to isospin structure. Predicted total cross sections for charm production are suppressed by $4$--$5$ orders ($\pi^- p \to D^{*-} \Sigma_c^+$) and $7$--$8$ orders ($\pi^- p \to D^{*0} \Sigma_c^0$) relative to strangeness counterparts.

该模型成功描述了两个奇异产生通道的总截面、微分截面及SDMEs。$\Delta(2150)1/2^-$共振态在阈值附近起主导作用。由于同位旋结构差异，非共振贡献在两通道间显著不同。预测的粲产生总截面相对于奇异对应过程被压低$4$--$5$个数量级（$\pi^- p \to D^{*-} \Sigma_c^+$）和$7$--$8$个数量级（$\pi^- p \to D^{*0} \Sigma_c^0$）。

Conclusion: The hybrid Regge framework provides a consistent description of strangeness production data, highlighting the importance of $s$-channel baryon resonances, especially $\Delta(2150)1/2^-$. Additional near-threshold measurements would help confirm resonance contributions. The strong suppression of charm production reflects the higher mass scale and smaller coupling constants, consistent with expectations from flavor symmetry breaking.

混合Regge框架为奇异产生数据提供了自洽描述，凸显了$s$-道重子共振态（特别是$\Delta(2150)1/2^-$）的重要性。更多阈值附近的测量将有助于确认共振态贡献。粲产生的强烈压低反映了更高的质量尺度与更小的耦合常数，符合味对称性破缺的预期。

Abstract: We investigate the mechanisms of strangeness production in the $π^- p \to K^{*0} Σ^0$ and $π^- p \to K^{*+} Σ^-$ reactions within a hybrid Regge framework in which effective Lagrangian vertices are combined with Reggeized exchanges. The nonresonant background consists of $t$-channel $K$- and $K^*$-Reggeon exchanges, $s$-channel nucleon and $Δ$ exchanges, and $u$-channel $Σ$- and $Λ$-Reggeon exchanges, whose roles differ markedly between the two isospin channels. We additionally include several $N^*$ and $Δ^*$ resonances in the $s$ channel and find that the $Δ(2150)1/2^-$ resonance provides the dominant near-threshold contribution. The resulting total and differential cross sections and spin-density matrix elements (SDMEs) are in good agreement with the available data. Additional measurements near threshold ($W \lesssim$ 2.5 GeV) would be valuable for clarifying the role of $s$-channel baryon resonances. Within the same framework, with Regge trajectories and energy-scale parameters fixed by a QGSM-motivated prescription, we also predict the cross sections for the charm-production reactions $π^- p \to D^{*-} Σ_c^+$ and $π^- p \to D^{*0} Σ_c^0$. Their total cross sections are suppressed by approximately $4$--$5$ and $7$--$8$ orders of magnitude, respectively, compared with those of the corresponding strangeness-production reactions. These results may serve as useful guidance for future experiments at facilities such as J-PARC.

### [80] [Uncover the correlation between jet energy correlators and multiplicity fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01102)
*Pi Duan,Weiyao Ke,Guang-You Qin,Lei Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We introduce the multiplicity-conditioned EEC jet function (MCJF) and compute it to next-to-leading order, revealing that the energy-energy correlator (EEC) in jets exhibits a dependence on normalized jet multiplicity $\nu$, with a $\nu$-dependent anomalous dimension emerging in the perturbative regime. This provides a direct probe of the multiplicity generating function and helps control multiplicity-related biases in nuclear measurements.

我们引入了多重性条件下的EEC喷注函数（MCJF），并在下一阶领头阶精度下进行了计算，发现喷注中的能量-能量关联器（EEC）在归一化多重性$\nu$上存在依赖性，且在微扰区域呈现出$\nu$相关的反常维度。这为多重性生成函数提供了直接探针，并有助于抑制核环境中EEC测量的多重性偏倚效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The energy-energy correlator (EEC) and jet multiplicity are key probes of QCD dynamics, but their interplay is not well understood. While EEC captures angular energy flow, multiplicity reflects the full particle production history. Studying how EEC varies with jet multiplicity allows access to new aspects of jet substructure and potential biases in heavy-ion collisions where jet quenching and medium response may correlate with multiplicity.

能量-能量关联器（EEC）和喷注多重性是研究QCD动力学的关键观测量，但二者之间的关联尚不清楚。EEC刻画角向能量流，而多重性反映粒子产生全过程。研究EEC如何随喷注重重性变化，可揭示喷注子结构的新特征，并有助于理解重离子碰撞中因喷注淬火与介质响应可能带来的多重性相关偏倚。

Method: We define the multiplicity-conditioned EEC jet function (MCJF), which conditions the EEC on a fixed normalized multiplicity $\nu = N_{\rm ch}/\langle N_{\rm ch} \rangle$. Using SCET (Soft-Collinear Effective Theory), we perform a factorization analysis of the MCJF to next-to-leading order (NLO), isolating hard, collinear, and soft contributions. The $\nu$-dependence enters through the multiplicity generating function, leading to a $\nu$-dependent anomalous dimension in the renormalization group evolution.

我们定义了多重性条件下的EEC喷注函数（MCJF），将EEC限定在固定的归一化多重性$\nu = N_{\rm ch}/\langle N_{\rm ch} \rangle$上。利用SCET（软-共线有效理论），我们对MCJF进行了因子化分析并达到下一阶领头阶（NLO）精度，分离出硬、共线和软贡献。$\nu$依赖性通过多重性生成函数引入，导致在重整化群演化中出现$\nu$相关的反常维度。

Result: The EEC in the angular range $\Lambda_{\rm QCD}/p_{T,\rm jet}\ll\chi\ll R$ acquires a $\nu$-dependent anomalous dimension, scaling as $\gamma_\nu \sim \nu \cdot \gamma_0$, indicating that the running of the EEC is modulated by jet multiplicity. This establishes the $\nu$-conditioned EEC as a direct probe of the multiplicity generating function in perturbative QCD. Additionally, this effect must be accounted for when interpreting EEC measurements in nuclear environments to avoid misattributing multiplicity-induced effects to medium modifications.

在角区$\Lambda_{\rm QCD}/p_{T,\rm jet}\ll\chi\ll R$内，EEC获得一个$\nu$相关的反常维度，标度形式为$\gamma_\nu \sim \nu \cdot \gamma_0$，表明EEC的跑动受喷注重重性调制。这使得$\nu$-条件化的EEC成为微扰QCD中多重性生成函数的直接探针。此外，在核环境中解释EEC测量时必须考虑此效应，以避免将多重性诱导效应误认为介质修正。

Conclusion: The multiplicity-conditioned EEC jet function (MCJF) reveals a novel correlation between jet energy flow and internal multiplicity, governed by a $\nu$-dependent anomalous dimension. This provides new theoretical insight into jet substructure and offers an experimental handle to probe the multiplicity generating function. It also highlights the importance of controlling multiplicity-dependent selection biases, especially in heavy-ion collision experiments.

多重性条件下的EEC喷注函数（MCJF）揭示了喷注能量流与内部多重性之间由$\nu$相关反常维度支配的新关联。这为喷注子结构提供了新的理论视角，并为实验探测多重性生成函数提供了可行手段，同时强调了控制多重性相关选择偏倚的重要性，尤其在重离子碰撞实验中。

Abstract: The energy-energy correlator (EEC) and multiplicity are two fundamental observables probing complementary aspects of QCD jets: the former characterizes the angular structure of energy flows in a scale-dependent manner, while the latter is sensitive to the entire history of particle production. In this \emph{Letter}, we uncover a nontrivial correlation between them by studying the EEC as a function of jet internal multiplicity. We introduce the multiplicity-conditioned EEC jet function (MCJF) and perform a factorization calculation to next-to-leading order accuracy. It is found that, for jet samples selected at a given normalized multiplicity $ν= N_{\rm ch}/\langle N_{\rm ch} \rangle$, the EEC in the angular region $Λ_{\rm QCD}/p_{T,\rm jet}\llχ\ll R$ acquires a $ν$-dependent anomalous dimension. Thus the $ν$-conditioned EEC provides a direct and robust probe to the multiplicity generating function in the perturbative regime. In addition, understanding $ν$ dependence of the EEC is also crucial for isolating possible multiplicity-dependent bias effects in the EEC measurements in nuclear environment.

### [81] [Integrating out a heavy Higgs singlet: on the edge between SMEFT and HEFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01125)
*Stefan Dittmaier,Sebastian Schuhmacher,Maximilian Stahlhofen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We integrate out the heavy Higgs $H$ in a singlet-extended Standard Model at one loop using the background-field method and expansion by regions, obtaining an effective Lagrangian to $\mathcal{O}(1/M_H^2)$. The result depends on how SM parameters scale with $M_H$, determining whether the EFT belongs to SMEFT or the more general HEFT. We show that with a phenomenologically motivated scaling—where the mixing angle $\alpha \sim \mathcal{O}(M_h/M_H)$—the resulting EFT contains non-SMEFT operators, making bottom-up matching with pure SMEFT insufficient. The decoupling is verified via agreement between full theory and EFT predictions for electroweak observables beyond $\mathcal{O}(1/M_H^2)$.

我们使用基于背景场方法和区域展开的函数方法，在单态扩展标准模型中于单圈水平上积出重希格斯场$H$，得到在大希格斯质量极限下至$\mathcal{O}(1/M_H^2)$的有效拉格朗日量。结果依赖于标准模型参数在$M_H$很大时的标度行为，这决定了有效场论属于SMEFT还是更一般的HEFT框架。我们采用一种现象学上合理的标度假设——混合角$\alpha \sim \mathcal{O}(M_h/M_H)$，表明此时无法仅用SMEFT算符进行自下而上的匹配，必须引入非SMEFT算符。通过检验多个电弱精度观测量在大$M_H$极限下的行为，验证了全理论与有效理论预测之间的差异衰减快于$1/M_H^2$，满足解耦定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Integrating out heavy new physics in a consistent quantum field theoretic framework is essential for connecting ultraviolet (UV) models to low-energy observables. In Higgs sector extensions like the singlet extension of the SM, the question arises whether the resulting low-energy EFT can be described within the Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT), which assumes linear realization of electroweak symmetry, or if it requires the more general Higgs Effective Field Theory (HEFT) with a nonlinear realization. This distinction hinges on the scaling behavior of model parameters (especially the Higgs mixing angle $\alpha$) in the decoupling limit $M_H \gg M_h$. The paper aims to clarify this issue in a one-loop calculation, going beyond tree-level analyses, and to assess the validity of bottom-up matching procedures using only SMEFT operators.

在新物理能标较高时，以一致的量子场论方法积出重场对连接紫外模型与低能可观测量至关重要。在如SM单态扩展等希格斯扇区扩展中，一个关键问题是：所得低能有效场论是否可纳入标准模型有效场论（SMEFT，假设电弱对称性线性实现），或必须采用更一般的希格斯有效场论（HEFT，对应非线性实现）。这一区分取决于模型参数（特别是希格斯混合角$\alpha$）在$M_H \gg M_h$解耦极限下的标度行为。本文旨在通过单圈计算（超越树图近似）澄清此问题，并评估仅使用SMEFT算符的自下而上匹配程序的有效性。

Method: We employ the background-field formalism combined with the expansion by regions to perform a functional computation of the one-loop effective action after integrating out the heavy Higgs field $H$. This approach ensures gauge invariance and consistency in the treatment of quantum corrections. The matching between the full theory and the EFT is carried out by expanding Green's functions in powers of $1/M_H$, keeping terms up to $\mathcal{O}(1/M_H^2)$. Renormalization of both the full and effective theories is consistently handled, including operator mixing and counterterms. We analyze two scenarios: one where parameters scale such that the EFT fits into SMEFT, and another with more general scaling leading to HEFT-type operators. The validity of the EFT is tested by comparing predictions for electroweak precision observables (e.g., $S$, $T$ parameters, Higgs couplings) in the full theory and the EFT in the large-$M_H$ limit.

我们采用背景场方法结合区域展开技术，通过对重希格斯场$H$积分后计算单圈有效作用量，实现功能性的EFT匹配。该方法保证了规范不变性和量子修正处理的一致性。通过将格林函数按$1/M_H$展开并保留至$\mathcal{O}(1/M_H^2)$项完成全理论与有效理论的匹配。对全理论和有效理论均进行了协变重整化处理，包括算符混合和抵消项。我们分析了两种情形：一种是参数标度使EFT可嵌入SMEFT；另一种是一般性更强的标度导致出现HEFT型算符。通过比较全理论与EFT在大$M_H$极限下对电弱精度观测量（如$S$、$T$参数，希格斯耦合）的预测来检验EFT的有效性。

Result: The resulting effective Lagrangian at $\mathcal{O}(1/M_H^2)$ contains bosonic EFT operators that cannot be written in the standard SILH basis of SMEFT when the Higgs mixing angle scales as $\alpha \sim \mathcal{O}(M_h/M_H)$. Specifically, operators involving higher derivatives of the Higgs doublet appear, which are characteristic of HEFT. We explicitly demonstrate that any attempt to match the full theory to SMEFT using only bosonic operators fails at one loop. Furthermore, we verify that the difference between full-theory and EFT predictions for electroweak observables vanishes faster than $1/M_H^2$, confirming the correctness of the EFT construction. Both theories asymptotically reproduce SM predictions as $M_H \to \infty$, satisfying the decoupling theorem.

在希格斯混合角标度为$\alpha \sim \mathcal{O}(M_h/M_H)$的情形下，所得至$\mathcal{O}(1/M_H^2)$的有效拉格朗日量包含无法写成标准SILH形式的玻色子算符，特别是涉及希格斯二重态高阶导数的项，这是HEFT的典型特征。我们明确证明，任何试图仅用玻色子SMEFT算符在单圈水平上完成匹配的做法都会失败。此外，我们验证了全理论与EFT对电弱观测量的预测差异衰减快于$1/M_H^2$，证实了EFT构造的正确性。当$M_H \to \infty$时，两者均渐近趋于标准模型预测，满足解耦定理。

Conclusion: The integration of the heavy Higgs in the singlet-extended SM at one loop leads to an effective description beyond SMEFT when the mixing angle $\alpha$ scales as $\mathcal{O}(M_h/M_H)$, necessitating the use of HEFT. This shows that SMEFT does not universally capture all decoupling new physics scenarios, even at one loop. The failure of bottom-up matching with SMEFT highlights the importance of UV-sensitive assumptions in EFT constructions. Our results emphasize the need for a careful analysis of parameter scaling in the decoupling limit and support the use of functional methods for rigorous EFT matching beyond tree level.

在单态扩展SM中，当混合角$\alpha$按$\mathcal{O}(M_h/M_H)$标度时，重希格斯场的单圈积分导致超出SMEFT的有效描述，必须采用HEFT框架。这表明即使在单圈水平，SMEFT也无法普适地涵盖所有解耦型新物理情景。自下而上使用SMEFT匹配的失败凸显了EFT构造中对紫外敏感假设的重要性。我们的结果强调了在解耦极限下仔细分析参数标度的必要性，并支持使用函数方法进行超越树图水平的严格EFT匹配。

Abstract: We use a functional approach based on the background-field formalism and the expansion by regions to integrate out the heavy Higgs field (associated with the mass eigenstate H) in a singlet extension of the Standard Model (SM) at the one-loop level. In this way, we obtain an effective Lagrangian to $\mathcal{O}(1/M_H^2)$ in the limit of large Higgs mass ($M_H \gg M_h\approx125$GeV) providing a consistent treatment of effects from Higgs mixing and the renormalization of the underlying model. In particular, we address how the choice of the scaling behaviour of the model parameters in the large-$M_H$ limit determines whether the effective Lagrangian can be accommodated in the SM Effective Field Theory (SMEFT) or involves non-SMEFT operators within the more general Higgs Effective Field Theory (HEFT) framework. For our calculation, we choose a limit that ensures decoupling of beyond-SM effects at $\mathcal{O}(1/M_H^0)$ by demanding that the Higgs mixing angle $α$ is of $\mathcal{O}(M_h/M_H)$ and putting minimal constraints on the other input parameters, which represents a phenomenologically viable scenario. The considered model is restricted to massless fermions, and the emerging Effective Field Theory (EFT) involves only bosonic EFT operators in addition to the SM Lagrangian. We explicitly show that any attempt of a bottom-up (diagrammatic) matching with only bosonic SMEFT operators at $\mathcal{O}(1/M_H^2)$ necessarily fails. We validate our results for the effective Lagrangian at next-to-leading order in the coupling expansion by verifying that the difference between EFT and full-theory predictions vanishes faster than $1/M_H^2$ for several electroweak precision observables in the large-$M_H$ limit. Moreover, both full-theory and EFT predictions asymptotically approach the corresponding SM results for very large values of $M_H$ as required by decoupling.

### [82] [$Λ_c N$ correlation functions with leading-order covariant chiral interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01154)
*Ru-You Zheng,Zhi-Wei Liu,Li-Sheng Geng*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The $\Lambda_c p$ momentum correlation functions are studied using covariant chiral effective field theory, revealing a weakly attractive interaction in the ${}^1S_0$ channel and a repulsive effect in the ${}^3S_1$ channel when $S$--$D$ mixing is included; the spin-averaged correlation function becomes repulsive due to triplet dominance, with clear implications for femtoscopic measurements.

使用协变手征有效场论研究了 $\Lambda_c p$ 动量关联函数，在 ${}^1S_0$ 通道中发现相互作用呈弱吸引性，而在包含 $S$--$D$ 混合时 ${}^3S_1$ 通道表现出排斥作用；由于三重态占主导，自旋平均关联函数呈现排斥行为，这对原子核散射测量具有明确意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the nature of the $\Lambda_c N$ interaction through femtoscopic correlation functions, particularly distinguishing between different theoretical models (covariant vs. non-relativistic chiral EFT and phenomenological models) and assessing the role of relativistic effects and coupled-channel dynamics such as $S$--$D$ mixing.

通过原子核散射关联函数理解 $\Lambda_c N$ 相互作用的本质，特别是区分不同理论模型（协变与非相对论手征EFT及唯象模型），并评估相对论效应和耦合道动力学（如 $S$--$D$ 混合）的作用。

Method: The $\Lambda_c p$ correlation functions are computed using $\Lambda_c N$ interactions derived from covariant chiral effective field theory, including up to next-to-leading order, with full treatment of $S$--$D$ wave mixing in the ${}^3S_1$--${}^3D_1$ coupled channels. The spin-singlet and triplet contributions are separately analyzed, and the resulting correlation functions are studied as a function of source size. A comparative analysis is performed with results from non-relativistic chiral EFT and phenomenological potentials.

使用协变手征有效场论导出的 $\Lambda_c N$ 相互作用计算 $\Lambda_c p$ 关联函数，包含至次领头阶，并在 ${}^3S_1$--${}^3D_1$ 耦合道中完整处理 $S$--$D$ 波混合。分别分析单态和三重态贡献，并研究关联函数随源尺寸的变化。与非相对论手征EFT和唯象势的结果进行了比较分析。

Result: The ${}^1S_0$ channel yields a weakly attractive $\Lambda_c p$ interaction, while the ${}^3S_1$ channel shows strong sensitivity to $S$--$D$ mixing: without it, the interaction is weakly attractive, but with it, the interaction becomes repulsive. Consequently, the spin-averaged correlation function — dominated by the triplet component — exhibits repulsive behavior when $S$--$D$ mixing is included. Variations with source size are significant enough to be resolved in current femtoscopic experiments. Systematic differences are found when comparing with non-relativistic chiral EFT and phenomenological models.

${}^1S_0$ 通道产生弱吸引性的 $\Lambda_c p$ 相互作用，而 ${}^3S_1$ 通道对 $S$--$D$ 混合极为敏感：无混合时为弱吸引，有混合时则变为排斥。因此，当包含 $S$--$D$ 混合时，由三重态主导的自旋平均关联函数呈现排斥行为。源尺寸变化的影响足够显著，可在当前原子核散射实验中分辨。与非相对论手征EFT和唯象模型的比较显示出系统性差异。

Conclusion: Femtoscopy is a powerful tool to probe the $\Lambda_c N$ interaction, especially sensitive to dynamical details such as $S$--$D$ mixing and relativistic effects. The repulsive nature of the spin-averaged $\Lambda_c p$ correlation function in the presence of $S$--$D$ mixing highlights the importance of coupled-channel effects. Discrepancies among different theoretical approaches suggest that upcoming high-precision experimental data can discriminate between them, providing crucial constraints for charmed baryon-nucleon interactions.

原子核散射是探测 $\Lambda_c N$ 相互作用的有力工具，尤其对 $S$--$D$ 混合和相对论效应等动力学细节敏感。在存在 $S$--$D$ 混合时，自旋平均 $\Lambda_c p$ 关联函数的排斥性质突显了耦合道效应的重要性。不同理论方法之间的差异表明，即将到来的高精度实验数据可用来区分这些模型，为含粲重子-核子相互作用提供关键约束。

Abstract: The $Λ_c p$ momentum correlation functions are investigated using $Λ_c N$ interactions derived within the covariant chiral effective field theory. Our analysis reveals that the interaction is weakly attractive in the spin-singlet ${}^1S_0$ channel. In contrast, the ${}^3S_1$ channel exhibits a pronounced sensitivity to coupled-channel effects, i.e., the inclusion of $S$--$D$ mixing results in a repulsive $Λ_c p$ interaction; its absence leads to a weakly attractive one. Consequently, the spin-averaged correlation function -- dominated by the triplet state weight -- exhibits repulsive behavior when the $S$-- $D$ mixing is present. Furthermore, the source size dependence of the correlation functions is examined, demonstrating that the resulting variations remain experimentally resolvable within the precision of current femtoscopic measurements. A systematic comparison with non-relativistic chiral effective field theory and phenomenological models yields distinct discrepancies in the femtoscopic correlation functions. These findings underscore the capacity of femtoscopy to discriminate between different theoretical descriptions of the $Λ_c N$ interaction and provide useful references for upcoming experimental data.

</details>
